1a1(dkar chag): ma rgya chamasam
1b1(dkar chag): swasti prA dza b+h+yaHtshogs gnyis chu gter
1b2(dkar chag): 'khyil dbus gzugs kyi sku// mtshan dpe'i
2a1(dkar chag): dpal 'bar gser gyi lhun po ni// nyi gzhon byugs ltar srid gsum lha nge ba// 'dren mchog
2a2(dkar chag): shAkya'i tog de spyi bos mchod// gang gi dpal gyi mgur nas tshangs dbyangs kyis// legs gsung brgyad khri bzhi
2a3(dkar chag): stong chos kyi ro// myangs pas 'chi med bdud rtsi'i dpal ster ba'i// bdon gnyis zung 'jug dam pa'i chos la 'dud//
2b1(dkar chag): rig dang grol ba'i yon tan gyis mdzes pa'i// rgyal ba'i myu gu byang sems tshogs rnams dang // rang rgyal nyan thos zhugs gnas brgyad
2b2(dkar chag): bcas sogs// theg gsum 'phags tshogs rgya mtshog tsug gos mchod// 'dzam bus mtshon pa'i gling 'dir thub pa'i bstan// mi
2b3(dkar chag): nub nyin mor byed pa'i dad la 'dzin pa// mi pham 'jam dbyangs gsang bdag 'od srungs sogs// theg gnyis bka' bsdu mdzad rnams
2b4(dkar chag): 'dud bya'i gnas// ji snyed shes bya'i gnas la sgro skur gyi// log smra'i gnyis 'thung klad 'gems lung rig gi/ mche ba mi bzang sbar mo'i
3a1(dkar chag): shugs 'chang ba'i// rgyan drug mchog gnyis smra ba'i seng ger 'dud// rim gnyis ting 'dzin rdo rje'i lcags kyu yis// log pa'i lam du 'phyan pa'i dregs bsnyems kun// bkug nas yang dag lam
3a2(dkar chag): du 'dzud grub pa'i dbang // 'khor los bsgyur ba brgyad cu'i tshogs la 'dud// brjod bya don ldan dam pa'i chos dang 'brel// nyon mongs spong zhing zhi ba'i phan yon ston// thub pa chen po'i spobs pa zhi ldan gyi// sde snod gsum
3a3(dkar chag): gyi bka' yis pad+mo'i tshal// rgya che bsdu du dang rgyus 'brel 'khrugs bsdebs shing // zab mo'i gnas rnams 'chos dang skyob pa yi// yon tan gnyis ldan bstun btsas nyin byed gyis// phyed nas 'gro la snang mdzad rnams
3a4(dkar chag): la 'dud// 'phags yul yon tan rgya mtsho'i gling mchog nas// gangs can brda' yi gzings kyi 'khrul 'khor la// brten nos bka' bstan yid bzhin nor bu'i tshogs// drangs mdzad 'jig rten mig rnams phyag bgyid
3a5(dkar chag): 'os// bsil ldan rabs yongs bskor gangs can 'dir// rgyal ba'i myu gu lha rigs sa chen 'di// dge bcu'i khrims kyis skyong zhing rgyal ba'i bstan// rgyas mdzad bod kyi chos rgyal rnams la 'dud// ljongasau 'di ri na'ang
3a6(dkar chag): phyi ma'i dus dag tu// mkhan slob chos gsum sogs kyis rgyal ba yi// yang dag bstan pa'i nyi 'od brdal ba la// log rtog tshwa 'dzin stug pos sgrib byed pa'o// hA shwang la sogs log smra'i dpung tshegs kun// legs
3b1(dkar chag): bshad lung rigs 'thor rlung drag po yis// pa mthar bskrad nas yang dag rgyal ba'i bstan// gsal mdzad slob dpon kA ma shI lA dang // lnga brgya'i gtsug rgyan a ti shA la stsogs// nges par bka' drin can rnams
3b2(dkar chag): phyag gi yul// rgyal bas gdul byar rnam par thar pa'i sgo// sna tshogs gsungs bzhin rang rang grub pa'i mtha'// rgyal ba'i dgongs bzhin ma nor 'dzin mkhas pa'i// ris med bod kyi bstan 'dzin rnams la
3b3(dkar chag): 'dud// khyad par thub bstan mdo sngags gnad kyi don// ji bzhin ma gtogs gcig zhen gcil dor nas// gang zag gcig gi lam gyi rim pa ru// mi 'char 'gal 'dus phyogs rer zhen pa yis// thub
3b4(dkar chag): bsten ming tsom lhag mar gyur pa'i dus// ston che shwAka thub dbang po'i tog sogs kyi// spyan sngar zhal bzhes bzhin du 'jam dpal dbyangs// ngur smrig zol la nyer brten rgyal ba yi// mdo sngags thub bstan
3b5(dkar chag): mya lus dgongs pa'i don// gang zag gcig gi lam gyi rimA pa ru// mi 'gal gcig glo gos gcig tu 'gro ba'i tshul// bsregs btsod brdar ba'i gser bzhin lung rig gi/ skya bar nas ston yang dag lam pa za/
3b6(dkar chag): bo// slar yang thar 'dod rnams kyi 'jug ngogs su// nges par sbyin mdzad mkhas dang grub pa'i rje// yongs kyi 'khor los bsgyur ba btsong kha ba// thams cad mkhyen nges de la de bzhin du// shes nas sgo gsum shugs
4a1(dkar chag): dral gus pas 'dud// bstan pa mchog de bshad dang sgrub pa yis// 'dzin mdzad 'jam dbyangs gtsang ba bdun bsgyud dang // snang mtha' spyan ras gzigs sprul yab sras sogs// gser
4a2(dkar chag): mdog cod pan 'dzin rnams gus pas 'dud// rgyal ba na mkha'i nor bu ma lus bas// gsal bar ma mdzad bdag sogs pad+mo'i tshal// thub po bstan kun+da'i tshal dang lhan cig tu// gsal mdzad bdag gi bshes gnyen
4a3(dkar chag): rnams la 'dud// yang dag don la zhi khro mi mnga' yang // khro chags zhi sogs zlos gar sna tshogs kyis// bstan dang bstan 'dzin skyong mdzad srung ma'i tshogs// 'phrin las sgrub las nam yang ma g.yel zhig/ de ltar bsod
4a4(dkar chag): nams zhing gi mchog rnams la// dngos po kun gyis 'dud pa'i phyag byas nas// ljongs 'dir srid dang zhi ba'i rgyan gcig gi/ thub bstan dgongs 'grel 'gyuraro cog bzhengs pa'i// dkar chag rin chen mdzes pa'i phra tshoms phreng //
4a5(dkar chag): sdebs legs tshig gi srad bur bsgru bar byas// gang sngon brjo du med po'i bskal pa nas// 'gyur med chos dbyings spros pa bral brnyes kyang // 'gro ba'i don phyir slob dang mi slob pa'i// nam mkha' ji srid rnam rol cir yang 'char// 'on
4a6(dkar chag): rang dus gsum rgyal po ma lus thob// gaushegs bzhugs bltams sogs 'gro la sman pa'i slad// rnam par ral pa sna tshogs mdzad na yang // srid mtshor bying nas nyes brgya bskyed pa'i gzhi// sgrib gnyis nags tshal tshang tshing
4b1(dkar chag): gcod pa'i mtshon// thub gsung dgongs 'grel bcas las gzhan du ci// des na mdzad pa kun las gsung gi ni// mdzad pa mchog ces dam pa rnams kyis bsngags// de phyir bskal bzang 'dren pa stong gi dbus// smad byung snying
4b2(dkar chag): stobs mchog gyur zas gtsang sras// gang gis gdul bya'i khams dang bsam pa dang // bag la nyal sogs dbang po dang mthun par// yan lag drug cu tshangs pa'i dbyangs snyan pos// dug gsum re r-i shas cher spyod pa dang //
4b3(dkar chag): de gsum cha mnyams spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa// brgya khri bzhi stong dag gis gnyen por ni// chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong gsungs// grangs med gdul bya'i khams dang bsam pa bzhin// rgyal bas chos tshul ji snyed bka' stsol kyang //
4b4(dkar chag): gdul bya'i nyams len rim pa nyid las ni// lung dang rtogs pa'i bstan pa gnyisu 'du// lung gis sgrub pa byed lugs gtan la 'bebs// rtogs paso gtan la phab ltar sgrub pa'o// lung la bka' dang dgongs 'grel gnyis su
4b5(dkar chag): ts+tsha du 'i 'dus bya nga // 9 ste ngas sbyi / sa hU~M sa sa ga sa na na b+h+re ts+tsha
4b6(dkar chag): thabs kyi bsti gnas rnams mang rgyal bas bkod// theg pa chen po 'bras bu'i gnas skabs kyi// sku dang zhing khams 'khor dang ma dzad po ni// yongs su dag pa'i rnam pa lam nyid du// byed dang mi byed sngags dang pha rol phyin//
5a1(dkar chag): de ltar sde snod gsum dang rgyud sde bzhis// legs bsdus drang nges sna tshogs rgyal ba'i bka'// 'dren pa mchog gis legs gsungs ji bzhin du// kun dga' nye 'khor 'od srungs chen
5a2(dkar chag): bo sogs// thun mong mdo sde 'dul mngon sde snod bsdus// 'jam dbyangs byams pa kun tu bzang po dang // khyad par thub pa chen po'i gsar ba'i mdzod// ma lus 'dzin la phyag ni rdo rje sogs// rgyal sras bdag nyid
5a3(dkar chag): chen po 'bum phrag bcus// rgyu dang 'bras bu'i theg chen sde snod bsdus// rgyal bas lung bstan 'od srungs chen po sogs// dgra bcom rnams kyis mi nub gsal bar mdzod// khyad par theg mchog bstan pa'i
5a4(dkar chag): snying po ni// 'dzin par lung bstan klu sgrub thogs med ces// nyi zla ltar brag shing rta che gnyis dang // 'phags pa lha dang dpa' bo sangs rgyas sbyangs// legs ldan 'byed dang zla ba grags pa'i zhabs// dbyig
5a5(dkar chag): gnyen zhabs dang blo brtan phyogs glang dang // phan chen yon tan 'od dang shAk+She 'od // chos kyi grags pa'i zhabs sogs 'dzam gling gi/ rgyan mchog rnams dang tsan+d+ra gaM mau drang // ye shes snying po dpal sbas zhi ba
5a6(dkar chag): mtsho// pad+ma'i ngang tshul seng ge bzang po dang // lha dbang blo dang shAkya blo dza mA ri// dul lha chos mchog grol sde rnam gnyis dang / chos kyi po shes gnyen sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs// zhi ba lha dang mar me mdzad
5b1(dkar chag): kyi zhabs// in+ta b+hU tI mda' bsnun sha ba ri// lu li dril bu nag po spyod pa'i zhabs// la ba pa dang bi b+hu ti tsan+ta/ bIR+YA Dom+b+hi lA li ta badz+ra// to lo nA ro mai tri dpal 'dzin dang // pad+ma badz+ra rat+na rak+Shi ta// don yod rdo/
5b2(dkar chag): rje shAkya ba shes glonyen dang // kun dga' snying po sangs rgyas gas ngo ba'i zhabs// byang chub mchog dong grub mchog r-i shin+ni pa// oM b+hU ka ra smai ti ngagra dbang grags// dri pa ma kI ru shrIHdz+nyA na sogs// rgyal
5b3(dkar chag): bas lung bstan shing rta che rnams dang / mkhas dang grub pa'i paN grub bgrang yas kyis// rgyal ba'i bka' yi dgongs pa'i gnas ji bzhin// drang nges legs par phye nas dgongs 'grel ba'i// chos
5b4(dkar chag): skyobs yon tan+da gnyis ldan bstan bcos ni// dpag med brtsom dang 'chad cing rtsod pa yis// gdul bya rnams kyi blo mig pad+mo'i tshe lnga// slar yang phye nas rab tu gsol bar mdzad// de lte'i dgongs 'brel
5b5(dkar chag): bo stana? bcos dbye ba ni// dron dang ldan zhing bsngal spong ba dang / sgrub pa lhur byed bstan bcos gsum du gsungs// de gsum ston byed rlig pa'i gnas lnga ste// gtan tshigs rig dang sgra dang gso ba dang //
5b6(dkar chag): bzo rigs pa dang nang gi don rig lnga// nang rig la'ang mdo rgyud dgongs 'brel gnyis// dang po la'ang 'khor lo rim pa gsum// so so'i lta ba dang ni spyod pa dang // de gnyis cha mnyam ston pa'i bstan bcos//
6a1(dkar chag): sngags la'ang rgyud sde bzhi pa so so dang // spyi yi dgongs 'grel bstan bcos bsam mi khyab// gzhan yang thor bu lugs kyi bstan bcos sogs// rnam g.yeng med pa'i yid can rtsom pa
6a2(dkar chag): pos// thur pa thob pa'i lam dang rjes 'bral mthun zhing dang // rgyal ba'i dgongs pa phyin ci ma log par// bkral po'i bstan bcos 'dzumasu klas pa rnams// 'phags yul kha che sing+ga la yi gling // oM rgyan za
6a3(dkar chag): hor gser gling sham+b+ha lA// lang+ga'i gling dang zangs glang bal po sogs// thub bstan ngar ba'i yul dang yul gru ni// sna tshogs 'gro ba'i bsod nams zhing du bzhugs// de nA thub bstan lnga brgya phrag bcu ru// gnas par
6a4(dkar chag): gsungs las 'bras bu'i le'u gsum// 'das shing sgrub pa'i le'u'i dus skabasu// rgyal po nyid kyis lha mi dri med 'ong // lung bstan myodo las nga ni mya dran las// 'dres nas bgrang bye nyis stong lnga brgya nA// gdong
6a5(dkar chag): dmar can gyi yul du dam pa'i chos// dar bar 'gyur zhes gsung ltar rgyal ba yi// 'phrin las 'jug pa dus las mi yol bas// bod yul mun po'i smag rum 'thibs pa 'dir// dam chos sgron mes snang bar
6a6(dkar chag): bya ba'i phyir// rigs gsum rgyu dra'i gar mkhan chos kyi rgyal// gnam ri ba tsan sogs gnam gyi khri bdun dang // stod kyi steng gnyis bar du legs pa drug/ sa la lde brgyad 'og gi btsan gsum sogs// gdung
6b1(dkar chag): rabs nyer dru ga brgyud mthar kun bzang gi sprul pa lha tho tho ri snyan shal ring // dam pa'i chos kyi dbu mchog rab tu brnyes// de nas rgyal rabs lnga nas 'phags pa'i mchog/ spyan ras gzigs sprul srong ba can
6b2(dkar chag): skam po yis// sprul pa'i bkod pa sna tshogs rab bkye nas// gtsug lag khang bzhengs rang byen rnam gnyis dang // rdo shAka gnyis sogs bsod nams zhing du drangs// 'jig rten ma gcig thon mes swam+b+ho
6b3(dkar chag): Tis// yi ge'i srol gtod dam chos ming bsgyur nas// bar du dam pa'i chos kyi srol bzang gtong // de nas gdung rabs ldan 'jam dbyangs kyi// sprul pa chos rgyal khri srong lde btson gyis// mkhan slob gnyi
6b4(dkar chag): dang pi mA mi tra dang // shin+ta gar+b+ha pad+ma'i ngang chus+t+r-i la sogs// spyan drangs gtsug lag khang dang rten bzhengs shing // sang mi mi bdun sogasau kyang rab tu byung // be ro tsA na ka tso go zheng sogs kyis// theg pa che chung dam
6b5(dkar chag): chos myang bsgyur nas// 'chad dang nyan pa'i sgo nas dar rgyas mdzod// gzhan yang phyag rdor sprul pa khri ralA sogs// snga drar dus dang phyi drar dus rnams su// rim par byon pa'i sras bcas rgyal ba yi// sprul
6b6(dkar chag): pa'i zlos gar rgyal blon byang chub sems// gang gi thugs rje'i byed po la brten nas// 'jig rten mig gcig bka' dran can rnam sau kris// dka' ba du mas 'phags pa'i yul bgrod nas// mkhas shing
7a1(dkar chag): grub pa'i phan grub mtha' yas dang // rgyal ba'i bka' yi dgongs 'brel dpag med pa// phyogs 'di'i bsod nams zhing du legs par drangs// de ltar bsgyur ba'i dgongs
7a2(dkar chag): 'brel bstan bcos grang // bsgyur ro cog rnams mkhas pa rnams kyis ni// phyogs gcig bsdus shing glegs pom la bkod nas// dkar chag mdzad la bstan 'gyur zhesu gra gas// 'di ni skye
7a3(dkar chag): dgu kun gyi rang rgyud kyi// nyon mo ljongs dag rnams bsla pa gsum gis 'chos shing // ngan 'go sad pa'i 'jigs las slob pas na// phan bde ma lus 'byung ba'i sa gzhi dang / sdug bsngal mun pa
7a4(dkar chag): sel ba'i sgron me dang // sgrib gnyis ma lus 'khrud pa'i bdud rtsi 'ang yin// des na dri bral rgyal ba'i bka' bzhin du// 'bri dang klog dang 'dzin dang 'chang ba dang // khA 'dron bgyid dang bkur sti bgyid
7a5(dkar chag): rnams kyi// bsod nams phung po gzugasu grub gyur na// namakha'i khyon kun gang yang ga la shong // gzhan yang phan bde'i 'byung gnas rgyal ba'i bstan// 'gro ba'i bsod nams zhing du gnas pa yang /
7a6(dkar chag): dgongs 'brel 'di rnams 'bri dang 'chad sogs la// rag lus des na rab rtsal gyis zhus mdor// chos rnams thams cad bka' dang bstan bcos gnyisu 'du// legs par gsungs dang de yi dgongs
7b1(dkar chag): 'grel te// de yi dbang gis shAkyal+li bstan pa 'di// 'jig rten khams 'dir yun du gnas par 'gyur// zhes dang i pham mgon gyis rgyud bla mA rA// nyon mongs dgra rnams ma lus 'chos pa dang // ngan 'gro'i srid la skyob
7b2(dkar chag): byed gang yin pa// chos skyob ston phyir nas bstan bcos te// gnyis po 'di dgra gzhan gyi lugs la med// gang zhig rgyal ba'i bstan pa 'ba' zhig gis// dbang byas rnam g.yeng med yid can gyis brtsoms// thor pa tho bo dang /
7b3(dkar chag): lom drang rjes mthun pa// de yang drang srong bka' bzhin spyi bos blang // zhes gsungs des na mdo sngags rgyal ba'i bka'i// dgongs 'grel 'gyur 'tshal rnams legs bzhengs pa// de yi bsod nams phung po 'di tsama? zhes// rgyal
7b4(dkar chag): ba'i ye shes spyod yul las gzhan ci// de ltar sngon gyi chos rgyal byang chub sems// lo paN rnams dang mkhas grub ba gang yas kyis// rgyal bka' mdo sngags dgrongs 'grel bcas pa rnams// legs par gzheng dang 'tshodanyan
7b5(dkar chag): gyi sgo nas// gtan mo 5 sgrub bstan pa ni// rgyas par mdzod nas skye dgu'i phyin bde spel// khyad par lnga brgya'i gtsug rgyan u ti shas// bstan la log par rtogs rnams legs bkag nas// bstan pa'i snying po lha chos bdun ldan gyi//
7b6(dkar chag): rnam thar gtsang ma'i bstan pa'i gsol gtod nas// 'brom ston chos kyi rgyal po la sogs pa// gnam gyis sa bkab 'dra ba'i bka' gdams kyis// dam pa mang po smin par mjed pa la// byang gi phyogs 'dir bshad sgrub bstan pa ni//
8a1(dkar chag): rgyus par mdzad nas skye dgu'i bde skyid kyang // rdzogs ldan gnyis pa'i dga' ston mchog la bkod// de yang ming tsam lhag mar gyur pa'i dus// bstan pa'i bdag po blo bzang klu sgrub nyid//
8a2(dkar chag): ngur smrig 'dzin pa'i zlos gar rab bsgyur ba// blo bzang gla gos pa'i dpal zhes sa gsum na// snyan par grags pa'i ba dan 'dzin pa des// thub bstan gzhi rtsa 'dul ba'i bstan pa ni// nyams par gyur pa gzhi nas gso
8a3(dkar chag): bur mdzad// khyad par du'ang rje bcu na 'jam dbyangs kyis// dge bab bshes gnyen mdzad nas the tshom gyi// dA ba bcad nas klu sgrub dgongs don bzhin// mtha' phral zab mo dbu ma'i lta ba dang / bstan pa'i snying
8a4(dkar chag): blo bla med rdo rje thog/ rgyud rgyal gsang 'dus 'khor lo byed ma chog gi/ lam gyi snying po zlab mo'i rdzogs rim gyi// rgyu lus 'od gsal zung 'jug la sogs dang / 'bar 'jig phyug rgya'i srog rtsol lam dang
8a5(dkar chag): ni de yis drangs pa'i lhon skyes bde tshon gyis// stong nyid rtogs pa'i ye shes lam gyi phul// gsang chen snying po'i bstan phyi'i gnang rnams kun// phra zhib lung rig phra mo'i lamo drangs nas// rdo rje 'chang
8a6(dkar chag): gaM dgongs pa ji lta bar// 'grel bar mdzad pa'i sngon med legs bshang ni// brtsom dang 'chang dang nyan pa la sogs pa'i// sgo nas thub bstan gsal bar mdzad pa dang // bong khams bde skying rgyas mdzad
8b1(dkar chag): bka' drin ni// stong gsum lus gser gyi bkang byas nas// bskal par phul kyang gzhal bar gla la nus// sngon byon dam pa'i rnam thar rjes slob cing // dkon mchog mchod dang rgyal ba'i bstan
8b2(dkar chag): la gus// snying stobs brtun po'i sa spyod dbang po ni// dus mtha' 'dir yang phyogs 'dir mi 'byung min// 'di na bsil ldan ljongs kyi dbus 'gyur 'chang // shAkya'i rgyal po'i pho brang lhaHsa zhes// 'dod
8b3(dkar chag): dgu'i 'byung gnas gang gi nor sbyin phyogs// lugs zung dga' ba brgya ldan rgyal po'i khrab// rin chan khang bzang po gam tshar du mngar// rkang 'thung gser pi'i du ku la yos mdzes// 'chi med
8b4(dkar chag): bdag po'i gnas la'ang co 'dri zhing // srid dang zhi ba'i dpal 'byor ma lus po// ngang gis 'du byi'i bsti gnas dam pa der// lus can kun gyi bsod nams ra bar dam pa'i rigs kyi dpag bsam ni// mkhyen
8b5(dkar chag): brtse'i yal 'dab mkha' lam kun khyab sa skyong kun gyi zur phung la// gang gi zhabs kyi rdul phreng nyer bkod stobs kyis 'khor los bsgyur ba ni// mi dpung bsod nams stobyas rgyas zhes grags phyogaso
8b6(dkar chag): kun rna ba'i bcud len byung // gang gau lhag bos ma nyin dang mtshan du gcig tu rgyal po'i bstan pa dar// de 'dzin byed pa'i skyes bu zhab kyis brtan dge 'dun sde rnams chos spyod 'phel// nyams thag 'gro
9a1(dkar chag): 'di ji ltar byas na bde drung skyid pa'i dga' ston la// 'god pa'i thabs bzang 'di ko ci zhes rnam pa kun tu gcig tu phyor/ de tshe 'gro ba'i bde skying ma lus pa// rgyal ba'i bstan pa nyid kyi ngar gud las
9a2(dkar chag): 'byung bar dgongs shing de 'ong de 'dzin gyi// skyes bu zhabs brtan bshad dang sgrub pa las// gzhan du med dgongs tshul nga sgrub pa yi// rgyal sras spyod la zhum med snying stobs kyis// slob pa'i thugs kyi dam bca'
9a3(dkar chag): khur du gzhes// 'di snang srid pa'i phun tshogs ma lus pa// rtswa rtser chags pa'i chu yi thigs pa dang // glog phreng bayo ba'i 'brug gI rol rtsed ltar// gzigs nas bdog pa'i dngos po thams cad la//
9a4(dkar chag): 'jungs pa med par dkon mchog gsum mchod dang // rgyal ba'i sku gsung thugs kyi rten bzhengs shing // dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams la rim gro dang // dge 'dun bsnyen bkur dbul zhing 'phongs pa la// sbyin
9a5(dkar chag): sogs gzhal du med pa'i bsod nams kyis// bya ba'i dngos po ku na lI rnam kun tu// brtson pas sngon byon chos rgyal rnam thar la// rjes su bsnyegs pa'i phyag ris bsnam mi khyab// de drug rnams kyang bstan dang
9a6(dkar chag): 'gro ba la/ phan bde rgyas pa'i thabs mchog kho na las// gzhan du nyid kyi 'di snang 'khri ba ni// rmi lam tsom du'ang mang sogs tshul bsams tshe// ring mo nyid nas grub pa'i dpeng phyug go/ go 'phang mthon por
9b1(dkar chag): gshegs pa'i dam pa zhig/ bstan 'gro'i dpal du byon par gdon mi za// 'di la dngos su mthong dang thos pa yi// nges pa'i gtan tshigs rnam pa mang yod kyang // thun mong bsnyad par bya ba ga la nus// des na
9b2(dkar chag): chos rgyal gang gi rnam dkar gyi// mdzad bzang rgya mtsho lta bu mang mnga' las// 'dir yang skye rgu'i phan bde rgyal ba'i bstan// ngar zhing rgyas dang nge 'dzin skyes bu rnams// sku tshe bstan zhing bshad sgrub 'phel ba dang /
9b3(dkar chag): sa spyod chen po sras 'khor dang bcas pas// thogs med nas bsags sgrib gnyis bag chags rnams// byang zhing tshogs gnyis myur du rdzogs po dang // sku tshe mnga' thang chub srid dpal 'byor rnams// yar
9b4(dkar chag): ngo'i zla ltar mi nub rab rgyus shIng // bong khams 'gro ba'i bde skying ma lus pa// rdzogs ldan bzhin du gong du 'phel ba dang // mar gyur mkha'i mnyam 'gro ba ma lus pa// srid mtsho las sgrol bying chen myur
9b5(dkar chag): thob phyir// rgyal ba'i bka' yi dgongs 'grel 'gyur cog gi/ glegs bla ma nyis brgya dang ni nyer lnga'i grangs// mthing shog nam mkha' bzhun 'dra'i ngos yangs por// dbu khang so sor thub pa chen po dang //
9b6(dkar chag): rdo rje snying sog sa de bzhin gshegs pa ni// so lnga po rnams tshar ni bcu gcig dang // sprin gyi bla ma la sogs bad gshegs brgyad// bdun cher rdor sems mi 'khrug rnam snang bcas// gsum gsum la sogs
10a1(dkar chag): sgyu yi snang brnyan ni// ye shes sems dpa' mngon sum byon pa ltar// rims bzhin bsod nams zhing gi mchog tu bzhugs// shog ngos gtsu ma gser sbyangs gzhu brtul gyi// khub dpon yig mkhas
10a2(dkar chag): pa'i smyug gu yis// g.yo zol meng par gang 'drongs kyis bskrun bri'o// yoM ge dbyibs legs 'bur 'dod brda' sdebs drag/ nyin byed phreng ba cher du mngar bA ltar// yid 'ong gzo 'bar mig gi bdud rtsi 'dra// lus can
10a3(dkar chag): rnams lha blang dung ngor bya'i gnas// mngon sum ston ltar lha me lhang der bzhugs// pad rag mdangs lde 'khu ba'i glegs bu shing // gser sho ga ri mo bkra ba nyi zla ltar// dgub bya thabs shes zung 'jug rten
10a4(dkar chag): 'brel ston// glegs tshob glegs thag rgyu tshogs phun tshogs shing // ding phon gan gos thon thi spus legs dang // mdzod gos rnying ma kha dog sna tshogs kyi// zhal kheb gdong dor burtsegs ma na bza' ling //
10a5(dkar chag): la srogs rgyu tshogs mu lus phun sum tshogs// gtsug lag mang por sbyangs pa'i yon tan can// 'byung gnas e snye chos lung dkar po nas// dpon yig mkhas 'dus sdor mo'i 'du byed kyis//
10a6(dkar chag): li byin mkhan po'i khengs pa 'phrog gam snyam// sngon mang ngo mtshar phul du rab byung zhing // srid dang zhi pa'i yon tan ma lus pa// gcig tu bsdus 'dra 'dzam gling rgyan gcig ni// skye rgu'i bsod nams
10b1(dkar chag): zhing gi mchog tu bskrun// 'di ltar bskrun pa'i rgyu song rags rim grangs// gtsom gser brtul dbus zho lnga stong dang // tshig brgya nyer lnga se pa phyed bcu gsum// dngul brtul dbus zho tshig stong bcus pa sogs// rgyu song rnam
10b2(dkar chag): ni dngul du phub pa la// dngul srang tshig khri brgya nga stong drug brgya dang // nyer gcig/ zho brgyad skar lnga la sogs pa// zang zing sgra mo'i nor rdzas snying med la// gnas skabs mthar thug kun tu longs spyad pi'o// mi zad
10b3(dkar chag): na mkha' mdzod kyi sgo 'phar phye// srid zhi'i rgyan gcig bsten 'gyur 'di rnams kyi// pu sta kAHrnams swa'i nang rnamasu// sde snod gsum dang rgyud sde bzhi dang ni// spyi yi dgongs 'grel thor bu dang bcas pa'i// bzhugs tshul go rim rnam grangs
10b4(dkar chag): myang na yang // 'dir ni mchog dang dman pa'i go rim bzhin// thog mar nang don rig pa'i skor la ni// theg pa thun mo min dang thun mong gi/ theg pa chung ngu'i bstan bcos rim pa dang // gzhan dag tshur gtsad gtan tshig rig pa dang / sgra
10b5(dkar chag): rig gzhan dag rjes 'dzin gso rig dang // bzo rig thor bu ba yi skor dang ni// bod kyi mkhas pa snga rabs rnams kyis ni// mdzad pa'i dkar chag rnying par 'khor rnams dang // gsar bcug mdo sngags rig gnas sna tshogs
10b6(dkar chag): dang // bsngo ba smon lam bkra shis bcas pa yi// chos chen go rim ji ltar bzhugs pa'i tshul// so sor ma 'dres rgyas shing gsal bar ni// mkhas pa'i gsung bzhin rim par sgrigs Sha la//
11a1(dkar chag): ka ba la khyad par du 'phags pa'i bstod pa slob dpon mtho btsun grub rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA daM ba dang / yo tsA ba rin chen mchog gi 'gyur la dpal brtsegs kyis gtan la phab pa/ de'i 'grel pa
11a2(dkar chag): slob dpon shes rab go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza ran+d+ha na dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ thams cad mkhyen pa dbang phyug chen po'i bstod pa zhes bya ba mtho btsun grub rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza ran+ta na dang / lo tsa ba rin chen
11a3(dkar chag): bzang po'i 'gyur/ lha las phul du byung bar bstod pa slob dpon bde byed bdag pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA de ba dang / lo tsA ba rin chen mchog gi 'gyur la/ dpal brtsegs kyis bcos shing gtan la phab pa/ de'i rgya cher bshad
11a4(dkar chag): pa slob dpon shes rab go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza ran+d+ha nA dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'phags ma nor rgyun mas ma'aba'i sangs rgyas kyi bstod pa/ paN+Di ta rgyal ba bzang po dang / lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i
11a5(dkar chag): 'gyur/ chos sku la gnas pa'i yon tan thun mong ma yin pa'i bstod pa/ slob dpon 'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzi na mi tra dang / shrI lin+d+ra bo d+hi dang / lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ de kho na nyid la bstod pa dpal gyi
11a6(dkar chag): go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta many+dzu shrI b+hU drA dang / lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ bdud btul ba la bstod pa rab dga'i lha'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i bstod pa'i tshogs kyi skor la/ chos kyi dbyings su bstod
11b1(dkar chag): pa dang / dpe med par bstod pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das par bstod pa dang / sems kyi rdo rje'i bstod pa dang / don dam par bstod pa dang / sku gsum la bstod pa rnams paN+Di ta nag po pa dang / nag tsho tshul rgyal gyi 'gyur/ sku
11b2(dkar chag): gsum la bstod pa'i 'grel pa paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha kA ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ sems can mgu bar bya ba'i bstod pa jo bo rje dang / nag tsho tshul rgyal gyi 'gyur/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma'i bstod pa paN+Di ta thig la
11b3(dkar chag): bum pa dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ bsam gyis mi khyab par bstod pa/ bstod pa las 'das par bstod pa/ bla na med pa'i bstod pa/ rje btsun 'jam dpal gyi don dam pa'i bstod pa/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi
11b4(dkar chag): snying rje la bstod pa/ gnas chen po brgyad kyi mchod rten la bstod pa/ mi 'dra cha gnyis/ mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi tshul la bstod pa/ phyag 'tshal ba'i bstod pa/ dmyal ba nas 'don pa'i bstod pa/ paN+Di ta ti la ka dang / pa tshab nyi ma
11b5(dkar chag): grags kyi 'gyur rnams so// slob dpon ma tri tsi tras mdzad pa'i bstod pa'i skor la/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das la bstod pa bsngags par 'os pa bsngags po zhes bya ba paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA daM ba dang / lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i
11b6(dkar chag): 'gyur/ de'i le'u bcu gsum pa pad+ma ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ dkon mchog gsum la bkra shis kyi bstod pa paN+Di ta bi d+yA ka ra sing ha pra b+hA dang / lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ti'i 'gyur/ sangs rgyas kyi
12a1(dkar chag): mtshan la bstod pa dang / gcig las 'phros pa'i bstod pa dang / sangs rgyas sum cu rtsa lnga'i bstod pa mtshan rin po ches spras pa zhes bya ba rnams slob dpon mA tr-i tsi tAs mdzad pa'o// dge bsnyen mtha'
12a2(dkar chag): yas lhas mdzad pa'i tshig brgyad pa'i bstod pa/ slob dpon ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa'i dkon mchog gsum gyi bstod pa/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon rgyal ba'i sras kyis mdzad pa paN+Di ta dz+nyA na shAn+ti dang / lo tsA ba dpal gyi lhun po'i sde'i 'gyur/
12a3(dkar chag): dkon mchog gsum gyi bstod pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ brgya lnga bcu pa'i bstod pa slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon dga' byed
12a4(dkar chag): snyem pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha ka ra warma dang / l-i tsA ba shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur/ gaN+DI'i bstod pa slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa paN+Di ta rgyala'i bA'i sde dang / lo tsA ba d+harma yon tan gyi 'gyur/ sbrel mar bstod pa zhes bya ba slob
12a5(dkar chag): dpon ma ti tsi tra dang / slob dpon 'i phyogs glang gnyis kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ku mA ra ka la sha dang / lo tsA ba bsod nams bzang po'i 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la bstod pa/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa'i bstod
12a6(dkar chag): pa slob dpon dkon mchog 'bangs kyis mdzad pa/ yon tan mtha' yas par bstod pa slob dpon dkon mchog 'bangs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA de ba dang / lo tsA ba rin chen mchog gi 'gyur la dpal brtsegs kyis bcos pa/
12b1(dkar chag): yon tan mtha' yas par bstod pa'i 'grel pa dang / yon tan mtha' yas pa'i don gyi tshig le'ur byas pa gnyis phyogs glang gis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sarba dz+nyA dwe ba dang / lo tsA ba rin chen mchog gi 'gyur la dpal brtsegs kyis
12b2(dkar chag): bcos pa/ sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das pa la bstod pa dpal chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa/ bshags pa'i bstod pa slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud d+hA kA ra war+m+ma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ de'i
12b3(dkar chag): 'grel pa slob dpon sangs rgyas zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA de nyid dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ sangs rgyas dbang bskur ba zhes bya ba'i bstod pa lo tsA bo rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das la bstod pa dpal
12b4(dkar chag): rdo rje 'dzin gyi dbyangs/ 'di rgyud dag las phyung ba yin/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa dang gnyis/ paN+Di ta bid+yA kA ra pra b+hA dang / lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa lnga'i bstod pa dang /
12b5(dkar chag): de bzhin gshegs pa bdun gyi bstod pa gnyis pad+ma kA ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rIn chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa brgyad la bstod pa slob dpon zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa/ rab tu snga bar nam langs pa'i bstod pa dang /
12b6(dkar chag): gnas chen po brgyad kyi mchod rten la phyag 'tshal ba'i bstod pa gnyis kha che'i rgyal po shrI ha ri sha daM bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rA dza shrI dz+nyA na mi tra dang / khe'u gang yon tan 'bar gyi 'gyur/ bskal bzang sangs rgyas stong gi bstod
13a1(dkar chag): pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan brjod rgyan gyi phreng ba zhes bya ba kha che baN chen gyis mdzad pa/ sbyor ba bzhi'i lha'i bstod pa/ paN+Di ta rat+na kIrtis mdzad pa/ bal po ma hA ba ni'i ring 'gyur/
13a2(dkar chag): bdag nyid chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan la bstod pa rgya gar gyi mkhan pa~M su ga tA shrIs mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang / shAkya'i dge slong kun dga' rgya lnga mtshani dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ bla ma dam pa chos kyi
13a3(dkar chag): rgyal po la bstod pa/ paN+Di ta lan+thi ka ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba shong ston gyis bsgyur ba dus mchod bzhi'i tshig le'ur byas pa kha che'i paN+Di ta shAkya shrIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal
13a4(dkar chag): gyi 'gyur/ tshigs su bcad pagacig pa'i 'grel pa phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa/ zha lu mo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ shAkya thub pa'i bstod pa bcu pa paN chen nags kyi rin chen gyis mdzad pa/ baN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba bstod
13a5(dkar chag): nams rgya mtsho'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / rgyud sde'i lha so so'i bstod pa rnams ni rang rang so so'i skabs su bri bar bya'o// yon tan mtha' yas rgya mtsho mnga' ba yi// mchod gnas bla med rnams kyi bstod pa'i
13a6(dkar chag): tshogs// sdeb sbyor snyan dngags rgyan gyis rab mdzes pa// 'grel pa dang bcas drug cu re bzhi bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag srid zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las thun mong ba'i mchod pa brjod pa'i tshul
13b1(dkar chag): gyis bstod pa'i tshogs bkod pa'i skabs te dang po'o// da ni rig pa'i gnas lnga las/ nang rig pa'i bstan bcos las/ 'bras bu sngags dang rgyu mtshan nyid kyi theg pa'i skor las/ dang po 'bras bu sngags kyi theg pa'i skor ni//
13b2(dkar chag): ka pa la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ kha che'i paN+Di ta so ma nA tha dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po 'bro dge slong shes rab grags kyis bsgyur ba las/ mkhas pa chen po shong ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis bcos
13b3(dkar chag): shing gtan la phab pa'o// 'di ni rtsa 'grel phyogs gcig tu bsdebs na bsod nams che zhing / ding sang bshad nyan dar ba'i phyir phan che ba la bsams nas 'dir bris pa yin gyi/ rgyud kyi rgyal po 'di bstan bcos kyi khongs su
13b4(dkar chag): gtogs nas bris pa ni ma yin no// bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel bshad rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rjes su 'jug pa stong phrag bcu gnyis pa dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs
13b5(dkar chag): dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i phyi 'jig rten khams kyi le'u dang / nang sems can khams kyi le'u gnyis/ 'gyur rgyud dang 'dra ba bzhugs so// / kha pa la dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa spyan ras gzigs
13b6(dkar chag): kyis mdzad pa'i dbang gi le'u dang / sgrub thabs kyi le'u dang / ye shes kyi le'u rnams 'gyur snga ma dang 'dra ba bzhugs so// / ga pa la 'jig rten dbang phyug gi sprul pa'i sku pad+ma dkar pos mdzad pa'i don dam
14a1(dkar chag): bsnyen pa zhes bya ba/ kha che'i paN+Di tA zla ba mgron pos bsgyur nas gtan la phab pa dang / dpal ldan dri ma dang bral ba'i 'od kyi rgyud la 'jug pa'i bshad sbyar mi g.yo ba'i snying po snang ba zhes bya ba dbang lo tsA
14a2(dkar chag): bapa blo brtan gyis bsgyur ba dang dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud kyi rgyal po'i dka' 'grel pad+ma tso na zhes bya ba dpal dus 'khor zhabs chen pos mdzad pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta so ma nA thas bsgyur ba dang / dbang mdor bsten pa'i 'gro la bshad
14a3(dkar chag): don dam bsdus pa zhes bya ba phyag rgya chen po grub pa'i slob dpon dpal nA ro'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta d+harma d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba las/ slar yang sgra tshad pa rin rgyal gyis bcos
14a4(dkar chag): shing gtan la phab pa dbang mdor bstan pa'i bshad pa legs pa'i bu dpal 'dzin dga' bas mdzad pa/ rgya gar shar phyogs kyi gnas brtan chen po byang chub sems dpa' nags kyi rin chen dang / rtses thang lo ts+tsha ba gzhon nu
14a5(dkar chag): dpal gyis bsgyur ba rnams bzhugs so// / nga pa la dbang mdor bstan pa'i 'grel pa dus zhabs pos mdzad pa paN+Di ta zla ba mgon po dang / 'bro shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ dbang mdor bstan gyi dka' 'grel
14a6(dkar chag): sh+lo ka sum brgya drug cu pa bu ston gyi 'gyur/ dbang rab byed kyi 'grel pa rdo rje'i tshig 'byed pa zhes bya ba slob dpon dA ri ka pas mdzad po 'bro shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo sgrub pa'i thabs yan lag bzhi pa
14b1(dkar chag): zhes bya ba dus zhabs pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi shwa shrI dang / lo tsA ba gyi rdo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ dus 'khor gyi sgrub thabs yan lag bcu gcig pa dus zhabs pa chen pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta zla ba mgon po dang / lo ts+tsha ba shes
14b2(dkar chag): rab grogs kyi 'gyur/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo sgrub pa'i thabs dang / dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga gnyis slob dpon sA d+hA pu tras mdzad pa paN+Di ta wA gI shwa ra gup+ta dang / lo tsA ba rA chos rab kyi 'gyur/ dus 'khor gyi dkyil cho ga yid
14b3(dkar chag): 'od phreng ba zhes bya ba dus zhabs pa chung bas mdzod pa/ paN+Di ta bi na shrI dang / lo tsA ba mchi mas yon tan 'bar gyi 'gyur/ dus 'khor lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs dus zhabs pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud d+hA shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA
14b4(dkar chag): pa byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ dus 'khor gyi sgrub thabs lhan cig skyes pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rol pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta wA gI shwa ra dang / rwa chos rab kyi 'gyur/ rdzogs pa'i rim pa ston po'i skor la byang chub
14b5(dkar chag): sems dpa' phyag na rdo rjes mdzad pa'i sbyor drug/ de pAl rab 'byor zhi ba dang / cog ro ting 'dzin bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'di phyag rdor stod 'grel las gud du phye bar snang ste/ sngar gyi rnams kyis bris 'dug pas bris/ dus kyi
14b6(dkar chag): 'khor lo'i snying po'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i sgru bo thabs bram ze bsod snyoms pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrI b+ha dra bo d+hi dang / gyi rdo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i man ngag dus zhabs pa chen pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud d+hA ka ra b+ha dra
15a1(dkar chag): dang / gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ sbyor ba yan lag drug gi man ngag dpal a nu ba ma rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba mi mnyam bzang po'i 'gyur/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon nyi ma
15a2(dkar chag): dpal ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ dus 'khor gyi man ngag nyi zla sgrub pa zhes bya ba rigs gsum mgon pos/ paN+Di ta be kun ni la gsungs pa/ bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ ye shes spyan sgrub dus zhabs pas
15a3(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ rnal 'byor gsum gyi snying po gsal ba zhes bya ba/ 'jo ma dbyangs grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta so ma nA tha dang / lo tsA ba 'bri shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ sbyor ba yan la ga drug gi man ngag
15a4(dkar chag): dus zhabs snyan rgyud ces bya ba/ paN+Di ta so ma nA tha shrI dang / 'bro shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ sbyor ba yan lag drug gi 'grel pa sbas pa mig 'byed ces bya ba/ slob dpon a wa d+hU tI pas mdzad pa/ zla ba grags pa'i 'gyur/ sbyor
15a5(dkar chag): pa yan lag drug gi man ngag tsi lu paN+Di tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sa man+ta shrI dang / lo ts+tsha ba rA chos rab kyi 'gyur/ sha ba ri pa'i sbyor drug bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ sbyor ba'i phreng ba rtsa mi sangs rgyas grags pas mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba dag
15a6(dkar chag): tshul shes rab dpal gyi 'gyur/ nang gi snye ma paN+Di ta bi b+hU ti tsan+d+ras mdzad pa/ de nyid kyi rang 'gyur/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i rtsa ba'i ltung ba byang chub sems dpas mdzad pa/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i sdom tshig slob dpon a b+hA ya ka ras mdzad
15b1(dkar chag): pa/ paN+Di tA ri bo pa dang / lo tsA ba kher gang 'khor lo grags kyi 'gyur/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i bstod pa rgyun chags zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta legs pa'i grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA bi na ya shrI mi tA dang / lo tsA ba ldan mA
15b2(dkar chag): tshul khrims seng ge'i 'gyur/ brgyad brgyad drug cu rtsa bzhi'i rnal 'byor ma'i gtor cho ga/ paN+Di ta kIrti tsan+d+ra de nga / lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ dus 'khor la 'jug po zhes bya ba'i rtsis kyi bstan bcos paN+Di ta 'jigs
15b3(dkar chag): med 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa de nyid dang / ding ri chos grags kyi 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta rA hu laM shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyis bcos pa/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rtsis kyi man ngag yan lag lnga'i rtsiso dang /
15b4(dkar chag): nyi zla 'dzin pa'i rtsis dang / gza' lnga so so'i rkyang rtsis kyi man ngag paN+Di ta chen po shAkya shrI b+ha dras mdzad pa/ dpal ldan mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas la sogs pa rgyud sna tshogs pa rnams kyi rnal 'byor yan lag drug pa dpe med srung
15b5(dkar chag): bas mdzad pa/ la stong ding ri bla 'khor mkhan pa khrod du/ rgya gar shar phyogs dza ga ta la'i paN+Di ta chen po bi b+hU ti tsan+d+ra dang / gnyal gyi lo tsA ba mi mnyam bzang pos ba sgyur ba/ rnal 'byor yan lag drug gi brjed byang yon tan gyis
15b6(dkar chag): 'gengs pa zhes bya ba/ mkhas pa chen po gnas brtan nyi ma dpal ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta shrI bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ras bsgyur ba/ 'di gnyis kyi zhu chen dbang lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pas mdzad pa rnams
16a1(dkar chag): bzhugs so// / tsa pA la dbang mdor bstan gyi 'grel pa paN+Di ta rnam rgyal dbang pos mdzad pa/ dbang blo brtan gyi 'gyur/ sbyor drug gi man ngag rdo rje tshig gi snying po bsdus pa zhes bya ba dang /
16a2(dkar chag): de'i 'grel pa gnyis pa Na chen shAkya shrIs mdzad pa de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dbyal chos bzang gi 'gyur/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i rab gnas tshogs 'khor/ sbyin sreg gsum slob dpon dus 'khor zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta wA gI shwa ra dang /
16a3(dkar chag): lo tsA ba rA chos rab kyi 'gyur/ mtshan brjod dus 'khor lugs su bshad pa grub thob nyi ma dpal ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ bdud rtsi thigs pa zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta nor bu dpal ye shes dang / nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer dang / chag lo
16a4(dkar chag): tsA ba chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa bdud rtsi thigs pa sgron ma gsal ba zhes bya ba a nu pa ma rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ga ta shrI dang / lo tsA ba d+harma kIr+t+ti dang / rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ mtshan brjod
16a5(dkar chag): 'grel pa mi'i dbang pos grags pas mdzad pa dang / mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa dri ma med pa'i 'od byang chub sems dpa' pad+ma dkar pos mdzad zer ba dge slong bsod snyoms pa'i 'gyur/ mtshan brjod phan yon gyi 'grel pa
16a6(dkar chag): sngags kyi snying po bsdus pa dus zhabs pas mdzad pa/ 'di gsum bong ma yin par snang ste/ snga ma rnams kyis bris snang bas bzhugs su bcug/ yin/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i mngon par rtogs pa byang chub sems
16b1(dkar chag): dpa' spyan ras gzigs kyis mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so// // shes dang shes bya dbyer med dus 'khor lo// phyi nang gzhan gsum bden gnyis dbyer med par// ston pa'i bstan bcos rjes 'brangs dang bcas pa//
16b2(dkar chag): mchog tu gyur pa lnga bcu rtsa gnyis bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar cha ga srong zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/ thabs shes rab gnyis su med pa'i rgyud dus 'khor gyi skabs te/ sngags skor gyi le'u dang
16b3(dkar chag): po'o// de ltar thabs shes rab gnyis su med pa'i rgyud kyi skor gyi bstan bcos rnams bkod nas/ nga ni rgyud sde sgo drug pa rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i rgyud/ bde mchog gi rgyud kyi skor gyi bstan bcos la//
16b4(dkar chag): cha ba la bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi stod 'grel byang chub sems dpa' phyag na rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dpal rab 'byor zhi ba dang / lo tsA ba cog gru ting nge 'dzin bzang pos bsgyur ba las/ shong lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pas bcos shing dag
16b5(dkar chag): par byas pa/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel pa sgrub pa'i thabs kyi gleng gzhi zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po lwa ba pas mdzad pa 'gos kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi dka' 'grel slob dpon b+ha ba b+ha Tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta mi mnyam
16b6(dkar chag): rdo rje dang / lo tsA ba ba ri rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi dka' 'grel rin po che'i tshogs zhes bya ba slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta tA ra ka lak+Sha dang / lo tsA ba gu na shrI'i 'gyur rnams bzhugaso// //
17a1(dkar chag): dza pa la bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi dka' 'grel dpa' bo yid 'ong zhes bya ba slob dpon skal ldan grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi dka
17a2(dkar chag): 'bral slob dpon lang+ga rgyal ba bzang pos mdzad pa/ sh+lo ka bdun brgya pa/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel pa 'khor lo sdom pa'i sgrub thabs gnas pa'i man ngag thams cad rgya cher 'grel pa zhes bya ba dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob
17a3(dkar chag): dben lha sbas kyis mdzad pa/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel pa yon tan ma lus pa'i gnas zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta chos skyong dang / lo tsA ba rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud
17a4(dkar chag): dang / de'i dka' 'grel slob dpon kong+ka nas mdzad pa gnyis sbyar ba'i 'grel pa/ gnyi ga'i bshad sbyar zhes bya ba slob dpon ta thA ga ta rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo
17a5(dkar chag): sdom pa'i 'grel pa de kho na nyid mkhas pa zhes bya ba/ rtag po'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ sdom pa'i rgyud nyung ngu'i mtshams sbyor paN+Di te su ma ti kirtis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang /
17a6(dkar chag): lo tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi rgya cher bshad pa tshig don rab tu gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pa ra he ta dang / lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyi
17b1(dkar chag): 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / nya pa la bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel pa in+d+ra b+hu d+his mdzad pa dang / bde mchog nges par brjod pa'i rgyud kyi 'grol po slob da bo nau shu rang gA badz+ras mdzod pa/ l-i ts+tsha ba 'phags pa
17b2(dkar chag): shes rab kyi 'gyur gnyis bzhugs so// / ta paM la bde mchog gi the shad rgyud rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon b+he ba b+ha Ta'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lhas
17b3(dkar chag): btsas kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel de kho na nyid brtan par byed pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po nor bzang gis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba g+h+ri jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ gsang ba rdo rje'i
17b4(dkar chag): rgyud kyi 'grel pa DoM bi he ru kas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rat+na badz+ra dang / lo tsA bA shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ gsang chen pad+ma zhes bya ba'i rgya cher 'grel pa kho che'i mkhan po longs spyod rdo rjes mdzad pa/ de nyid kyi rang 'gyur rnams bzhugs
17b5(dkar chag): so// phyi ma 'di bde mchog dang / sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi rgyud 'grel du 'dod pa ci rigs su snang zhing / so sor dbye dka' bar snang na'ang sdom pa 'byung ba'i rgyud phyi mo'i phyi ma zhes bshad pa dang / mkha' 'gro ma ni rdo rje phag
17b6(dkar chag): mo'o zhes sogs pade mchog dang mthun pa rogs che bar snang bas 'dir bkod // / tha ba la rdo rje mkho' 'gro'i 'grel ba mching ba gcig bzhug so// / da pa la mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i 'grel pa
18a1(dkar chag): gru gzings zhes bya ba slob dpon pad+ma badz+rAs mdzad pa zlo ka stong phrag brgyad pa paN+Di ta dza ya se na dang / mats+tsha ba chos kyi yon tan gyi 'gyur bzhugs so// / na pa la sdom pa 'byung ba/
18a2(dkar chag): rgyud kyi dka' 'grel pad+ma can zhes bya ba dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon rat+na rak+Shi tAs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta thams cad mkhyen pa'i dpal gyis rang 'gyur du byas pa la/ shong bro brtan gyis bcos pa/ he ru ka mngon 'byung gi 'grel
18a3(dkar chag): yi ge \u0f7fd+yA d+ha zhes b+hA ba~M/ paN+Di ta zla ba gzhon nus na dz+ye gA baN+Di tat+t+wa thA gr-I tA rak+Shi tA dang / oM ts+tsha ba d+hi mablo gros kyi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor mgun tu spyod pa'i rgyud kyi bshad sbyar/ slob dpon tA thA ga tA rat+na tis mdzad pa/ ba
18a4(dkar chag): denyid dang / lo ts+tsha ba rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor ma'i kun tu spyod pa'i bshad pa tshig don rab tu gsol ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad ba/ paN+Di ti pA ra tsi ta dang / lo tsA ba 'a phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur/
18a5(dkar chag): bde mchog na mkha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa slob dpon rin tshon 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta stong nyid ting nge 'dzin dang / lo tsA ba shes rab ye shes kyi 'gyur/ de ltar rgyud so so'i 'grel pa rnams bkod nas/ sgrub
18a6(dkar chag): thabs dkyil chog/ man ngag la sogs pa'i sgor ni/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa'i bstod pa/ bde mchog gi sgrub thabs de kho na nyid kyi snying po zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' phyag na rdo rjes mdzad pa/ baN+Di
18b1(dkar chag): so ma nA thas/ gnyal mi shes rab mchog gi don du bsgyur ba/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug lU i pas mdzad pa'i bde mchog gi sgrub thabs dpal bcom ldan 'das mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba paN+Di ta shwad+d+ha ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba
18b2(dkar chag): rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta nA ba ko Ti pa dang / lo tsA ba 'gros lhas btsas kyis bcos pa/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa 'i sgrub thabs de kho na nyid bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po rig pa'i 'i brtul zhugs pa dpel
18b3(dkar chag): dA ri ka pas mdzad pa/ b+hang+ga la'i paN+Di ta ku mA ra badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong nyi ma rdo rje'i 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i cho ga de kho na nyid la 'jug pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rig pa'i brtul zhugs pa/ dpal dA ri ka pas
18b4(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ku mA ra badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba dge slong nyi ma rdo rje dang / spyil cig gi tho gar dge mdzes kyi 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo sprom pa'i bstod pa don thams cad grub pa rnam dag gtsug gi nor bu zhes bya ba slob
18b5(dkar chag): dpon dA ri kA bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma badz+ra dang / lo tsA brgya brtson seng gi 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta ku mA rA badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba nyi ma rdo rjes bcos pa/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu bas mdzad pa'i bde mchog lus kyi dkyil 'khor gyi dkyil
18b6(dkar chag): chog dbang gi bya ba mdor bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta kriSh+Na ba dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa lus kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba
19a1(dkar chag): mal gyo blo gros grags kyi 'gyur/ rdzogs rim ston pa 'khor lo sdom pa'i rim pa lnga pa slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kr-iSh+Na pa dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur la/ bar+Na
19a2(dkar chag): ta su ma ti kIrti dang lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyis bcos pa ste/ de dag la dril bu skor gsum du grags so// slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa'i bde mchog lus dkyil gyi mngon par rtogs pa dang / rim lnga'i rang 'grel
19a3(dkar chag): gnyis/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ bde mchog lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ni ska laM ka dang / lo tsA ba dpyal chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog
19a4(dkar chag): lha lnga'i sgrub thabs rin po che yid bzhin gyi nor bu zhes bya ba slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ti su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ bde mchog phyag gnyis pa lhan cig skyes pa'i sgrub thabs
19a5(dkar chag): slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rat+na rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i bstod pa rgyal po in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad
19a6(dkar chag): pa dang / bde mchog lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha la bstod pa rin po che'i sgyu 'phrul sbyin pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / mar pa chos dbang gi 'gyur/ bde mchog 'khor lo'i bstod pa
19b1(dkar chag): rgyun chags rtog ge ba chen po chos kyi glags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma Ni ka shrI dz+nyA na dang / chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ bde mchog sbyangs pa'i yon tan bcu gsum mya'i sgrub thabs rin po che gtsug gi nor bu zhes bya ba/ slob
19b2(dkar chag): dpon chen po lwa ba pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / lo ts+tsha ba mar pa chos dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rin po che rab tu gsal ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/ slob dpon chen po lwa ba pos mdzad
19b3(dkar chag): pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA bA mar ba chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ nag po pa'i skor la/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i sgrub thabs nag po spyod pa bas mdzad pa/ sh+lo ka brgya nyi shu brgyad pa dang / bde mchog 'khor lo'i dkyil
19b4(dkar chag): ga nag po spyod pa pas mdzad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lngas btsas kyi 'gyur/ yang dkyil chog ngo nyid paN+Di ta dAR+Ya r-iskaM b+he dra dang / lo chen rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog 'khor lo'i sbyin sreg
19b5(dkar chag): gi cho ga nag po spyong ba pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba rig pa gzhon nu'i 'gyur te bskyed pa'i rim pa skor gsum mo// rdzogs rim skor gsum la/ dpyid kyi thig le nag po spyod pa pas mdzad pa/ baN+Di ta su mu ti kIN+Di
19b6(dkar chag): dang / lo ts+tsha ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ gsang ba'i de kho na nyid rab tu gsal ba brtul zhugs spyod pa nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang /
20a1(dkar chag): lo tsA ba chos kyi dbang phyug gis bcos pa/ rim pa bzhi pa nag po spyod pa pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur te/ nag po chos drug tu grags so//
20a2(dkar chag): bde mchog yi ge bdun pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ngag gi dbang phyug dang / lo tsA ba klog sgyu shes rab brtsegs kyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / pA pa la rdo rje sems dpa'i
20a3(dkar chag): sgrub thabs zhes bya ba'i bde mo chog gi sgrub thabs slob dpon lU i bas mdzad pa/ rgyal po oMn+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa'i bde mchog gi rgyun bshags bsdus pa/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i snying po'i de kho na nyid grub pa slob dpon dzA
20a4(dkar chag): yon+d+ha ra ba dzad pa/ bdag byin gyis brlab pa'i man ngag dang / phyag rgya chen po'i man ngag gnyis ri khrod chen po'i gsung / rtsa mi'i 'gyur/ bde mchog lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs in+d+ra b+hu d+hI 'bring pos mdzad pa/ rtsa mi'i
20a5(dkar chag): 'gyur/ sdom pa bshad pa zhes bya ba slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ 'or ston chos 'byung gi 'gyur/ bde mchog yi ge bdun pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa/ slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa'i 'khor
20a6(dkar chag): lo sdom pa'i sgrub thabs bdud rtsi 'dzag pa zhes bya ba/ bde mchog shes par byed pa zhes bya ba bde mchog gi mngon par rtogs pa slob dpon byang chub rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta b+ha dra shrI bo d+hi dang / lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi
20b1(dkar chag): bde mchog dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon DoM bi hA ru kas mdzad pa rje bo r+d+ha dang / nug tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ bde mchog gi sgrub thabs m+b+ha i bas mdzad pa'i 'grel pa pradz+nyA rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ bAN+Di tas/
20b2(dkar chag): ma ti kIrti dang / yo tsA ba blo ldan shI s+ya rab kyi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i phyi rol mchid pa'i cho ga/ gtor ma'i cho ga/ lag mchod kyi cho ga/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga ste/ pradz+nyA rak+Shi ta'i chos bzhir
20b3(dkar chag): grags pa rnams/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i dbang gi bya ba'i rim pa/ paN+Di ta chen po slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rje'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ 'di ni lo tsA ba chen po
20b4(dkar chag): thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston zhabs kyi bka' drin las/ brda sprod pa'i tshul la blo'i snang ba cung zad skyes pa/ lo tsA ba d+hArma shrI b+hA dra'i 'gyur/ bde mchog ldan skyes myur me mdzad kyi mdzad pa nag tsho'i 'gyur/ bde mchog gi
20b5(dkar chag): sbyin sreg gi spyi'i glusal byung pad+ma dbyangs kyi mdzad pa/ bde mchog gi sUts+tsha'i cho ga ba ri lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'o sgrub thabs paN+Di tA lang+ga rgyal ba bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang / ba ri lo tsA ba'i
20b6(dkar chag): 'gyur/ 'khro rje lo sbom po'i de kyol 'khor gyi cho ga paN+Di ta lang+ga rgyal ba bzong pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta 'jam dpal dang / lo tsA bo dge slong ba ro'i 'gyur/ dpal lhan cig skyes pa'i bdag byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa
21a1(dkar chag): pas mdzad pa me nyag lo tsA'i 'gyur/ dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs nA ro bas mdzad pa/ dpal he ru ka'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba slob dpon rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ baN+Dit+tad+hAm shrI b+hU dra dang /
21a2(dkar chag): lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog gi bkra shis slob dpon rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta tA ra ka la shu dang / zhus byas kyi lo tsA ba tshul khrims bkra shis kyi 'gyur/ de kho na nyid kyi snying po'i sgrub thabs
21a3(dkar chag): slob dpon dang byed go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi nA ya ka dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ he ru ka'i rnam dge slob dpon shrad+d+ha ka ra warmas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde me chog
21a4(dkar chag): bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs bram ze b+hing+ga ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta gzhon nu bum pa'i rang 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / mar ba 'i chos dbang gis bcos pa/ bde mchog yi ge bdun pa'i sgrub thabs paN+Di tA gnyis med rdo rjes
21a5(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ mar ba'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ mai tri pas mdzad pa'i bang mchog bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs/ rgya gar phyag na rdo rje dang / ba reg thos pa dga'i 'gyur la/ pa ri lo tsA bas btsos shing / slad kyi paN+Di tA bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA
21a6(dkar chag): nan dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyis bcos shing gtan la phab pa/ bde mchog bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs 'khor lo sdom pa'i man ngag ces bya ba slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i ra
21b1(dkar chag): gnas slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / rma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ bde mchog bcu gsum pa nags rin gyis mdzad pa/ lU i pas mdzad pa'i bde mchog gi mngon rtogs kyi 'grel pa/ jo bo rjes
21b2(dkar chag): mdzad pa paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ jo bo rjes mdzad pa'i bde mchog lha bcu gsum ma'i sgrub thabs dang / lha lnga ma'i sgrub thabs gnyis pa paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/
21b3(dkar chag): bde mchog dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs jo bo rjes mdzad pa de nyid dang / nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ de'i rdzogs rim ston par byed pa rdo rje ga ngan gyi glu rtsa 'grel jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba tshul
21b4(dkar chag): khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ spyod pa'i glu rtsa 'grel jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / nag tshe tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ bde mchog lU i pa'i rjes su 'brangs pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon a b+ha yA ka ra gup+tas mdzad pa/
21b5(dkar chag): paN+Di ta rat+na rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba zhang grub pa dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ dbang gis rab tu byed pa zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon a b+ha yA ka ra gup+tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba shes rab dpal gyi 'gyur/ bde
21b6(dkar chag): mchog ljin skyes kyi sgrub thabs rang byin gyis brlab pa zhes bya ba slob dpon a b+ha yA ka ras mdzod pa/ paN+Di ta rat+na rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ bde mchog gi sgrub thabs dpal nyin mor mdzad kyis mdzad
22a1(dkar chag): pa/ bar+t+ti t+ta su b+hU ti shan+ti dang / lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog gi sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon nyin mdzad rdo rjes mdzad pa/ dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud las btus pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs byung
22a2(dkar chag): chub kyi sems kun tu gzigs pa'i phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon ka la ka pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kri ka ra dang / lo rU ba 'gos lhas bcas kyi 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i lhan cig skyes pa'i de kho na nyid snang ba slob dpon
22a3(dkar chag): dpag med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra rak+Shi ta dang / mar pa chos dbang gi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i snying po'i de kho na nyid bsdus pa dang / lhan cig skyes pa'i de kho na nyid snang ba dang / dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i de kho na nyid kyi
22a4(dkar chag): man ngag dang gsum slob dpon ku sa li pas mdzad pa/ snga ma paN+Di ta ngag gi dbang phyug dang / phyi me gnyis paN+Di ta badz+ra bo d+hi dang / lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa gnyis su med pa'i man
22a5(dkar chag): ngag rnal 'byor gyi gtum mo slob dpon dge ba'i mgon pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta wA gI shwa ru dang / mAr pa chos dbang gi 'gyur/ lU i pa'i mngon par rtogs pa'i 'grel pa sdom pa 'byung ba zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta de bzhin ga
22a6(dkar chag): pa rdo rjes mdzod pa/ de'i 'grel pa khyad par gsal byed/ bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga gnyis de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bi b+hu ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga yid 'ong phreng
22b1(dkar chag): ba zhes bya ba slob dpon dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga mnyes pa'i snying po zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bde mchog gi man ngag ye shes 'byung ba zhes bya ba ka ya s+tha ba ga ya
22b2(dkar chag): d+ha ras mdzad pa/ de nyid dang / lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ bde mchog sdom 'byung gi sgrub thabs/ paN+Di tak+ShAn+ti shrI dang / lo tsA ba shong blo brtan gyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / pheM ba la mkha' 'gro
22b3(dkar chag): rgya mtsho'i sgrub thabs rin po che pad+ma rA ga'i gter zhes bya ba/ slob dpon dza ya se nAs mdzad pa/ d+harma yon tan gyi 'gyur/ rkang pa bzhi bcu rtsa brgyad pa'i bstod pa/ paN+Di ta dza ya se nA dang / d+harma yon tan gyi 'gyur/ mkha' 'gro/
22b4(dkar chag): rgya mtsho'i gtor cho ga rin po che oMsma gar+b+ha dang / maN+Dal gyi cho ga rin po che mar ga ta dang / dbang bskur ba'i cho ga rin po che dbang gi rgyal po dang / sbyin sreg gi cho ga rin po che me shel dang bzhi dza ya se nAs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid
22b5(dkar chag): dang / lo tsA ba ye shes rdo rje'i 'gyur/ rang byin gyis brlab pa'i man ngag gi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ slob dpon ku mA ra shrIs mdzad pa/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i man ngag zhal nas snyan du brgyud pa yid bzhin gyi nor bu zhes bya ba
22b6(dkar chag): mar ba chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi bstod pa shukla ka la shas mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba bsod nams bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs la bstod pa bram ze rin chen
23a1(dkar chag): rdo rjes mdzad pa/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i bstod pa bram ze rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma hA dza na dang / lo tsA ba myur pa chos dbang gi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i bstod pa slob dpon mai tri bsdu mdzad pa/
23a2(dkar chag): bde mchog gi rgyun bshags rgyas pa slob dpon b+hu ri pas mdzad pa/ dzaM bo rje dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog gi dkyil cho ga rgyal po'i sras dpal 'jigs byed lha'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba
23a3(dkar chag): grags 'byor shes rab kyi 'gyur/ dbang bskur ba'i rim pa'i cho ga paN+Di ta bde ba'i rgyal pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pA ra he ta dang / lo ts+tsha ba nag tsho shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di
23a4(dkar chag): ta ma nA ka shrIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA su ma ti kIrti deng / lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga paN+Di ta d+harma shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba rig pa gzhon nu'i 'gyur/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog 'i byung ba zhes bya
23a5(dkar chag): ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga/ slob dpon dbu ba blo ldan gyis mdzad pa/ lhan cig skyes pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba mkhas pa chen po dz+nyA na shrIs mdzad cing / pho brang zhi ba 'od kyis bsgyur ba/ slob dpon nag po
23a6(dkar chag): pas mdzad pa'i sgron ma bzhi'i 'grel pa paN+Di ta shrI d+ha ra nyid kyis mdzad cing bsgyur ba'o// de ltar bde mchog yab bka'i skor rnams bkod nas/ yum gtso bor gyur pa'i skor la/ dpal rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rgyal po seng ge'i gdan can
23b1(dkar chag): khyab 'jug sbas pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta 'jigs med lha dang / lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ grub pa'i rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs/ rgyal po in+d+ra b+hu d+his mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nA len+d+ra pa dang / lo tsA ba shes rab glags kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal
23b2(dkar chag): 'byor ma'i sngags kyi de kho na nyid nges par bstan pa/ rgyal po in+d+ra b+hu d+hi chen pos mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba ye shes rdo rje'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor mo'i sgrub thab sa lcam lak+Sh+mI ka ras mdzad pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma dmar mo sgrub thabs ri khrod dbang phyugs mdzad pa/ rdo rje myor ma dkar mo'i sgrub
23b3(dkar chag): thabs in+d+ra b+hu d+his mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bai ro tsa na'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs zhal gnyis ma chung ba ri khrod dbang phyug gi mdzad par grags pa paN+Di ta bsod nams 'byung gnas bzang po dang / lo tsA ba rma ba na chos 'bar gyi
23b4(dkar chag): 'gyur/ phag mo'i sgrub thabs de kho na nyid ye shes yang dag par grub pa zhes bya ba zhal gnyis ma che bar grags pa paN+Di ta stong nyid ting nge 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta b+ha ren+d+ha ru tsi dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ don grub
23b5(dkar chag): ma chung ba'i sgrub thab sa slob dpon a wa d+hu tI pas mdzad pa dang / don grub ma che ba'i sgrub thabs ye shes dbab pa zhes bya ba dpal stong nyid ting nge 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ di bu bcad ma chung ba'i sgrub thabs lha mo dpal gyi blo gros
23b6(dkar chag): mas mdzad pa dang gsum/ paN+Di ta b+ha ren+d+ha ru tse dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ dbu bcad ma'i sgrub thabs che ba zhes bya ba dpal birba pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta b+ha ren+d+ha ru tse dang / lo tsA ba rma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje
24a1(dkar chag): rnal 'byor ma'i gsang ba sbyin sreg gi cho ga/ sangs rgyas byin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta b+ha ren+d+ha ru tse dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ gzhung drug sbyin sreg dang bcas pa 'di dag bong na grags pa'i
24a2(dkar chag): rim pa ltar bkod pa'o// rigs ldan ma'i de kho na nyid nges pa zhes bya ba o D+yan du grub pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dI pa ka ra shrI dz+nyA na'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma mchod pa'i cho ga/ phag mo rus sbrul zhabs kyi sgrub thabs grub thob shwa
24a3(dkar chag): papa ri pas mdzad pa dang / de'i man ngag phag mo thugs kyi sgrub pa dang gnyis/ paN+Di ta A nan+da ka ra dang / lo tsA ba dpyal chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ mkha'i spyod ma dmar mo'i sgrub thabs/ grub thob rngon pa pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta niH
24a4(dkar chag): laM ka dang / dpyal chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byorar ma'i gzhan don slob ma rjes su bzung ba'i cho ga dang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i dbang mdor bsdus pa dang / rdo rje pheg mo'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga dang gsum grub thob
24a5(dkar chag): sha ba ri dbang phyug gis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta gau taM shrI dang / lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ zhal gnyis ma chung ba'i 'grel po rnal 'byor gyi rjes su 'bring ba zhes bya ba grub thob dA ri ka pas mdzad pa dang / paN+Di ta klu'i sbyin pa'i
24a6(dkar chag): rnal 'byor gyi snying po'i don bsdus bstan pa dang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i man ngag slob dpon dA ri ka pas mdzad pa dang gsum/ paN+Di ta dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma keng rus ta ra Na zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon
24b1(dkar chag): dA ri ka pas mdzad pa dang / de'i 'grel pa ku mA ra bo d+his mdzad pa dang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dza lan+d+ha ra pas mdzad pa/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa'i phag mo'i sgrub thabs dang / oM D+ya Na nas byung ba'i phag
24b2(dkar chag): mo'i sgrub thabs gnyis/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ phag mo dkar mo'i sgrub thabs kong+ga sbyin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba ba ri cho sa grags kyi 'gyur/ phag mo dkar mo'i
24b3(dkar chag): bstod pa slob dpon kong+ga sbyin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rat+na rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba zhang grub pa dpal gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i bzhed pa'i sbas pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga/ slob dpon kong+ka byin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA pa la hu'u dang / ba ri rin
24b4(dkar chag): chen grags kyi 'gyur/ rdo dz+haiM rnal 'byor ma'i dgongs pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon kong+ga byin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / lo tsA ba mtshur dz+nyA na A ka ra'i 'gyur/ phag mo'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg gcig 'di bod ma 'dra'o//
24b5(dkar chag): rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon shes rab bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba mar pa chos dbang gi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rig pa 'dzin pa gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta phyag na rdo rje dang /
24b6(dkar chag): lo tsA ba mtshur gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma mchod pa la sogs pa mdor bsdus pa'i man ngag/ paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Nis mdzad pa/ de nyid dang lo tsA ba mtshur gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs kyi cho ga don thams cad grub pa
25a1(dkar chag): zhes bya ba/ slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i lus dang po pa'i sgom pa mdor bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ baN+Di ta su ma ti kIN+Di
25a2(dkar chag): dang / lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ 'di nA ro mkha' spyod kyi gzhung yin/ gzhan don slob ma rjes su bzung ba'i cho ga/ paN+Di ta wA gI shwa ra b+ha ren+du ru tses mdzad pa de nyid dang / ye shi sa rdo rje'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i
25a3(dkar chag): sgrub thabs lha sum cu so bdun ma dang / de'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga gnyis shrI dbu ma pa ti tat+tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta wA gI shwa ra gup+ta dang / lo tsA ba rA chos rab kyi 'gyur/ phag mo'i mngon par rtogs pa'i snye ma zhes bya ba paN+Di
25a4(dkar chag): te dge ba'i 'byung gnas sbas pa zhes bya bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dA la shI lnga'i rang 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i bde ba mchog gi sdom pa la 'jug pa nges pa dron gyi dkyil 'khor zhes bya ba/ slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes
25a5(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na'i rang 'gyur/ de kho na nyid yang dag par grub pa'i rgya cher 'grel pa de kho na nyid bshad pa zhes bya ba/ paN+Di tA brtson 'grus dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di tau many+dzu shrI dang / dze ta kar+Na dang / lo tsA
25a6(dkar chag): ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma phag mo khros pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzod pa/ paN+Di ta bud d+ha shrI dz+nyA na dang / gnubs lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi l-i gyur/ mkha' spyod dkar mo'i
25b1(dkar chag): bstod pa jo bo rjes mdzad pa de nyid dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ mai tI mkha' spyod kyi rjes gnang gi cho ga/ gzhan don slob ma rjes su bzung ba'i cho ga gnyis dza ya se nAs mdzad pa/ phag mo dmar chung ma'i sgrub thabs
25b2(dkar chag): sa raM ha pas mdzad pa/ phag mo rin chen rgyun gyi sgrub thabs jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rdo brjes mdzad pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs paN+Di tA dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang / rgya brtson seng gi
25b3(dkar chag): 'gyur/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i bstod pa paN+Di ta dI bo kaM ra shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa de nyid dang / lo tsA ba khu na tso'i 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo mdor bsdus po'i bstod paM paN+Di ta drug gi dbang phyug dang / klog skya lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ ye shes dbab pa'i
25b4(dkar chag): cho ga/ dpal rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i dgongs pa'i gsang ba sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon a b+hi yuk+Shas mdzad pa/ gzhan yang a b+hi yuk+ti sa mdzad zer ba'i phag mo'i las tshogs/ lag mchod rnams bzhugs so// lag mchod rnam
25b5(dkar chag): ni the tshom gyi gzhir snang ngo // bde mchog 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel nyi shu lnga// yab skor gtso bo brgya phrag gcig dang lnga// yum gyi skor la lnga bcu rtsa dgu ste// gril bas brgya dang brgyad cu rtsa brgyad bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur/
25b6(dkar chag): cog gi dkar chag sring zho'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/ bde mchog gi skor te le'u gnyis pa'o// / ba pa la rgyud sde lnga pa kye rdo rje'i rgyud kyi skor la/ kye rdo rje'i 'grel pa byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje snying pos
26a1(dkar chag): mdzad pa'i le'u lnga pa yan chad paN+Di ta d+hA na shI la dang / lo ts+tsha ba 'bro seng dkar shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta su b+hU ti shrI shUn+ti dang / lo nI bA tsog gru ting nge 'dzin bzang pos zhus te gtan la phabyA pa las
26a2(dkar chag): slad kyi paN+Di ta 'jigs med lha dang / lo tsA ba snyil cor shes rab glags kyi 'gyur/ dbang blo gros brtan pas bcos pa dang / le'u drug pa man chung 'bro'i 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i dka' 'grel pad+ma can zhes bya ba/ slob dpon mtsho skyes
26a3(dkar chag): kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta k+Shi ti gar+b+ha dang / lo tsA ba khu ston dngos grub kyi 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i rnam 'grel slob dpon b+ha ba b+ha Tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pu N+ye kIrti dang / lo tsA ba se rtsa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur rnams bzhugaso//
26a4(dkar chag): ma pa la dgyes pa rdo rje'i dka' 'grel rnal 'byor rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba brtul zhugs spyod pa nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kr-iSh+Na pa dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ brtag gnyis kyi 'grel pa kha sbyor shin tu
26a5(dkar chag): drim med pa zhes bya ba slob dpon nAd+hA da shras+t+ra mdzad pa paN+Di ta bi ma la shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA bo shong blo brtan gyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / tsa pA la kye rdo rje'i 'gyel pa ku mu ti slob dpon mi thu ba zla bas
26a6(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje'i 'grel pa rdo rje tshig gi snying po bsdus pa zhes bya ba dpal nA ro pas mdzad pa/ kha cha shAkya shrI dang / dpyal chos bzang gi 'gyur la/ dbang blo brtan gyis bcos pa/ kye rdo rje'i dka' 'grel dran pa'i
26b1(dkar chag): 'byung gnas zhes bya ba/ slob dpon nag po pa chung bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dpal ldan zla ba dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lhas bcas kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje'i 'grel pa slob dpon pad+ma'i myu gu rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pad+ma A ka ra dang /
26b2(dkar chag): lotsA ba mtshur dbyig gi rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i 'grol ba mu tig phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon rat+na A ka ra shAn+ti pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAn+ti b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dgyes pa
26b3(dkar chag): rdo rje'i dka' 'grel spyan 'byed ces bya ba/ d+harma kIrtis mdzad zer ba rnams bzhugs so// 'di rgya gar ma min par 'dug ste/ sbyar gyi rnams kyis kyang bris pa'i stabs kyis bris zin 'dug pas 'dir bzhugs su bcug pa
26b4(dkar chag): yin no// tsha gong ma la kye rdo rje'i 'grel pa rab tu gsal ba'i kha sbyor zhes bya ba slob dpon kA ya s+tha bgres pos mdzad pa/ glan dar ma blo glos kyi 'gyur/ tsha 'og ma la dgyes pa rdo rje'i dka' 'grel rdo rje'i
26b5(dkar chag): tshig btu ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon kA ma d+he nus mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi nA ya de ba dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi don bsdus pa gsham cung ma tshang ba gcig/ 'dir dgyes rdor
26b6(dkar chag): gyi 'grel pa nA ro pa'i gsung gi 'od zer las skyes pa/ zhes bya ba ni rdzun mar snang bas ma bris so// thun mong ma yin pa'i bshad rgyud rdo rje gur gyi dka' 'grel zhal nas brgyud pa zhes bya ba/ rgyal po in+d+ra b+hu d+his
27a1(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nyi ma sbas pa dang / lo tsA ba shAkya brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/ gur brtag pa dang po'i bshad sbyar slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA gA ya d+hA ra dang / lo tsA ba 'brog mi shA
27a2(dkar chag): ye shes kyi 'gyur/ gur gyi dka' 'grel de kho na nyid rgyas pa zhes bya ba/ lha'i rigs kyi blo gros chen pos mdzad pa/ ga ya d+ha ra dang / 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dgyes rdor bde mchog la sogs rgyud sde mang po'i thun mong
27a3(dkar chag): gi bshad rgyud dpal sam+bu Ti'i 'grel pa la/ slob dpon in+d+ra b+hU taus mdzad pa'i yang dag pa'i lta ba'i dran pa'i snang ba zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta shrI badz+ra bo d+hi dang / lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so//
27a4(dkar chag): dza pa la sam+ma Ti'i 'grel pa man ngag gi snye ma zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa/ sh+lo ka stong phrag brgyad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / rtswa mi sangs rgyas grags kyi 'gyur la/ kha che ba Na chen dang / dpyal chos
27a5(dkar chag): bzang gis bcos pa la/ dbang lo tsA ba blo brtan gyis dag par bcos pa bzhugs so// / wa pa laM sam+bu Ti'i rgya cher bshad pa rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/
27a6(dkar chag): kye'i rdo rje'i rgyud phyi ma phyag rgya chen po thig le'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa zab pa'i don gsal ba rmad du byung ba zhes bya ba o D+yaH gyi slob dpon zab pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shes rab gsong ba dang / mo tsA ba g.yung drung snying po'i 'gyur
27b1(dkar chag): phyag rgya chen po thig le'i 'grel pa dga' ba'i spyan zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta shes rab gsang bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA bA rin chen rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ ye shes thig le'i rgyud kyi le'u nyi shu rtsa gsum pa yan chad kyi 'grel
27b2(dkar chag): po dpal rang bzhin dga' ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba'i dka' 'grel/ slob dpon rdo rje gsang bas mdzad pa/ shes rab gsal ba'i rang 'gyur/ ye shes thig le'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel gsang ba'i de kho na nyid ces bya ba slob dpon dz+nyA na
27b3(dkar chag): pa ra ma yis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba byang chub 'byung gnas kyi 'gyur/ rnyog pa med pa'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel slob dpon gzhon nu zla bas mdzad pa dang / de kho na nyid kyi rgyud kyi dka' 'grel rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon ma hA su kha ta
27b4(dkar chag): badz+ra sa mdzad pa de nyid dang / lo tsA ba byang chub 'byung gnas kyis bsgyur ba/ 'grel chung phran brgyad la/ dgongs pa'i skad kyi 'grel pa slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta many+dzu g+ho Sha dang / shes rab grags kyi
27b5(dkar chag): 'gyur/ glu'i de kho na nyid ces bya ba rdo rje glu'i 'grel pa slob dbo na mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rat+na badz+ra dang lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje'i glu bshad pa zhes bya ba slob dpon sgron ma can gyi sdes mdzad pa/
27b6(dkar chag): paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ mngon par rtogs pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba dang / kye'i rdo rje'i de kho na nyid rnam par phye ba dang / bshad rgyud kha sbyor dang / rdo rje mkha' 'gro las rtsa'i skabs bshad pa ste/ rtsa'i
28a1(dkar chag): 'grel pa gnyis paN+Di ta rat+na badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ dur khrod kyi bshad pa gnyis rat+na shrI mi tru dang / shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ brdanges par bzung ba mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal
28a2(dkar chag): mtshan gyis bsgyur ba dang brgyad do// yang slob dpon rnal 'byor pas mdzad pa'i dur khrod brgyad kyi bshad pa/ paN+Di ta bud+d+ha ka ra badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dpal rin po che snye ma zhes bya ba'i rgya cher 'grel pa zhes
28a3(dkar chag): bya ba/ rgya gar gyi slob dpon chen po shrI gup+ta'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ de nyid kyi rang 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// de ltar rgyud so so'i dgongs 'grel rnams bkod nas spyi'i dgongs 'grel sgrub thabs dkyil cho ga lam rim la sogs
28a4(dkar chag): pa'i skor la// / zha pa la dgyes pa rdo rje lha dgu'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon mtsho skyes kyis mdzad pa/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa leng shAkya brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/
28a5(dkar chag): slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa'i mar me'i rtse mo lta bu'i man ngag/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / 'brog mi shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje'i bstod pa dang sbyin sreg gi/
28a6(dkar chag): cho ga slob dpon mo tshe skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa/ dam tshig lnga pa pad+ma 'byung gnas kyis mdzad pa/ ba ri chos grags kyi 'gyur/ dpal kye rdo rje la b+ha dra rA ga'i bstod pa/ slob dpon pad+ma badz+ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba shAkya
28b1(dkar chag): ye shes kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs slob dpon byang chub snying pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dI
28b2(dkar chag): paM ka ra rA dza dang / lha mu ne btsan po'i 'gyur/ slob dpon byang chub snying pos mdzad pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga/ slob dpon DoM bi he ru kas mdzad pa'i de kho na nyid bcu pa/ jo bo rje dang dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ r-I bi he ru kas mdzad
28b3(dkar chag): pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i 'du ba bsgrag pa/ pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na'i rang 'gyur/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga DoM bi he ru kas mdzad pa paN+Di ta dz+nyA na A kA ra dang / lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ kye rdo rje lha dgu'i sgrub thabs/
28b4(dkar chag): DoM bi pas mdzad pa paN+Di tA nags kyi rin chen dang / rtsis thang lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa kha che dngul gyi bum+b+ha pas mdzad pa paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang / rtses thang lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub
28b5(dkar chag): thabs rab tu gsal ba zhes bya ba sgra gcan gsang bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang / rtses thang lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ DoM bi pa'i slongs mo'i 'grel pa/ paN+Di ta dze ta kar+Na dang / lo tsA bA nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal
28b6(dkar chag): bzang po'i 'gyur/ dpal he ru ka phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon a la la badz+ras mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje'i dran pa gcig pa'i man ngag slob dpon gar+b+ha ri bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA in+d+ra ru tsaM dang / lo tsA ba 'brog ma
29a1(dkar chag): shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa dag pa rdo rje sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon dza lan+d+ha ri pAs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta many+dzu shrI dang / lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal
29a2(dkar chag): mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs yan lag drug pa zhes bya ba slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rat+na shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba shAkya ye sheHsa kyi 'gyur/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i sgrub thabs bzang po
29a3(dkar chag): yongasu bzung ba zhes bya ba slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa dang / 'byung po thams cad pa'i gtor chog mi thub zla bas mdzad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / 'brog mi shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ de kho na nyid bzhi'i man ngag
29a4(dkar chag): gsal ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/ tai lo bas mdzad pa rat+na shrI'i rang 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs kyi rgyal po slob dpon a wa d+hU tI pa gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs 'khrul pa spong ba zhes bya ba slob dpon rin chen
29a5(dkar chag): 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzod pa dang / lhan cig skyes pa'i dga' ba yang dag par sbyor ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ dpal rab 'byor zhi ba dang / lo tsA ba ting nge 'dzin bzang po'i 'gyur dang / lhan
29a6(dkar chag): cig skyes pa'i rnal 'byor gyi rim pa ku mA rA ka lo shu'i rang 'gyur gnyis 'gyur tho dad pa ma gtogs pa chos gcig tu 'dug pas phyi ma bzhugs/ de'i 'grel pa 'byur mi ma da khyi mo ma zhing marjong bram ze tha ga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di
29b1(dkar chag): man+ta kA lA bu'i rang 'gyur/ k+She rdo rje'i sgrub thabs rnam par dag pa'i gter zhes bya ba a wa d+hU tI gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang / rtses thang lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ slob dpon kam+ba las mdzad pa'i dgyes
29b2(dkar chag): pardo rje'i sgrub thabs de kho na nyid bzhi 'i rim pa zhes bya ba paN+Di ta bai ro tsa nA rak+Shi ta dang / glu nyin dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ he ru ka zhal gcig pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon yan lag med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA badz+ra pA Ni/
29b3(dkar chag): dang le tsA ba rma ban chos 'bur gyi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i sgrub thabs slob dpon bde ba'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma tsan+d+ra dang / lo ts+tsha ba d+harma tsan+d+ra'i'i gyur/ dpal kye'i rdo rje'i bya ba'i rim pa rin chen 'bar ba zhes bya ba'i sgrub
29b4(dkar chag): thabs slob dpon pradz+nyA in+d+ra ru tses mdzad pa/ de nyid dang shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ bAN+Di ta de nyid dang / 'gros lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ slob de pon
29b5(dkar chag): nag po pas mdzad pa'i dgyes pa rdo rje'i sgrub thabs de kho na nyid gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba/ paN+Di tA de nyid dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i gzhung 'grel gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga zhes bya ba/ slob
29b6(dkar chag): dpon nag po pas mdzad pa dang / ro sreg gi cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa gnyis paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba 'gas lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra
