30a1(dkar chag): dang / lo tsA ba 'gros kyi 'gyur/ rab gnas kyi cho ga'i tshul slob dpon nag po byas mdzad pa dang / tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i rim pa slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa gnyis paN+Di tA de nyid dang /
30a2(dkar chag): lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i mchod rten gyi cho ga dang / gshin gyi cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dze ta kar+Na dang / lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ dgyes rdor gyi dkyil cho ga he ru
30a3(dkar chag): ka 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon nyin mo'i 'byung gnas zla ba'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ dpal he ru ka'i man ngag rang byin gyis brlab pa zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ti stong nyid ting 'dzin rdo rjes mdzad pa/
30a4(dkar chag): de nyid dang / lo tsA ba shes rab ye shes dang / sa rtsa bstod nams rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ he ru k+Sha 'byung ba zhes bya ba kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon skyong nyid rdo rjes mdzad pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po pur+Na kIr+t+ti
30a5(dkar chag): dang lo tsA ba s+thA nA me rdo rje bla ma'i 'gyur/ kye rdo rje phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs slob dponA d+hA ra b+h+rUMs mdzad pa/ podz+yo ti su me to kIr+t+ti dang / lo tsA ba mar ba chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i dbang gtan la
30a6(dkar chag): dbab pa slob dpon dzi ta ri pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ dzi ta ris mdzad pa'i gur nas gsungs pa'i khro bo bcu'i rig pa'i cho ga/ paN+Di ta tri ta kar+Na dang / mo ts+tsha ba
30b1(dkar chag): nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal dbang po'i 'gyur/ sgrub thob binA pas mad+hA pa'i gsang ba'i dang dang / dang rkyen po'i rim pa gsum pa dang gnyis/ dgyes pa rdo rje phyug gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Dit+tasgyu ma tI hrIH
30b2(dkar chag): dradra dang / lo tsA ba shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ gsung bsdus pa dgyes pa rdo rje'i sgrub thabs kyang zer/ dpal kye rdo rje'i mngon par rtogs pa'i thig le rnam par grags pa'i mkhas pa gnas brtan shAkya srung ba'i zhabs
30b3(dkar chag): kyis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba skyob pa dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ chos spyod mdor bsdus pa'i bya ba dang / sats+tsha gdab pa'i cho ga 'di gnyis rgya gar ma yin min the tshom za'o// bung ba 'dod pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon rat+na tsan+d+ras
30b4(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / khu dngos grub kyi 'gyur/ gtor ma'i de nyid bsdus pa slob dpon d+harma pA las mdzad pa/ ro sreg pa'i cho ga/ slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad snga mdzang pa/ 'dir bod rgya ston zhes bya bas
30b5(dkar chag): bris pa'i tshogs 'khor ni bod ma yin pas ma bris so// mdzad pa po'i mtshani mA smos pa la/ dpa' bo gcig pa phyag bcu drug pa he ru ka'i sgrub thabs/ kye rdo rje'i spyan dbye ba'i cho ga/ sAts+tsha bya thabs gtor ma'i cho ga
30b6(dkar chag): tshe chung bzhi/ phyag mtshan gyi phan yon rnams la mdzad byang 'gyur byang mi snang zhing / the tshom gyi gzhi'o// thig mo chen po zhes bya ba'i rdzog mi rim paN+Di ta sgege pa rdo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ dpal kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs mngon
31a1(dkar chag): par rtogs pa'i rim pa don rab tu gsal ba zhes bya ba/ dgyes pa rdo rje sems dpa' gsum gyi sgrub thabs nA ro pa'i zhal gyi lung dang sbyar ba/ de kho na nyid kyi snang ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems
31a2(dkar chag): dpas mdzad zer ba 'di brdzun mar 'dug ste/ paN+Di tas bshad 'dug pas bzhugs su bcug pa yin no// kye rdo rje'i lag tu blang po'i rim pa zhes bya ba se rtsa bsod na mos rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ 'di so rtsa bsod nams rgyal
31a3(dkar chag): mtshan gyis brtsams pa yin pa 'dra ste/ sngar gyi rnams kyis bris 'dug pas bris so// dgyes pa rdo rje'i gtor ma'i cho ga jo bo rjes mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so// // za ba la kye'i rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor
31a4(dkar chag): gyi rim pa slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i sgrub thabs slob dpon yan lag med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kun tu bzang po dang / lo tsA ba
31a5(dkar chag): tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon sa ha dza ba lis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta b+ha ren+d+ha ru tse dang / lo tsA ba rma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ man ngag rim pa gsum pa zhes bya
31a6(dkar chag): ba slob dpon Do bi he ru kas mdzad pa/ go bar byed pa'i snying po brgya pa'i ming / slob dpon snang ba mtha' yas rdo rjes mdzad pa/ dpal dgyes pa rdo rje'i sgrub thabs rin chen sgron ma zhes bya ba dpal mar me mdzad ye shes
31b1(dkar chag): kyis mdzad pa/ baN+Di ta d+hA nA shrI dang / lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ dbang bskur ba'i cho ga slob dpon chen po pradz+nyA shris mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga/ mkha' 'gro ma ne gus mdzad pa mkha' 'gro ma de nyid
31b2(dkar chag): dngadang lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ dpal brtse ba'i rdo rje phyag bcu drug pa'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta kr-iSh+Na bas mdzad pa/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i gtor ma'i cho ga slob dpon a la la badz+ra sa mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba gyi jo
31b3(dkar chag): zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i gtor ma'i las kyi rim pa kho tsha rin tshe na rdo rjes mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje'i 'byung po thams cad pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga/ slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
31b4(dkar chag): po'i 'gyur/ kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs he ru ka mnyes par byed pa'i cho ga zhes bya ba slob dpon 'jam dpal ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ de nyid dang / rong zom chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ dgyes pa rdo rje lhan cig skyes pa'i sgrub thabs
31b5(dkar chag): slob dpon shrI A nan+da bi dz+ras mdzad pa/ sbyin sreg gi las kyi rim pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal gyi zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i bstod pa kha che rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di te ku mA ra ka lo sha dang / lo tsA ba
31b6(dkar chag): byang chub shes rab kyi 'gyur rnams so// de ltar yab skor rnams bkod nas/ yum gyi skor la/ slob dpon DoM bi he ru kas mdzad pa'i bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs bdud rtsi 'od kyi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba dang / bdag med ma'i sgrub
32a1(dkar chag): thabs mi thub zla bas mdzad pa dang gnyis/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+hA ra dang / lo tsA ba shAk+Sha ye shes kyi 'gyur/ bdag med lha mo bcoM lnga'i bskyod pa slob dpon myi thub zla bas mdzad pa/ slob dpon
32a2(dkar chag): gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa'i bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / mtshur A kA ra'i 'gyur/ bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs rgyas par bstan pa zhes bye ba slob dpon dkon mchog 'byung gnas kyis mdzad pa/
32a3(dkar chag): bdag med ma dpa' mo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs bskyed pa dang rdzogs par ldan pa zhes bya ba slob dpon bsod snyoms pa sgra ga can 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta prad+d+ha in+d+ra ru tse dang / lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ bdag
32a4(dkar chag): med ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ bdag med ma'i man ngag ces bya ba ting nge 'dzin rdo rje'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de ba A kA ra tsan+d+ra dang / mo tsA ba si rtsa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ bdag med
32a5(dkar chag): ma'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo'i sgrub thubs nA ro pa'i lung dang sbyar ba 'di the tshom gyi gzhi'o// lhan cig skyes pa'i rol pas mdzad pa'i bdag byin gyis brlab pa'i sgrub thabs dang / de'i man ngag paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang /
32a6(dkar chag): ba ri rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/ ku ru kul+le'i sgrub thabs slob dpon lhun skyes sgeg pas mdzad pa/ dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ ku ru kul+le'i man ngag chen po lnga slob pa pon zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa/ dA ni shI la'i rang 'gyur/
32b1(dkar chag): ku ru kul+le'i bstod pa DoM bi he ru kas mdzad pa/ ku ru kul+le'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta bi ma le dang / lo tsA ba gzhon nu 'od kyi 'gyur/ ku ru kul+le'i sgrub thabs o D+ya Na nas byung ba many+dzu shrI dz+nyA na dang / rong zom chos bzang gi 'gyur/
32b2(dkar chag): ku ru kul+le'i lha bcu gsum gyi sgrub thabs/ ku ru kul+le'i sgrub thabs slob dpon kr-i Da badz+ras mdzad pa rnams so// gur gyi skor la/ gur ri gas bsdus mkha' 'gro lnga'i sgrub thabs mi thub zla bas mdzad pa/ li la badz+ra
32b3(dkar chag): dang / sa rtsa bsod nams rgyal ma tshan gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje gur gyi sgrub thabs dkyil 'khor bsdus pa'i rjes su 'brang ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon lha'i brtul zhugs kyis mdzad pa mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ mkha' 'gro
32b4(dkar chag): ma rdo rje gur gyi man ngag de kho na nyid bcu pa zhes bya ba slob dpon dri med grags pas mdzad pa mer pa chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA na dang /
32b5(dkar chag): shAkya shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba chag dgra bcom gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs dmar po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs yang rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs slob depo ni dge ba'i mgon pos
32b6(dkar chag): mdzad pa pad+me tA bad+d+ha shrI dz+nyA nA dpag nubs byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ gur nas gsungs pa'i ro sreg gi cho ga/ slob dpon blo gros chen pos mdzad pa/ biN+Di ta a bi d+hU tI pa dang / ba dze l-i tsA ba'i 'gyur/ gur nas gsungs pa'i
33a1(dkar chag): ro sreg gi cho ga/ slob dpon ta thA gA ta rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ gur nas gsungs pa'i bla ma'i gdung bsreg pa'i cho ga/ paN+Di ta a shrI dz+nyA nA dang / lo tsA ba
33a2(dkar chag): dge slong dpal gyi snying po'i 'gyur/ phyag rgya chen po thig le'i skor la/ phyag rgya chen po thig le'i sgrub thabs rin po che char yang zhes bya ba'i shes rab gsang bas mdzad cing rang 'gyur du bsgyur ba/ rin chen thigs pa zhes
33a3(dkar chag): bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ shes rab gsang bas mdzad cing bsgyur ba/ dbang rin chen snang ba zhes bya ba/ dpal shes rab gsang bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba kaM chos kyi ye shes dang / phyugs mtshams dbang phyug
33a4(dkar chag): rgya mtsho'i 'gyur/ phyag chen thig le'i rgyud la brten pa tso'i ye shes mkha' 'gro'i sgrub thabs slob dpon longs spyod rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di to pradz+nyA shrI gup+ta dang / lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ sdig pa
33a5(dkar chag): thams cad 'dag pa'i me mchod kyi ting nge 'dzin zhes bya ba/ paN+Di tA rin chen rdo rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ dpal dga' ba'i me tog gi phreng ba zhes bya ba ye shes thig le'i rgyud kyi man ngag in+d+ra b+hU ti'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa dang /
33a6(dkar chag): des mdzad pa'i de kho na nyid bdud rtsi'i man ngag gnyis/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA shrI gup+ta dang / lo tsA ba rin chen rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ dbang rin chen phreng ba dang / dbang gi rim pa mdo ra bsdus pa/ rim pi lnga pa zhes bye ba/ yan lag
33b1(dkar chag): brgyad pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba rnams dpal shes rab gsang ba'i zhal snga nas mdzad cing de nyid kyi rang 'gyur/ rin po che'i 'od ces bya ba snying po de kho na nyid kyi sgrub thabs ye shes thig le'i man ngag/ shes rab gsang ba'i slob ma/
33b2(dkar chag): nA ro pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta badz+ra gu Na b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba rin chen rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ bde ba chen po bdud rtsi'i 'od ces bya ba dpal ye shes rin po ches mdzad pa/ byang sems thigs pa'i man ngag ces bya ba las kyi zhabs
33b3(dkar chag): kyis mdzad pa/ dpal gsang chen dga' ba'i thig le zhes bya ba dpal ma hA ma ti'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta A tsir+ya du lo pa dang / chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur rnams bzhugaso// kye rdo rje'i rgyud 'grel sum cu drug/ yab
33b4(dkar chag): sbyor gyi gnyis yum skor bcwo brgyad de// gur la bcu dang thig la gnyis bco lnga// gril bas brgya dang drug cu thom pa bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag srid zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/ dgyes pa
33b5(dkar chag): rdo rje'i sbyor te le'u gsum pa'o// / de ltar dgyes rdor gyi skor rnams bkod nas/ dpal gdan bzhi'i skor lnga/ dpal gdan bzhi pa'i 'grel pa/ dran pa'i rgyu mtshan zhes bya ba slob dpon b+ha ba b+ha Tas mdzad
33b6(dkar chag): pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra deng / mo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / 'a ba la dpal gdan bzhi'i rnam par bshad pa sbyor ba'i gdan yan chad slob dpon dag ba'i go chas mdzad pa/ de
34a1(dkar chag): man chad smr-i tis mdzad pa smr-i ti'i 'gyur/ dpal gdan bzhi'i man ngag mchan khung gi sbyor ba slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ dpal rdo rje gdan bzhi'i sgrub thabs slob dpon Ar+ya de bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di
34a2(dkar chag): ta ka ma la gup+ta dang / lo ts+tsha ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ dpal rdo rje gdan bzhi lha mang gi sgrub thabs bal po'i poN+Di ti dza ga ta A nan+ta dzI b+ha dras mdzad pa/ bod kyi lo tsA ba dpal ldan smra ba'i seng ge'i 'gyur/ gdan bzhi'i yum
34a3(dkar chag): skor ye shes dbang phyug ma'i sgrub thabs 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dz+nyA na kIrti'i rang 'gyur gdan bzhi'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga snying po mdor bsags pa zhes bya ba 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba
34a4(dkar chag): 'gos khug pa lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ gdan bzhi'i zab don ston pa shing gcig gi dka' 'grel slob dpon 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa/ rdo rje'i dril thabs kyi mchod pa'i rim pa 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa/ gdan bzhi'i sgrub thabs
34a5(dkar chag): b+ha ba b+ha Tas mdzad pa/ 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ chu'i sbyin sreg slob dpon b+ha ba b+ha Tas mdzad pa/ gzhon nu tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ gdan bzhi'i yum skor la/ ye shes mkha' 'gro ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon 'a jigs
34a6(dkar chag): med 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa/ sgra tshad pa rin chen rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ gdan bzhi'i sgrub thabs ye shes mkha' 'gro ma dang / rnal 'byor na mkha'i sgrub thabs bal po'i paN+Di ta rnam po ra rgyal ba'i dbang po'i sdes
34b1(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ gdan bzhi'i de kho na nyid bzhi pa slob dpon dzi ta ri bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ gdan bzhi'i de kho na nyid drug rnam par bzhag pa slob dpon smr-i ti dz+nyA na kIr+t+tis mdzad pa/ de nyid
34b2(dkar chag): kyi rang 'gyur rnams so// dpal ldan rdo rje gdanA bzhi'i rgyud 'grel gsum// yab yum sgrub thabs dkyil 'khor cho ga dang // rdzogs rim la sogs chos skor bcu gcig ste// gril bas bcu phrag gcig dang bzhi bzhugs so//
34b3(dkar chag): bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag srid zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las gdan po zhi'i sbyor te le'u bzhi pa'o// // sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i rgyud kyi sbyor la/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa/ sgyu ma
34b4(dkar chag): can zhes bya ba/ slob dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bde gshegs grags pa dang / lo tsA ba ye shes sems dpa'i 'gyur/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa yon tan po ldan pa zhes bya ba rin chen 'byung gnos
34b5(dkar chag): zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA zhi ba bzang po dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa dran pa zhes bya ba nag po rdo rjes ma dzad pa/ paN+Di ta dzI na wa ra dang / lo tsA ba 'gros lhas bcas kyi 'gyur/
34b6(dkar chag): sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel dpal rgyan pas mdzad pa/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i sgrub thabs yum rdo rje mkha' 'gro mas o D+yan gyi yul du byon nas gsungs pa/ paN+Di ta a wa d+hU tI dang / lo tsA ba shAkya brtson 'grus kyi
35a1(dkar chag): 'gyur/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i rgyud kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i he ru ka'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba dang / rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs/ shin tu spros pa med pa zhes bya ba dang / mahA mA ya'i sgrub thabs rmongs pa
35a2(dkar chag): sgrol ba'i brtag pa zhes bya ba rnams slob dpon ku ku ri pa sa mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta a nI la badz+rI dang / lo tsA bo 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga ku ku rI pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA n+yA bkroT
35a3(dkar chag): dang / 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha la bstod pa/ slob dpon ku ku ri pas zhal gzigs dus mdzad pa/ de kho na nyid kyi man ngag slob dpon blo bzang snying pos mdzad pa/ de'i ring 'grel
35a4(dkar chag): gnyis paN+Di ta ka ma la gup+tA dang / tshe nA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i sgrub thabs dpal rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dz+nyA na shrI b+hU drA dang / mo ts+tsha ba 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i
35a5(dkar chag): spangs rgyas mkha' 'gro mo'i sgrub thabs slob dper nag po pas mdzad pa/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rim pa gsal ba zhes bya ba nag po spyod pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta karma badz+ra dang / lo tsA bo gzhon nu tshul khrim/
35a6(dkar chag): kyi 'gyur/ 'di la dpe la lar ku ri bas mdang zer ba'ang 'dug/ spyi'i chos spyod slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ rigs lnga'i mkha' 'gro'o bstod pa/ rje btsun he ru ka 'khor dang bcas pa la bstod pa/ bdun tshigs kyi cho ga
35b1(dkar chag): chog slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ sAts+tsha gdab pa'i cho ga/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i rdzogs rim slob dpon chos kyi zhabs kyis zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA zhi ba bzang po dang / 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ sgyu 'phrul chen
35b2(dkar chag): mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta chen po zhi ba bzang po dang / lo ts+tsha ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga sbyin sreg dang bcas pa/ grub thob
35b3(dkar chag): dpal rgyan pas mdzad pa/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bla ma'i zhal snga'i man ngag ces bya ba slob dpon mkhas pa 'dul ba byin gyis mdzad pa/ he ru ka phyag rgya gcig po'i sgrub thabs/ ro sreg pa'i sgrub thabs
35b4(dkar chag): kyi cho ga/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta sku med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ sgyu ma chen mo'i sgrub thabs rnam par grol ba zhes pa dge slong d+harma shrI b+ha dra'i 'gyur bzhugs so// sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa bzhi/
35b5(dkar chag): sgrub thabs ro la sogs chos skor nyer gnyis te// gsang ba yid bde'i chos skor dri ma med// bcu phrag gnyis dang bcas pa'i drug bzhugs so// / bstan pa tsis 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag srid zhi'i
35b6(dkar chag): rkyen gcig ces bya ba las/ sgyu ma chen mo'i skor te le'u lnga pa'o// / ya ba la rdo rje bdud rtsi'i dka' 'grel slob dpon dri med bzang po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/
36a1(dkar chag): rdo rje badrud rtsi'i rgyud kyi shA shad bu slob dpon yon tan bzang po'i mdzad pa sgra ti'i 'gyur/ rdo na bdud rgyud kyi 'gres pa bdud rgyu 'jug pa zhes bya ba grub tho blu gos mdzad pa/ par+N+Na t+kAr pA la dang /
36a2(dkar chag): sgo tsA ba mchi mas yon tan 'bar gyi 'gyur la/ phyis padz+rI ti shrI la kA dz+nyA badz+ra dang / oM ts+tsha bklog skye shes rab ba rtsegs kyis bcoMswA pa gsum bzhugs s+ho// he ru ka dpal rdo rje bdud rtsi yi// rgyud kyi rgyal po'i rnam bshad dris
36a3(dkar chag): med/ mkhas grub rnams kyis mdzad pa rnam pa gsum// shin tu khyad par 'phags pa legs par bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag sring zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/ rdo rje bdud rtsi'i sgor te leru drug pa'o//
36a4(dkar chag): sangs rgyas thod pa'i sgor la/ sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel ye shes ldan pa zhes bya ba grub thob chen po sa ra ha'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba gyi rdo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ slob dpon
36a5(dkar chag): pad+ma badz+ras mdzad pa'i sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel de kho na nyid kyi zla ba zhes bya ba las le'u gnyis pa yan chad ji tsam rnyed pa dang / sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel mi 'jigs pa'i gzhung 'grel slob dpon
36a6(dkar chag): a b+ha lA ka ra gup+tas mdzad pa/ ding ri chos grags kyi 'gyur yin nam zer ba'i 'gyur rnying la dbang blo brtan gyis hor khong bsabs shing zhu chen mdzad pa/ bram ze chen po sa ra ha pas mdzad pa'i sangs rgyas thod pa lha nyi shu
36b1(dkar chag): rtsa lnga'i sgrub thabs/ 'byung po thams cad pa'i gtor chog/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rim pa gsal ba rnams paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / senaT gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ r-i gi ar mo'i sgrub thabs/ lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rin
36b2(dkar chag): chen grub kyi 'gyur rnams so// dpal ldan sangs rgyas thod pa zhes bya ba'i// rgyud kyi rgyal po'i rnam bshad rnam pa gsum// sgrub dkyil gtor cho ga ri gi'i sgrub thabs te// chos skor dri ma med pa bdun bzhugs so// bstan
36b3(dkar chag): bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag srid zhi'i rgyun gcig ces bya ba las/ sangs rgyas thod pa'i skor te le'u bdun pa'o// / sangs rgyas mnye ma sbyor gyi skor la/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi 'grel pa rgyud
36b4(dkar chag): kyi 'grel pa rgyud kyi don rnam par bshad pa zhes bya ba oD+ya Na gyi rgyal po dngos grub brnyes pa brgya byin sdong pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bid+yA ka ra sid+ha dang / lha rin po che'i 'gyur/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi 'grel pa sangs
36b5(dkar chag): rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi rgyan zhes bya ba slob dpon rab tu dga' ba'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rnams bzhugs s+ho// / ra pa la sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi rgyud kyi dka' 'grel slob dpon in+d+ra b+hU tIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA
36b6(dkar chag): sh+lod+d+ha ka ra warmo dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi rgyud ji snyed pa'i 'grel pa shes rab snang ba zhes bya ba sh+lo ka drug stong lnga brgya bdun cu pa slob dpon kun dga'i snying pos mdzad pa smr-i ti
37a1(dkar chag): dz+nyA na kIr+t+ti'i rang 'gyur/ 'di mnyam sbyor gyi rgyud phyi ma'i 'gyel par snang gi rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel pa min par snang ngo // sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi dka' 'grel slob dpon rab zhi bshes gnyen gyis
37a2(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha ka ra waM rma dang / d+harma shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA pa rin rje chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ slob dpo na ku ku rA dzas mdzad pa'i rdo rje sems dpa'i gsang don rnam par dgod pa dang / rnam par snang mdzad kyi gsang
37a3(dkar chag): don rnam par dgod pa dang / he ru ka'i gsang don rnam par dgod pa dang / pad+ma gar dbang gis gsang don rnam par dgod pa dang / rin chen nyi ma'i gsang don rnam par dgod pa dang / rta mchog rol pa'i gsang don rnam
37a4(dkar chag): par dgod pa dang drug/ paN+Di ta bid+yA ka ra sid+d+ha dang / lo tsA ba lha rin po che'i 'gyur/ dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi rjes su 'jug pa'i cho ga lnga pa slob dpon ku ku rA dzes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrI badz+ra ha sa dang / lo tsA ba rin chen
37a5(dkar chag): mchog gi 'gyur/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon ku ku rA dzAs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta gu len+d+ra gu dra dang / lo tsA ba dran pa na mkha'i 'gyur la lha rin po ches bcas pa/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor
37a6(dkar chag): gyi tshogs 'khor gyi cho ga rgyal po an+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta A nan+d+ra gan+d+ha da / mo tsA ba dran pa na mkha'i 'gyur lo rin po ches bcos pa/ he ru ka'i sgrub thabs slob dpon thu bo rA dza hastis mdzad pa dang /
37b1(dkar chag): ka'i sgrub thabs slob dpon hUM mdzad rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bIr+ya sid+d+ha dang / lha rin po che'i 'gyur/ yang de nyid rdo rje bzhad pa dang / rma rin chen mchog gi 'gyur dang gnyis/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi man ngag yan lag
37b2(dkar chag): bzhi don snang bar byed pa zhis bya ba slob dpon hUM mdzad grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rdo rje bzhad pa dang / rma rin chen mchog gi 'gyur/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi dkyil 'khor sgrub pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba slob dpon
37b3(dkar chag): hUM mdzad rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bid+yA ka ra sid+ha dang / lo tsA ba lha rin po che'i 'gyur/ khrag 'thung chen po'i sgrub thabs yang dag par grub pa zhes bya ba slob dpon hUM mdzad rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dong lo tsA ba gnu
37b4(dkar chag): na mkha'i snying po'i 'gyur/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga sems can thams cad la bskyed pa zhes bya ba kha che rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ye shes rdo rje dang / lo tsA ba gnyen bsod nams
37b5(dkar chag): kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs rgyal po in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa dang / bde ba chen po rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs dang / rdo rje sems dpa' rjes su dran pa'i cho ga slob dpon thu bo rA dzA hastis mdzad pa rnams
37b6(dkar chag): bzhugs so// sangs rgyas kun rdo nga mnyam por sbyor ba yi// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog rgyud 'grel lnga// sgrub tho bas la sogs chos skor bcu dgu ste// mnyam sbyor chos skor nyi shu rtsa bzhi bzhugs// bstan
38a1(dkar chag): bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag sring zhi'i rgyun gcig ces bya ba las/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi skor te le'u brgyad pa'o// / la ba la sgrol ma rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud ltar du
38a2(dkar chag): bshad pa la/ sgrol ma lha lnga'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad po/ paN+Di ta d+harma badz+rI dang / lo tsA ba dar ma rin chen gyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma spyi'i mngon par rtog pa zhes bya ba 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad bya/ lha mo sgro'i
38a3(dkar chag): ma phyag 'tshal nyi shu rtsa gcig ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa/ yang de'i so so'i sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa slob dpon nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta many+dzu shrI dang / lo tsA ba mal gyi
38a4(dkar chag): blo gros grags kyi 'gyur/ oT+Tan nas 'byung ba'i man ngag gi rim pa'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta nyi ma spras pas mdzad pa/ kha che paN+Da chen gyi phyag dpe las bsgyur ba/ slob dpon nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa'i phyag 'tshal
38a5(dkar chag): nyi shu rtsa gcig ma'i sgrub thabs/ kha che pA Na chen shAkya shrI dang / lo tsA be byams paM'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa rnam ngag gtsug gi nor bu zhes bya ba slo ba dpon nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa/ rgya brtson 'grus seng ge'i
38a6(dkar chag): 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i po stong pa slob dpon nyi ma sbas pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sA d+hu kIrti dang / lo tsA ba ldan ma tshul khrims seng ge'i 'gyur/ lha mo dam tshig sgrol ma'i bstod pa/ sgrol ma me tog phreng 'dzin gyi bstod pa slob dpon
38b1(dkar chag): thams cang mkhyen+d+ra pa'i ba shes gnyen gyis mdzad bya sdu 'gyur/ spyil ma me tog phyung 'dzin gyi bstod pa slob dpon thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Dita ka na ka wa ma dang / so tsAb pa chab nyim grags tu
38b2(dkar chag): 'gyur la/ slad kyi paN+Di ta ma Ni ka shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyis bcos pa/ me tog phreng 'dzin tsheg par bdun mar bcas pa/ paN+Di ta zla ba gzhon nu'i rang 'gyur/ lha mo sgrol ma la smre sngags kyi gsol 'debs kyis
38b3(dkar chag): bstod pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ slob dpon de bzhin gshegs pa'i srung bas mdzad pa'i phreng 'dzin lha
38b4(dkar chag): lnga'i spyi sgrub/ so so'i sgrub thabs la/ sgrol mo dkar mo la brten nas stong nyid bsgom pa/ sngon mo la brtan nas lta ba ngan pa sun dbyung ba/ ser mo la brten nas chom rkun bcing ba/ dmar mo la brten nas shes rab bskyed
38b5(dkar chag): pa/ ljang ser la brten nas 'chi ba blu ba dang drug/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i srung byas mdzad cing / paN+Di tA de nyid dang / lo ts+tsha ba cog gru mya ngan med pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'dir sgrub thabs rnams bla med du bkral 'dug pas/
38b6(dkar chag): bstod pa me tog phreng 'dzin yang bla med du bkod // lha mo sgrol ma la bstod pa don thams cad grub pa zhes bya ba slob dpon ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa/ 'di gur gyi rdo rje sgrol ma dang cha mthun par byas 'dug pas bla med du
39a1(dkar chag): bkod ngo do// sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rim pa'i sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta ma hA dza na dang / lo tsA ba gzhon nu 'od kyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i dkyil 'khor lha bcu'i sgrub pa'i thabs slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i rol
39a2(dkar chag): pas mdzad pa/ 'brog mi lo tsA'i 'gyur// oM T+TAN+Da sgrol ma'i skor la/ 'phags ma gnas kyi dbang phyug ma'i sgrub thabs/ mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje ldan mas gsungs pa/ paN+Di tA saM g+ha me shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba 'jam dpal sgeg pa'i
39a3(dkar chag): rdo rje'i 'gyur/ on+ya Na sgrol ma'i mngon rtogs kyi rim pa zhes bya ba dang / oM r+yA Na sgrol ma'i rim pa gsang ba las kyang ches gsang ba zhes bya ba dang / oM D+ya Na sgrol ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba'i cho ga mdor bsdus pa paN+Di
39a4(dkar chag): ta bA ra he tas mdzad pa rnams/ paN+Di ta saM g+ha ma shrI dang / lo tsA bo 'jam dpal sgeg pa'i rdo rje'i 'gyur/ sgrol ma dpa' mo gcig ma'i rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs dang / o D+ya Na sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje ldan mas
39a5(dkar chag): gsungs pa gnyis paN+Di ta pA ra he ta dang / lo tsA ba nag tsho shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ 'di sngar gyi dang 'gyur la mi 'dra ba'i khyad chen po 'dug pas bris/ gtor ma'i cho ga nyung ngu dang / zhing gi dbang phyug ma'i mchod pa'i
39a6(dkar chag): rim pa/ paN+Di ta pA ra ho ta dang / lo tsA ba nag tshe shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ de kho na nyid kyi tshig le'ur byas pa'i man ngag dang / de'i 'grel pa slob dpon su dza ya shrI b+ha dras mdzad pa gnyis/ ma hA mA ya'i rdzogs rim
39b1(dkar chag): de dang cha 'dra bar 'dug na'ang / nag tsho'i lugs la/ oM D+ya Na sgrol ma'i rdzogs rim du bzhed do// gnas chen brgyad kyi lha mo sgrol ma la bstod pa/ slob dpon mi bskyod rdo rjes mdzad pa ste/ gsum paN+Di ta pA ra he ta dang /
39b2(dkar chag): lo tsA ba nag tshe shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ zhing gi dbang phyug ma'i bstod pa blon po'i rigs shin tu dga' ba'i paN+Di tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ye shes rdo rje dang / lo tsA ba nag tsho chen po'i 'gyur/ rdo rje dril bu'i mtshan
39b3(dkar chag): nyid dang / thod pa mchod pa'i cho ga gnyis/ paN+Di ta pA ra he ta dang / lo tsA ba nag tsho shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ 'di o T+ya Na sgrol ma'i chos skor du mdzad do// rmi lam sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon zla ba'i bshes
39b4(dkar chag): gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ga ta shrI dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i 'chi kha ma'i man ngag pa Na chen shAkya shrIs mdzad pa/ de nyid dang lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'phags ma sgrol
39b5(dkar chag): ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs bsdus pa 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/
39b6(dkar chag): sgrol mi'i sgrub thabs kha che pa Na chen gyis mdzad pa/ dmyal pad+mo can gyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa paN+Di ta zla ba grags pas mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i bstod pa tshig rkang bcu gnyis pa/ sgrol ma u pra la khyim sa mdzo twa ra'i
40a1(dkar chag): sgrub thabs paN+Di tA nags kyi rin chen gyis mdzad pa paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes kyi 'gyur/ sgrol ma drag mo'i sgrub thabs rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen
40a2(dkar chag): dang chos 'khor lo tsA'i 'gyur/ ral gcig ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i gtor cho ga bsdus pa/ sgrol ma ral gcig ma'i blo 'phel rtag pa rdo rjes mdzad pa gsum/ dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/
40a3(dkar chag): ral gcig ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon rol pa'i sbas pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ ral gcig mi dmar mo'i sgrub thabs kun spangs rdo rje zhes bya bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta mi dbang bzang po dang / legs
40a4(dkar chag): pa'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ ral gcig ma dmar mo'i byin rlabs kyi cho ga nag po spyod pa pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta myi dbang bzang po dang / gzhon nu shes rab kyi 'gyur/ mchog gi sgrol ma ral gcig ma'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta dA na
40a5(dkar chag): shI la dang / khu rnal 'byor pa'i 'gyur/ sgrol ma lha lnga'i sgrub thabs rin po tshe gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rat+na da ti dang / lo tsA ba rma ban gyi 'gyur/ thugs rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs
40a6(dkar chag): dngos grub phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje dang / ba ri lo tsA'i 'gyur/ sgrol ma'i nang gi gtor cho ga slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa dang / phyir bzlog gi 'khar lo dang / sgrol ma
40b1(dkar chag): gsang grub slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa rnams/ paN+Di ta rat+na da ti dang / rma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ thugs rje sgrol ma las sna tshogs kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ khwa gdong ma srung mnga'
40b2(dkar chag): nag mo zhes bya ba slob dpon rtag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ sgrol ma'i man ngag me long dwangs pa zhes bya ba/ rma dang / ba ri'i 'gyur/ de rnams sgrol mi rnal 'byor bla med du bkral ba'i skor rnams so// ma rgyud spyi dang 'brel
40b3(dkar chag): ba la or+yaN gyi rnal 'byor pa dang / rnal 'byor ma'i rang byung gi longs spyod dur khrod kyi rtog pa zhes bya ba birba pas mdzad pa las btus pa/ pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrti'i rang 'gyur/ slob dpon don yod rdo rjes mdzad pa'i rjes
40b4(dkar chag): chags kyi sbyor bas de kho na nyid kyi rnal 'byor la 'jug pa'i man ngag ces bya ba dang / las kyi phyag rgya brtag pa'i man ngag gnyis paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dbang chos kyi rten 'brel 'gro
40b5(dkar chag): ldog nA ro bos mdzad pa/ bla ma te pu pa dang / rma ban gyi 'gyur/ byang chub kyi sems bde ba chen po'i man ngag gnyis jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon ngag dbang
40b6(dkar chag): grags pas mdzad pa'i 'chi ba blu ba'i man ngag sh+lo ka sum brgya drug cu paM/ jo bo rje dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'di phyi nang gi rgyud du ma dang 'brel yang khyad par ma rgyud rdo rje mkha' 'gro dang / gdan bzhi dang
41a1(dkar chag): 'grel par snang bas 'dir bkod do// rmi lam brtag pa bi b+hU ti tsan+d+ra'i rang 'gyur/ pad+ma dra ba dpal 'byung gi sgrub thabs rgyal ba dpal ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta su ma na shrI dang / bod
41a2(dkar chag): lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ pad+ma dra ba'i rim pas bcom ldan 'das kyi dkyilas 'khor mchod pa'i cho ga rgyal ba dpal ye shes ming gzhan pad+ma rdo rje zhes bya bas mdzad pa/ kha che'i paN+Di ta chen po su ma na shrI b+ha dra dang /
41a3(dkar chag): bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ ma rgyud dang phyogs mthun pa mgon po nag po'i skor la/ nag po chen po'i rgyud drag po'i brtag pa dur khrod chen po zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa slob dpon rta dbyings kyis mdzad pa dang /
41a4(dkar chag): nag po chen po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dngos grub rin chen 'byung gnas zhes bya ba dang / sbyin sreg gi cho ga ye shes kyi me sbar ba dang gnyis paN+Di ta sa man+ta shrI mdzad pa de nyid dang / rwa chos rab kyi 'gyur/ nag po chen po yab
41a5(dkar chag): yum can gyi sgrub thabs klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang lo tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes kyi 'gyur/ dpal nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa dang / mgon po bya rog gdong can gyi
41a6(dkar chag): nang sgrub dang gnyis/ paN+Di ti a b+ha yA ka ra gup+ta dang / lo tsA ba rtsami sangs rgyas grags kyi 'gyur/ nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/ byin gyis brlab pa'i nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs
41b1(dkar chag): sha ba ri pas mdzad pa/ nag po chen po'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba'i cho ga/ bram ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nag po ro 'dzin dang / gyi ljang dbu dkar ba'i 'gyur/ mgon po nag po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon
41b2(dkar chag): bsod snyoms pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA su ma ti kIrti dang / lai ts+tsha ba prad+d+hi kIr+t+ti'o 'gyur/ nag po chen po'i gtor cho ga dI paM shrI ka ra dz+nyA nAs mdzad pa de nyid dang / 'khyim ston pa'i 'gyur/ lha mo nag mo'i sgrub thabs lo ka shrI'i
41b3(dkar chag): 'gyur/ lha mo re ma tI dmag zor gyi man ngag/ A tsar+ya dmar po zhi bas kyis mdzad pa/ yang nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs chag nyis/ nag po chen po'i bstod pa rkang brgyad 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ nag po chen
41b4(dkar chag): po'i bstod pa zlum ze mchog sred kyis mdzad pa/ nag po chen po'i bstod pa a bu d+hU tI pas mdzad pa/ nag po chen po la bstod bsgral sangs rgyas grags pas mdzad pa/ bya rog ming tsu na dang / bya rog gdong can la
41b5(dkar chag): bstod pa/ rtsa mi sangs rgyas grags pas mdzad pa se lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ 'di gnyis rtsom mkhan bod kyis brtsams pa yin kyang / saM skr-i ta'i skad du brtsams shing / bod skad du bsgyur ba yin pas/ sngar gyi rnams kyis
41b6(dkar chag): bris 'dug pas bris so// nag po chen po'i bstod pa rkang pa brgyad pa paN+Di ta bai ro tsa na badz+ra dang ding ri chos grags kyi 'gyur/ nag po chen po'i bstod pa brgyad pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ dud sol ma'i sgrub thabs nA ma phas
42a1(dkar chag): na rlobs mdzad pa s+ho b+hU gyur/ dang l+yA stan+na k+ta nas ma la bstod pa brgyad pa zhes bya ba zlum pa mchog sreng kyis snadad pa rnams bzhugs so// sgrom su bla mang spyod la lbu brgya dran
42a2(dkar chag): ma rgyud spyi 'grel bdun dang pad tra'i gnyis// mgon po nag po'i skor la nyi shu ste// gril bas chos skor brgyad cu rtsa lnga bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag sring zhi'i rgyun gcig ces bya ba las/ sprul
42a3(dkar chag): la sogs pa'i skor gyi le'u ste dgu pa'o// / rnal 'byor chen po thabs kyi rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa'i skor la/ dang po mgon po klu sgrub kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i 'phags skor la// / shrI pa la
42a4(dkar chag): gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa slob dpon chen po klu sgrub kyis mdzad zer ba'i le'u bcu bdun pa yan chad man+ta ka la shu'i rang 'gyur/ le'u bco brgyad pa gzhon nu bum pa'i rang 'gyur gnyis bzhugs so// 'grel pa
42a5(dkar chag): 'di slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad ma mdzad rtsod pa can du 'dug na'ang / bong ma ma yin par 'dug cing / mtshan bzang po la g.yar 'dug pa'i don la dbu ru bzhugs su bcug pa yin no// // sa pa la dpal gsang
42a6(dkar chag): bab 'dus pa'i 'grel pa sgron ma gsal ba zhes bya ba'i rgya cher bshad pa slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur la/ 'gos kyi g.yar khral cung zad 'tshal
42b1(dkar chag): ba las slar yang zhus chen bgyis pa'i 'gyur gsum la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i sbyor ba yan lag drug pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad pa/ pad+d+hi ta shAd+d+ha ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur//
42b2(dkar chag): gsang 'dus rgyud phyi ma le'u brgyad pa'i 'grel pa thams cad kyi sgron ma/ paN+Di ta snyan grogs bzang pos mdzad pa/ smr-i ti'i rang 'gyur/ 'di the tshom gyi gzhi zhig snang ngo // / ha pa la rgyud dgongs pa lung ston
42b3(dkar chag): gyi nang gi rdo rje bzlas pa'i rgya cher bshad pa zhes bya ba dang / ye shes rdo rje kun las btus pa'i rgyud las 'byung ba'i rgyan bdun rnam par dkrol ba dang gnyis/ shrad+d+ha ka ra wArmas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/
42b4(dkar chag): sgron ma gsal bar byed pa'i gsal byed ces bya ba'i dka' 'grel zhes bya ba/ slob dpon thugs rje'i dpal gyi zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ sgron ma gsal ba mdor bshad pa'i sa gcod
42b5(dkar chag): snying gi me long zhes bya ba/ mkhas b+ha ku mA ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta gzhon nu bum pa dang / lo tsA ba shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur/ sgron ma gsal ba'i dka' ba btus pa'i 'grel pa zhes bya ba/ slob dpon legs ldan 'byed kyis mdzad
42b6(dkar chag): pa/ paN+Di ta rgyal ba mchog dang / lo tsA ba shAkya brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / a ki gnyis la/ sgron gsal gyi TIk+ka dgongs pa rab gsal zhes bya ba/ slob dpon b+ha bya kIrti'i zhal snga nas/
43a1(dkar chag): mdzad pa sh+lo ka stong phrag bcu drug pa/ paN+Di ta ku mA ra'i rang 'gyur/ sgron gsal le'u dang po'i 'grel bshad slob dpon 'phags pa lhas mdzad zer ba 'di bod ma 'dra bar 'dug na'ang / sngar gyi rnam
43a2(dkar chag): kyis bris 'dug pas bris so// / khi pa la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad rgyud rdo rje phreng ba'i rgya cher 'grel pa zab mo'i don gyi 'grel pa zhes bya ba paN+Di ta A laM ka ka la shas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid da
43a3(dkar chag): steng pa lo tsA bas bsgyur ba las/ le'u bzhi bcu rtsa bzhi pa'i phyed yan chad kyi 'grel pa ji tsam rnyed pa bzhugs so// 'di'i 'phro nga rung du yang btsal bar bya'o// de ltar rgyud 'grol gyi skor rnams bkod nas/ da ni sgrub thabs
43a4(dkar chag): dkyil chog man dag la sogs pa'i skor la// / gi pA la sgrub pa'i thabs mdor byas pa slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA shrAd+h+r-i ka rA warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/
43a5(dkar chag): sgrub pa'i thabs mdo dang bsres pa zhes bya ba slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+hArma shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga nyi shu pa slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad zer ba/ paH
43a6(dkar chag): tosu b+hA shrI ta dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ dbang bzhi pa'i rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAn+ti gar+b+ha dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i
43b1(dkar chag): byang chub sems kyi 'grel pa tshigs bcang ma/ paN+Di ta gu Na A kA ra dang / lo tsA ba rab zhi bshes gnyen gyi 'gyur la/ phyis paN+Di ta ka na ka warma dang / pa tsha ba nyi ma grags kyis bcos pa/ byang chub sems 'grel lhug pa
43b2(dkar chag): ma paN+Di ta dza ya A nAn+na dang / lo tsA ba khu mdo sde 'bar gyi 'gyur/ rdzogs rim rim pa lnga pa slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Da ta shrAd+d+ha kA ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur la/ yang paN+Di ta ka me la
43b3(dkar chag): gup+ta dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bcos pa/ rim lnga'i don 'grel spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma slob dpo na Ar+ya de bas mdzad pa/ pi N+Di ta shrad+d+ha ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ sh+lo ka stong sum
43b4(dkar chag): brgya pa/ sems la dmigs pa'i rim pa'i don 'grel sems kyi sgrib pa sbyong ba'i rib tu byed pa zhes bya ba 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dz+nyA na ki ra dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ sgra lus kyi don
43b5(dkar chag): 'grel bdag byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba dang / 'od gsal gyi don 'grel mngon par byang chub pa'i rim pa zhes bya ba gnyis/ slob dpon Ar+ya dwe bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha kA ra wArma dang / lo ts+tsha ba rin chen
43b6(dkar chag): bzang po'i 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i ro sreg gi cho ga slob dpon Ar+ya de bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha ka ra warma dang / laM tsA bo rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ slob dpon Ar+ya de bas mdzada'i zer ba'i ya ra la ha la sogs tshul
44a1(dkar chag): bzhir bshad pa/ slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa bskyed rim rnam gzhag rim pa/ slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga nyi shu pa paN+Di ta thig le bum pa dang /
44a2(dkar chag): lo tsA ba pa tsha ba nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur/ las kyi mtha' rnam par 'byed pa slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma Ni kA shrI dz+nyA ni dang / paN+Di ta dwe wen+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ rim lnga'i 'grel pa
44a3(dkar chag): rim pa lnga'i khongs su bsdu ba zhes bya ba slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta A la ka ka la sha dang / lo tsA ba nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur/ rim lnga'i 'grel pa rnal 'byor yid 'phrog/ ma ga d+ha'i paN+Di ta thub pa
44a4(dkar chag): dpal bzang pos mdzad pa dkyil lo shrI ba chos kyi bzang po'i phyog dpe'i rgya dpe las bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon zla ba rgyab med byas kyi 'grem badzin chen grong ba'i gags na sa grags pas mdzad pa'i rdo rje
44a5(dkar chag): sems dpa'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba sh+lo ka rkang pa dang bcas pa'i brgya phrag gnyis pa/ paN+Di ta ta thA ga ta rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba klog skya gzhon nu 'bar gyi 'gyur la/ slad kyi paN+Di ta dI pa ka ra rak+Shi ta dang / ba ri lo tsA bas bcos pa/
44a6(dkar chag): rdo rje sems dpe'i sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa lA li badz+ra'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ bi b+hU ti tsan+d+ra'i rgya dpe la bltas nas/ lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ khro bo bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i sgrub thabs dpal ldan zla ba grags
44b1(dkar chag): pas mdzad pa paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha kA ra war+m+ma dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyun gyi 'grel pa zhes bya ba slob dpon zla ba grags pas mdzad zer ba 'di ni the tshom gyi gzhi cig snang ngo //
44b2(dkar chag): gsang 'dus kyi dkyil 'a'akhor gyi cho ga sh+lo ke phyed dang brgyad brgya pa slob dpon sgra gcan 'dzin dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur gsing ba
44b3(dkar chag): 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje sems dpa' mchod pa'i tshig slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang 'gros lhas bcas kyi 'gyur/
44b4(dkar chag): gtor ma'i cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ nag po pas mdzad pa'i rab gnas 'gos kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje 'chang chen po'i lam gyi rim pa slob dpon sgra dbyangs bcu gcig pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma shrI b+ha dra dang / lo
44b5(dkar chag): tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i gtor cho ga za hor gyi mkhas pa shAn+ta de bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba 'gos kyi 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i sbyin sgeg gi cho ga/ slob dpon rab 'jigs
44b6(dkar chag): rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha ka ra warma dang / d+harma shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ da ni sgrub skor de dag gi 'grel pa'i skor la/ sgrub thabs mdor byas kyi 'grel pa rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba/ slob dpon
45a1(dkar chag): rin chen 'byung ldan zhi bas mdzad pa/ karma badz+ra'i rang 'gyur/ sgrub pa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa zhes bya ba dz+nyA nA badz+ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ku mA ra dang / lha btsun pa'i 'gyur/ dpal gsang ba 'dus
45a2(dkar chag): pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha'i sku la bstod pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug mi gnas rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ro br-id+d+ha ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ byang chub sems 'grel gyi rnam bshad smr-i tis mdzad
45a3(dkar chag): pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid kyi 'gyur dad pa smra ba zhes bya ba bstod pa rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / ngi pa la sgrub thabs mdor byas dang rim lnga gnyis ka'i 'grel pa slob dpon b+ha bya
45a4(dkar chag): kIr+t+tis mdzad pa paN+Di ta rgyal ba mchog dang / lo tsA ba shAkya brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/ rim lnga'i bshad pa nor bu'i phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon klu bying gi mdzad zer ba/ paN+Di ta karma badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba ra kyi ma
45a5(dkar chag): gzhon nu tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ 'di slob dpon klu byang gris mdzad ma mdzad the tshom za bar 'dug kyang / rgya gar gyi paN+Di tas mdzad par 'dug pas bris so// rim lnga'i 'grel pa nag po dam tshig rdo rjes mdzad pa/
45a6(dkar chag): paN+Di de nyid dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ rim lnga'i dka' 'grel don gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon brtson 'grus bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba shes rab brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/
45b1(dkar chag): rim lnga'i dgongs 'grel zla ba'i 'od zer zhes bya ba slob dpon a b+ha yA kA ra gup+tas mdzad pa/ bi b+hU ti tsan+d+ras rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'o// sgrub thabs mdor byas kyi dka' 'grel/ paN+Di ta bi b+hU tI tsan+d+ras mdzad pa/ bod kyi
45b2(dkar chag): lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen grub kyi 'gyur/ rim lnga'i 'grel pa dron gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad zer ba 'di brdzun ma yin par 'dug na'ang / sngar gyi rnams kyis kyang bris 'dug pas bris so//
45b3(dkar chag): spyod bsdus sgron ma'i bshad pa slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ slob dpon zla bo grags pas mdzad pa'i rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrib thabs kyi 'grel pa/ ta thA ga tas mdzad pa/ dI paM ka ra rak+Shi ta dang / khams pa
45b4(dkar chag): bo ri lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ rim lnga'i 'grel pa kha che'i paN+Di ta lag smais mdzad pa paN+Di ta chen po tA ra ka la sha'i sras man+ta ka la sha nyid kyi ba sgyur ba rnams bzhugs so// / de ltar 'phags skor la 'grel
45b5(dkar chag): pa bco lnga dang / sgrub thabs la sogs kyi sgor sum cu rtsa brgyad de/ chos skor lnga bcu rtsa gsum mo// slob dpon ye shes zhabs kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi skor gyi rgyud kyi 'grel pa'i skor la//
45b6(dkar chag): ci pa la dpal gseng ba 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi le'u bco brgyad pa'i phyed kyi rtsa ba'i rgyud rdzogs pa'i 'grel pa man ngag gtan la dbab pa zhes kyang bya/ slob ma la phan pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rab tu zhi ba'i ye shes kyis
46a1(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ 'di slob dpon ye shes zhabs kyi dngos slob tshe 'di nyid la mya ngan las 'das pa'i gang zag bzhi'i ya gyal rab tu zhi ba'i bshes gnyen dang gcig mi gcig dpyad do// le'u bco
46a2(dkar chag): brgyad pa'i phyed kyi rtsa ba'i rgyud rdzogs pa man chad kyi 'grel pa slob dpon bi shwa mi tras mdzad pa/ gsang 'dus rgyud phyi ma dang bcas pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon tha ga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha ka rA wa~Mrma dang d+harma badz+ra dang /
46a3(dkar chag): lo hUM ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / chi ba la gsang 'dus rtsa rgyud le'u bcu bdun pa'i 'grel pa rin po che'i ljon shing zhes bya ba slob dpon chen bo tse lu pas mdzad pa/
46a4(dkar chag): paN+Di tA ka ma la gu h+ya dang / lo tsA ba mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ gsang 'dus rgyud le'u bcu bdun pa/ rgyud phyi ma le'u bco brgyad pa dang bcas pa'i 'grel pa/ slob dpon sman pa'i bu rgyal bas
46a5(dkar chag): byin gyis mdzad pa gnyis bzhugs so// / dzi ba lnga gsang 'dus le'u bcu bdun pa'i 'grel pa dri ma medo sbas pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pu N+ya shrI mi tra dang / lo tsA ba dar ma glags kyi 'gyur/ le'u
46a6(dkar chag): bo co brgyad pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon zla ba'i 'od kyis mdzad pa/ pu N+ya shrI dang / ngar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ yang dag rig byed ces bya ba rgyud phyi ma'i rnam par bshad pa slob dpon sman pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta
46b1(dkar chag): ka ma la gu h+ya dang / lo tsA ba mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad sbyar snyim pa'i me tog ces bya ba slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa'i le'u bcu gsum pa yan chad
46b2(dkar chag): rnams bzhugs so// / nyi pa la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad sbyar snyim pa'i me tog gi le'u bcu bzhi pa man chad/ paN+Di ta shAn+ta badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dpal gsang ba
46b3(dkar chag): 'dus pa'i rtsa ba'i rgyud le'u bcu bdun pa'i 'grel pa zla ba'i 'od zer zhes bya ba slob dpon dga' ba'i 'byung gnas go chas mdzad pa/ 'di ye shes zhabs kyi rjes su 'brang bya ba'i dmigs bsal mi 'dug na'ang / lha'i skyed
46b4(dkar chag): cho ga la sogs yeng shes zhabs lugs dang mthun par byung zhing / sngar gyi mkhas pa dag gis kyang ye shes zhabs lugs kyi phyogs su bris 'dug pas 'dir yang de bzhin bris so// de ltar rgyud so so'i 'grel pa
46b5(dkar chag): rnams bkod nas/ spyi'i man ngag la sogs pa'i sgrub skor la// / tri pa la rim pa gnyis pa zhes bya ba'i de kho na nyid bsgom pa'i zhal gyi lung / 'jam dpal zhal lung chen mar grags pa sangs
46b6(dkar chag): rgyas dpal ye shes zhabs kyis bsdus pa/ paN+Di ti ka ma la gu h+ya dang / lo tsA ba lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ zhal gyi lung chung ba sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis bsdus pa dang / sgrub thabs kun tu bzang po
47a1(dkar chag): zhes bya ba sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bsnyen sgrub yan lag bzhi'i sgrub thabs kun tu bzang mo zhes bya
47a2(dkar chag): pa sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ smr-i ti dz+nyA na kIrti'i rang 'gyur/ he ru ka'i sgrub thabs slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ de'i rang 'grel/ 'di gsum la sgrub pa'i thabs kun tu bzang mo
47a3(dkar chag): gsum zhes zer ro// grol ba'i thig la sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ pi NI ta ka mya la gu h+ya dang / lo tsA ba lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ bdag grub pa la 'jug pa slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shwe
47a4(dkar chag): zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAn+d+ha badz+rA dang lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ chu sbyin dbang po'i sgrub thabs gsum slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa pAd+d+hi tA dza ya saM nA dang / lho tsA ba dang ma
47a5(dkar chag): yon tan gyi 'gyur/ sbyin sreg gnyis kyi cho ga dang / gtor chog mi nub pa'i sgron ma dang / tshogs 'khor gyi 'khor lo sna tshogs 'khor lo dang / rin chen 'bar ba dang / rtsa ba'i ye shes chen po dang / tshogs su bcad
47a6(dkar chag): pa'i mdzod dang / byang chub sems kyi thig le dang / bkra shis kyi rnam bshad chen po dang / rgyud kyi rnam bshad dang / dkyil 'khor cho ga nyis brgya lnga bcu pa rnams la lung dang mthun pa'i chos bcu bzhi zhes bshad pa la/
47b1(dkar chag): rgyud kyi rnam bshad ni ma mdzad/ dkyil cho ga ni kha cher khyer nas/ rgya gar na med par bshad/ gzhan rnams la gong du smos pa rnams ma gtogs pa bong du 'gyur ba mi snang ngo // stang stabs kyi bkod pa slob dpon
47b2(dkar chag): chen po ye shes zhabs kyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyi dngos slob tshe 'di nyid la mya ngan las 'di'i ba bzhi'i ya gyal mar me mdzad bzang pos mdzad pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bzhi brgya lnga
47b3(dkar chag): bcu pa/ paN+Di ta pad+ma ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur rnams so// da ni de dag gi rjes su 'byung ba'i 'grel pa'i skor la/ zhal lung chen mo'i 'grel pa mdzes pa'i me tog ces bya ba slob dpon bi dI pA
47b4(dkar chag): dus mdzad pa/ paN+Di ti kA mA la gu h+ya dang mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ kun tu bzang po'i sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa slob dpon dpal 'bras rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bid+yA badz+ra dang / bi b+hA kA ra dang /
47b5(dkar chag): lo tsA ba rIn chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ kun tu bzang po'i sgrub thabs kyi 'grel pa slob dpon tha ga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di t+yA shrad+d+ha ka rA warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ yan lag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs kun tu
47b6(dkar chag): bzang mo'i rgya cher bshad pa snying po'i snye ma zhes bya ba slob dpon kun tu bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta n+yA na shrI dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ grol ba'i thig le'i rnam bshad slob dpon sman pa'i zhabs
48a1(dkar chag): kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ka ma la gu h+ya dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA
48a2(dkar chag): bid+yA badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba rnams bzhugs so// da ni de dag gi rjes su 'brang ba'i sgrub thabs dkyil cho ga la sogs pa'i skor la/ yan lag bzhi pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs kun tu bzang mo zhes bya ba'i rnam
48a3(dkar chag): par bshad pa slob dpon chen po bI dA pA das mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la gu h+ya dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chen po mnga' bdag ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi sgrub pa'i
48a4(dkar chag): thabs 'jig rten snang byed ces bya ba'i rnam par bshad pa slob dpon chen po bi dA pA das mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ka ma la gu h+ya dang / zhus tshan gyi lo tsA ba mnga' bdag ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur//
48a5(dkar chag): thi pA la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i sgrub thabs dngos grub 'byung ba'i gter zhes bya ba slob dpon bi dA pA dAs mdzad pa/ sbyor ba bdun pa'i dbang bzhi'i rab tu byed pa dang / gtor ma chen po'i cho ga dang / mi shigs pa rin
48a6(dkar chag): po che'i sgrub thabs dang / bdag gi don grub par byed pa'i rnal 'byor gyi bya ba'i rim pa zhes bya ba rnams slob dpon bi dA pA ngos mdzad cing / paN+Di ta ka ma la gu h+ya dang / lo tsA ba mnga' bdag lha ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/
48b1(dkar chag): sbyor ba yan lag drug gi snang ba'i rim pa zhes bya ba rnam par snang mdzad rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pu n+ya shrI dang / lo tsA ba g.yung drung 'od kyi 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i sgrub thabs rdo rjes mdzad po shrId+d+hi kI ri wAr+m+ma dang / dge slong
48b2(dkar chag): roriron chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba slob dpon dpal kun tu bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ga ta kIrti'i rang 'gyur/ kun tu bzang po'i bsdus dona'i slob dpon sangs rgyas
48b3(dkar chag): zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs dang / de'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang gnyis slob dpon bsod snyoms byas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA shrid+d+ha ka ra wArma dang / lo tsA ba rin
48b4(dkar chag): chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ dga' ba'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba slob dpon rgyal bas byin gyi sa mdzad pa/ ye shes zhabs kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i dpal gsang 'dus mi bskyod rdo rje'i sgrub thabs slob 'i dpon rin khyim pa
48b5(dkar chag): chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pad+ma ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'di la smr-i ti'i rang 'gyur gcig kyang yong mod kyi don gcig cing 'gyur 'dri bzang bas 'a di bris so// 'dus shing rtogs par sla ba zhes
48b6(dkar chag): bya ba'i 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta pun+d+ha shrI mi tras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba klog skya gzhon nu 'bar gyi 'gyur/ mdor bsdus pa'i dbang gi rab tu byed pa slob dpon dga' ba'i rdo rjes mdzad pa sh+lo ka
49a1(dkar chag): sum brgyu pa/ jo bo rje dang / ba ri'i 'gyur/ gsadra ba 'dus pa'i dbang bskur ba'i cho ga mdor bsdus pa paN+Di ta ngag dbang grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su mA ti kIrti dang lo tsA ba klog sgyu gzhon nu
49a2(dkar chag): 'bar dang / mar ba chos dbang gi 'gyur/ yan lag bdun ldan sh+lo ka bzhi brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga pa/ paN+Di ta ngag dbang grags pas mdzad pa/ 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ de kho na nyid snang ba dang / de'i rang 'grol de kho
49a3(dkar chag): na nyid snang ba'i bshad pa zhes bya ba gnyis ngag dbang grags pas mdzad pa/ 'gos lhas becis kyi 'gyur/ 'di gsum gsang 'dus kyi chos skor yin kyang / ye shes zhabs lugs kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i gsal kha
49a4(dkar chag): mi snang ste/ sngar gyi rnams kyis ye shes zhabs lugs kyi skor du bris pas bris so// gsang 'dus kyi sgrub thabs rab tu gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon dpe med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bIr+ya badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba
49a5(dkar chag): rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ gsang 'dus kyi dkyil 'khor la spyan ras gzigs gtso bor ston pa gsang ba 'dus pa 'jig rten dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs zhes bya ba jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba
49a6(dkar chag): rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ jo bo rjes mdzad pa'i 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs dang / dpal gsang ba 'dus pa la bstod pa jo bo rjes mdzad po gnyis/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba rin chen
49b1(dkar chag): bzang po'i 'gyur/ de kho na nyid bcu pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rgyan pas mdzad pa/ dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ 'dus pa'i rab gnas kyi cho ga slob dpon zla 'od kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta gu N+ya kIrti dang / lo tsA ba bskyod
49b2(dkar chag): nams rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ bstan pa'i nor thams cad pa zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon rat+na kIrti si mdza pa paN+Di titede nyid dang / lo tsA ba mchi mas yon tan 'bar gyi 'gyur/ khro bi bcu'i gtor ma'i cho
49b3(dkar chag): ga dge slong 'od srungs gzhon nus mdzad pa'i dbang gtan la dbab pa/ par+t+ti ta ta thA ga ta rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ ye shes zhabs lugs kyi sbyor ba yan lag drug pa'i 'grel pa
49b4(dkar chag): paN+Di ta smr-i tis mdzad cing de nyid kyi rang 'gyur/ ye shes zhabs lugs kyi sbyor ba yan lag drug pa zhes bya ba/ 'di gnyis 'grel pa chen po nas sbyor drug la mos pa zhig gis/ logs su phyung ba yin par
49b5(dkar chag): 'dug+sa pasaM/ logs su ma bris kyang btub mod kyi/ sbyar gyi rnams kyis kyang bris 'dug cing / don bzang pos bris so// 'jam pa'i rdo rje mchod pa'i cho ga/ slob dpon dpal byin gyis mdzad pA/ shAk+Sha'i dge
49b6(dkar chag): slong blo gros seng ges zhu chen byas nas paN+Di ta chen po bi b+hU ti tsan+d+ras rang 'gyur du mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so// / di pa la gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud lo brten pa'i arga'i cho ga snying
50a1(dkar chag): bsdus pa zhes bya ba dang / gsang ba 'dus pa'i rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga ye shes snang ba zhes bya ba dang gnyis slob dpon snang byed zla bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ti wa ren+d+ra ka dang / l-i tsA ba pradz+nyA/
50a2(dkar chag): kIr+t+ti'i 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i rab gnas kyi cho ga/ slob dpon mi 'jigs pa'i phyag gis mdzad pa/ dus tha ma'i cho ga gshin po bde bar gshegs pa'i gnas la 'gyod pa zhes bya ba dpal ting nge 'dzin rdo
50a3(dkar chag): rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dpal phyogs dbang dga' byed dang / lo ts+tsha ba pradz+nyA kIrti'i rang 'gyur/ spyan ma'i ngan song sbyong ba'i cho ga dpal ting nge 'dzin rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bai ro tsa na badz+rA gyi zhal snga na so dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dang
50a4(dkar chag): riro chos grags kyi bsgyur ba rnams so// de ltar ye shes zhabs kyi rjes su 'byung ba rnams la 'gyul pa'i sbyor dgro/ sgrub thabs la sogs chos kyi skor bzhi bcu zhe gcig ste/ chos skor lnga bcu tham pa'o// de ltar
50a5(dkar chag): ye shes zhabs lug sa kyi rjes su 'byung ba rnams bkod nas/ da ni slob dpon rdo rje bzhad pa la sogs pa'i bzhed lugs kyi gsang 'dus kyi skor ni/ dpal gsung ba 'dus pa'i rtswa rgyud le'u bcu bdun pa'i 'grel
50a6(dkar chag): pa dgongs pa thams cad nye bar len pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rdo rje bzhad pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dz+nyA na gar+b+ha dang / lo tsA ba bai ro tsa na'i 'gyur/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi gleng gzhi bla ma'i man ngag gis bshad pa slob
50b1(dkar chag): dpon sgeg pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bde ba chen po'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba'i gsang 'dus kyi sgrub thabs rdo rje bzhad pas mdzad pa dang / de'i 'grel pa slob dpon chen po bi mA la gar+b+has mdzad pa rnams te/ 'di dag sngar gyi rnams
50b2(dkar chag): kyis ye shes zhabs lugs kyi gseb tu bris mod kyi/ 'di dag ye shes zhabs kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i gsal kha med cing / lha bskyed cho ga la stsogs kyang 'phags skor dang tshe mthun cing / ye shes zhabs lugs dang mi
50b3(dkar chag): mthun pas lugs gud du byas so// gsang 'dus lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs/ slob dpon rdo rje sgeg pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ de ltar rdo rje bzhad pa lugs kyi chos skor
50b4(dkar chag): lnga'o// gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud/ rtsa ba'i rgyud dang / rgyud phyi ma go nyis ka bla ma'i man ngag las bris pa zhes bya ba dang / lha mo'ibazhis zhus kyi bshad pa man ngag rgyas pa zhes bya ba gnyis smra tis mdzad cing de nyid kyi rang
50b5(dkar chag): 'gyur/ lha mo bzhis zhus kyi rgyud kyi bshad pa slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa/ smr-i ti'i rang 'gyur rnams te 'di dag kyang sngar gyi rnams kyi ye shes zhabs lugs kyi skabs su gtogs par bshad mod kyi ye
50b6(dkar chag): shi sa zhabs lugs kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i gsal kha med cing / bzang po zhabs kyi rjes su 'brang ba smr-i tis gsal bar gsungs pas 'di dag kyang lugs tha dad yin no// de ltar bzang po zhabs dang smr-i ti'i chos skor
51a1(dkar chag): gsum mo// / ni pa la gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud kyi dka' 'grel slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA bI dz+nyA ya shrI b+hA rA dang / nu ba rin chen bzang po'i chu
51a2(dkar chag): lngalha/ smad naswA pAd+d+hi tA shrAd+d+ha kA ra warma dang / lo ts+tsha ba rin chen bzang pos bcos pa'o// 'di 'grel pa mkhan pos rnal 'byor gyi rgyud du bkral nas snang na'ang / rgyud kyi ngo bo rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud yin pas skabs
51a3(dkar chag): 'dir bris so// slob dpon kun dga' snying po'i lugs kyi chos sbyor gcig go// gAsang 'dus 'phyag sa sgor ye shes zhabos su gas dang / rdo rje 'i zhang pa bzang po'i zhabs dang nI// skr-i ti kun dga' snying po la sogs

51a5(dkar chag): gas+t+ya ba 'dus pa'i rgyud dang mo pa'i sbyor rnams bkod nas/ da ni de'i cha dang mthun pa'i rgyud/ gA kin+da rjeg byed dgra nAg gi rgyud le'u bcoM bAd+d+ha d+hA 'i 'grel pa lhun cig skyes pa'i snang ba skyes bya ba sgrub thob dpas

51b1(dkar chag): bi nA ya tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ ga shIn rje gshed nag po'i rgyud kyi rgyu cher 'grel pa mngon par mthong ba'i lam gyi sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta prad+d+ha shrI dz+nyA na kr-Irti'i

51b3(dkar chag): gshed nag po'i rnam 'grel ye shes sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon pad+ma pA Nis mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA sa ra me shwa dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba rong zom chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba rnams bzhugs so//

52a5(dkar chag): pa'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga slob dpon kA ma la rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ shrI pradz+nyA dz+nyA na kIrti'i rang 'gyur/ maN+Dal gyi cho ga rtog med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ gshin rje gshed dgra nAg gi sgrub thabs ku mu ta
52a6(dkar chag): kha phye baM zhes bya ba/ slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pi nA ya tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ gshin rje gshed nag po zhal gsum phyag drug pa'i sgrub tho bas/ gshin rje
52b1(dkar chag): gshed nag po dus mthar phyin pa'i sgrub thabs shrI paN+Di ta sa mdzad pa dang / gshin rje gshed nag po'i sgrub thabs dang / gshin rje gshed rnam par snang mdzad kyi sgrub thabs dang / gshin rje gshed rin chen 'byung ldan gyi
52b2(dkar chag): sgrub thabs dang / 'od dpag tu med po'i snying po 'dod chags gshin rje gshed kyi sgrub thubs dang / gshin rje gshed rdo rje rnon po'i sgrub thabs dang / rdo rje sems de pa' bde ba'i sgrub thabs dang / rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma rnal

52b5(dkar chag): skyes kyi sgrub thabs ka ma l-i rak+Shi tas mdzad pa/ tho ba gshi na rje gshed kyi sgrib thabs dA nga / dbyu ga pa gshin rje gshed kyi sgrub thabs dang / ral gri gshin+da rje gshed kyi sgrub thabs de nga / pad+ma gshin rje gshad

53a5(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ gshin rje gshed nag pa'i 'khor lo'i mu na ngag/ slob dpon nA ga bo d+his mdzad pa/ dge slong tshwa sA rab kyi 'gyur/ gshin rje gshed nAg
