56a2(dkar chag): rje gshed dra mar po'i sgrub thabs dang / maN+Dal gyi cho ga grub thob dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ gshin rje gshed dmar po dang / nag pa'i mchod pa'i cho ga dang / gshed
56a3(dkar chag): dmar gyi ting nge 'dzin gyi cho ga dang / gtor ma'i cho ga rnams grub thob dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa dang / gshed dmar gyi sgrub thabs rnam par snang mdzad srung bas mdzad pa dang / gshed dmar lha lnga'i sgrub thabs
56a4(dkar chag): rang byin gyis brlab pa'i man ngag dang bcas pa blo gros bzang pos mdzad pa rnams pad+ma ta nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer dang / chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ gshing dmar gyi 'khrul 'khor gyi gsal byed bsdus pa
56a5(dkar chag): zhes bya ba dang / gshin rje gshed dmar gyi las tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i de kha na nyid gsal bar byed pa slob dpon byang chub snying pos mdzad pa/ rdo rje gangan pa ni sgra laM ka dang / dpyal chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ gshin
56a6(dkar chag): rje dgra dmar po'i sgrub thabs blo bzang snying po'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ gshin rje gshed dmar po'i rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor zhes bya ba paN+Di ta 'jigs med 'byung gnas
56b1(dkar chag): smras pas mdzad pa/ g+ha shrIn rje gshed dmar po'i 'tsho ba'i de kho na nyid ces bya ba'i mun ngag/ paN+Di ta dar paN+Da A tsar+yas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang / lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen gyi 'gyur/ gshin rje mthar byed dmar
56b2(dkar chag): po'i byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa grub thob 'khor lo sgyur ba/ bram ze dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po darba Na A tsar+ya dang / glo bo lo tsA ba dge slong shes rab rin chen gyi 'gyur/ lha mo 'od 'dzin
56b3(dkar chag): ma'i byin rlabs grub thob dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po de ba A kA ra dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba las/ phyis rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paN+Di ta darbAn A tsar+ya dang / lo tsA ba
56b4(dkar chag): dge slong rdo rje 'dzin pa zhe sdang rdo rje'i 'gyur/ 'od 'dzin mo'i sgrub thabs dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ lo paN sngar dang 'dra/ rat+na gi sems gong du 'pho ba'i mun ngag dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rgya gar
56b5(dkar chag): mngon shes can dang / bod kyi la ts+tsha pA 'gos khug pas bsgyur ba las/ phyis darban A tsar+ya dang lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen gyi 'gyur/ byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa darban A tsar+ya dang / glo bo lo tsA bo dge slong
56b6(dkar chag): pradz+nyA rat+na'i 'gyur/ me lha mchod pa'i cho ga rgya gar gyi mkhan po darban A tsaur+ya dang / dge slong shes rab rin chen gyi 'gyur/ bdud rtsi byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa birba pas mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po darban
57a1(dkar chag): A tsAr+ya dang / lo tsA ba zhe sdang rdo rje'i 'gyur/ srung 'khor gyi byin rlabs dang / phyir bzlog man ngag gsang ba las kyang ches gsang ba/ bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed dmar po'i zhal
57a2(dkar chag): gradams slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po i nu pa ma rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba daMr ma yon tan gyi 'gyur la/ phyis rgya gar shar phyogs kyi mkhan po chen po dAR+Yan A tsar+ya dang / lo tsA ba
57a3(dkar chag): shes rab rin chen gyi 'gyur/ lngas gshin gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon la liM ta badz+ra sa mdzad pa/ bal po thugs rje chen po dang / rwa rdo rje grogs kyi 'gyur/ gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sngags ba tu slob dpon dpal
57a4(dkar chag): 'dzin gyis mdzad pa dA na shI la'i 'gyur/ gshin rje gshed dmar po'i las kyi phreng ba'i sgrub thabs yid bzhin nor bu zhes bya ba la longs spyod can ma'i rtog pa/ dga' byas tshim ma'i sgrub thabs/ gnod sbyin
57a5(dkar chag): ma Ta pho myo'i sgrub thabs/ gnod sbyin ma sa'i bdag mo bkra shis ma'i sgrub thabs/ gnod sbyin dga' byed kyi sgrub thabs/ gnod sbyin phur 'debs kyi sgrub thabs/ gnod sbyin rdeg byed kyi sgrub thubs/ dpal
57a6(dkar chag): zla be lha mo'i sgrub thabs/ ro na chen phreng ba ma'i sgrub thabs/ klu mo zhal mtha' yas ma'i sgrub thab so// klu mo skyong zhal ma'i sgrub thabs/ klu mo ai yu ma'i sgrub thab so// 'phrog ma rna tsho 'dzin ma'i sgrub
57b1(dkar chag): thabs/ yid 'phrog ma'i sgrub thabs/ legs par dga' mu'i sgrub thAbs/ spyan yangs ma'i sgrub thabs/ 'dod chags dga' ma'i sgrub thabs/ gzhan gyis mi thub ma'i sgrub thabs/ lhag par rgyal ba mi pham ma'i
57b2(dkar chag): sgrub thabs/ gang ba bza po'i sgrub thabs/ 'byung mo mdzes ma'i sgrub tha bas/ dpal rgyu la mdzes ma'i sgrub thabs/ dri med mdzes ma'i sgrub thabs/ sha za pi lu pa lnga'i sgrub thabs/ sha zla nor bu 'dzin pa'i
57b3(dkar chag): spro ba thabs/ sha za nag po'i sgrub thubs/ sha za nag po'i snying po'i sgri ba thabs/ sha za ha na ma'i sgrub thabs/ a lu ka zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs a la sbas pa zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ bong bu'i gdong can ma'i
57b4(dkar chag): sgrub thabs/ a lu bi na zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ u tsusma zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ k+Shu k+Shu se ri kunA nga'i sgrub thabs/ sha za mo rna ba 'dzin pa'i sgrub thabs/ sha za mo nug mo bi sgrub thab ste/ sgrub thabs sum cu
57b5(dkar chag): rtsa bdun pa shes rab skyong gis mdzad pa/ dA nA shI li'i ring 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// de ltar gshin rje gshed dmar la chos skor lnga bcu rtsa dgu'o// 'khrul 'khor mthar thi ga gshin rje gshed po'i rgyud//
57b6(dkar chag): gshin rje gshed nag rdo rje 'jigs byed dang // gshin rje gdong drug gshed dmar la sogs kyi// chos skor brgya dang sum cu rtsa drug bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur cog gi dkar chag sring zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba
58a1(dkar chag): las/ gshin rje gshed kyi skor gyi le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o// / phi pa la mtshan yang dag par brjod pa rnal 'byor bla med kyi lugs su bkral ba'i skor la/ mtshan
58a2(dkar chag): yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa mtshan don gsal bar byed pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa/ gnyigs dz+nyA na'i 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa don gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba dga' rab rdo rjes
58a3(dkar chag): mdzad zer ba 'di the tshom gyi gzhi'o// mtshan yang dag par brjod pa nye bar bsdus pa'i rnam par rtog ge zhes bya ba dpal gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrI badz+ra bo d+hi dang / lo tsA bo dpyal se rtsa bsod nams
58a4(dkar chag): rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ dpal ldan byang chub mchog gis mdzad pa'i sngags don rnams gzigs dang / slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa'i nye bar bsdus pa rnam par rtog ge gnyis kyi don bsdus mtshan gyi sgron
58a5(dkar chag): ma zhes bya ba shes rab bla mas mjed pa/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa snying po mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i slob dpon gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na'i rang 'gyur/ 'jam dpal
58a6(dkar chag): ye shes sems dpa'i mngon par rtogs pa dang / 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'i rin po che'i phyag rgya dri ma med pa'i cho ga zhes bya ba dang / rang bzhin du gnas pa'i sngags kyi spyod pa bcu pa zhes bya ba dang / rmi lam brtag
58b1(dkar chag): pa zhes bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi byang chub bsam gtan gyi dug sel bar byed pa'i mar me zhes bya ba dang / 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'i yid 'jug pa'i bsam gtan gyi 'khor lo zhes bya ba dang / thig le grub
58b2(dkar chag): pa zhes bya ba dang / thig le gcig po zhes bya ba dang / 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'i snying po grub pa zhes bya ba ste dgu/ paN+Di ta gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad cing / rnal 'byor bsod snyoms pa pradz+nyA shrI dz+nyA na kIrti'i rang 'gyur/
58b3(dkar chag): 'jam dpal gyi gdams pa ma tri pa'i man ngag nye bar bsdus pa dang de'i 'grel pa zab cing rgya che ba zhes bya ba'i 'grol pa slob dpon dril bu pas mdzad pa paN+Di ta many+dzu shrI sid+d+hi dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan she sa ra ba kyi 'gyur/
58b4(dkar chag): 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs zhi ba 'od kyi rim pa zhes bya ba dang / 'jam dpal khro bo'i sgrub thabs rdo rje 'od kyi rim pa zhes bya ba dang / dkyil cho ga dang / skyabs 'gro sems bskyed dbang bzhi'i cho ga dang / rdo rje glu'i
58b5(dkar chag): gdams pa zhes bya ba dang / khrus kyi cho ga dang / gtor ma'i cho ga dang / bdun tshogs kyi cho ga dang / ro sreg gi cho ga dang / sauts+tsha gdab pa'i cho ga dang / rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga dang / sbyin sreg gi cho ga dang / thun mo dgi
58b6(dkar chag): dngos grub sgrub pa'i man ngag dang / maN+Dal dbul ba'i man ngag ste bcu gsum po rnams ni bram ze sdom pa bzang pos mdzad cing / 'bro lo tsA ba d+harmA ba'i 'gyur/ 'di dag la the tshom zo ba snang yang / rgya gar mar byed kyi
59a1(dkar chag): 'dug pas bris so// mtshan brjod rnal 'byor chen po tha med du// dgongs pa 'grel ba'i rgyud 'gre la rnam pa lnga// sgrub thabs la stsogs nyi shu rtsa ba'i ste// gril bas chos skur nyi shu rtsa dgu na/
59a2(dkar chag): bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag srid zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/ mtshan brjod rnal 'byor bla med du be krol ba'i sgor te le'u baM cu gnyis pa'o// / bde chen ral gcig lha nyi shu rtsa
59a3(dkar chag): lnga'i sgrub thabs/ ral pa gcig pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba dang / ral gcig lhatha bdun gyi bdag nyid kyi sgrub thabs dang / ral gcig yum gyi sgrub thabs rnams mi pham sbas pa'i bshes
59a4(dkar chag): gnyen mtshan gyi rnam grangs rol pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa dang / ral gA cig yab yum lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs shrI badz+ra kIrtis mdzad pa dang / ral gcig ma'i sgrub thabs 'khor gnod sbyin dang bcas pa mi tra dzo kis
59a5(dkar chag): mdzad pa rnams/ shrI dzaM ga ta mi tra A nan+da dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ bsngo ba nor bu'i sgron ma paN+Di ta me phram zla bas mdzad pa paN+Di ta su b+hA ri shAn+ti dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ ral
59a6(dkar chag): gcig la bstod pa paN+Di ta bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ de'i rdzogs rim ston pa'i man ngag rang gi sems ngal bso ba tshigs su bcad pa nyi shu rtsa lnga po/ spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug
59b1(dkar chag): gris gsungs pa/ grub chen mi tra dz+re kI dang / lho tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ rtogs pa brjod pa sum cu pa zhes bya ba mi tra dzo kis mdzad pa de nyid dang / gnubs lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ kha sAR+Ya
59b2(dkar chag): Ni yab yum gyi sgrub thabs/ grub thob mi tra dzo kis mdzod pa de nyid dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ dpal gnod sbyin spun gnyis kyi sgrub thabs/ mi tra dzo kis mdzad pa de nyid dang / gnubs byams pa'i
59b3(dkar chag): dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'di dag ma rgyud kyi phyogs su gtogs pa 'dra bar snang yang / bla ma rnams kyis phra rgyud kyi phyogs su byas snang bas 'dir bris so// rigs kyi 'jig rten mgon po'i sgrub thabs kyi snong ba/ rje btsun
59b4(dkar chag): ma hi mas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+har+m+ma d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ rigs kyi 'jig rten mgon po'i rtogs pa lnga bcu'i 'grel pa mdor bsdus paN+Di tA dri med dpal ba zang pos mdzad pa de nyid dang
59b5(dkar chag): lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ rigs kyi 'jig rten dbang phyug bsgom pa'i rim pa dang / de'i rjes gnang gi cho ga gnyis paN+Di ta bi mA la shrIs mdza pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba shong blo brtan gyi 'gyur/
59b6(dkar chag): rigs kyi 'jig rten dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs bram ze bying+ga ras mdzad pa/ 'jam dpal sgeg pa'i rdo rje'i 'gyur/ spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug yi ge bdun pa'i sgrub thabs mi tra dzo kis mdzad pa de nyid dang / lo tsA ba
60a1(dkar chag): byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'di rnams rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud du gsal bar gsungs shing / thabs shes rab kyi rgyud 'dir gtogs gsal bar ma gsungs kyang / thabs rgyud dang mthun pa gtso
60a2(dkar chag): che bar snang bas 'drir bkod do// tshe dang ye shes dpag tu med pa'i sgrub thabs dang / dkyil cho ga gnyis mkha' 'gro ma grub pa'i rgyal mos byas pa yin zer ba rnal 'byor bla med du byas pa 'dri'ang rgya gzhung yin zer nas bris
60a3(dkar chag): so// tshe dpag med kyi sgrub thabs de'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga sbyin sre ga rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs rnams grub pa'i rgyal mos mdzad pa/ rgya gor gyi paN+Di ta zla ba bzang po dang glan dar ma tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ spyan ras gzigs
60a4(dkar chag): dbang rnal 'byor bla med du// 'gyur ba'i ral gcig 'jig rten mgon po sogs// tshe dpag med pa'i chos skor rnam gnyis te// bcu phrag gcig la dgu yis brgyan pa bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur ro tsag gi dkar
60a5(dkar chag): chag sring zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/ bde chen ral gcig la sogs pa'i skor gyi le'u ste bcu gsum pa'o// / phyag na rdo rje rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud du bkral ba la/ 'khor lo chen po'i
60a6(dkar chag): skor ni drag po gsum 'dul gyi rgyud kyi 'grel pa bdud rtsi myu gu zhes bya ba dza pa ri pas sa wa ra~M paM la man ngag tu zhus pa dang / sgrub thabs rgyas pa 'khor lo chen po zhes bya ba dang / 'bring po lag na rdo rje gos sngon po
60b1(dkar chag): can gyi gzungs kyi sgrub thabs bdud rtsi thigs pa zhes bya ba dang / mdor bsdus sgrub thabs mdor bsdus zhes bya ba ste/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i sgrub thabs gsum dang / klu rigs bzhi'i sgrub pa'i thabs dang /
60b2(dkar chag): gnod sbyin gyi sde rnam par sbyong zhing sel ba'i sgrub thabs dang / yi dwags dang / sha za dang / grul bu mi dang / srul po rnams rnam par sbyong zhing / sel ba'i sgrub thabs te 'jig rten pa'i sgrub thabs gsum dang /
60b3(dkar chag): phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi gzungs kyi gau tor ma'i cho ga dang / rmi ltas rim pa drug dang / bsad pa bdud rtsi gso ba dang / bdud rtsi 'o mo'i mchod pa dang / klu khro bos bsad pa'i phrin las dang / klu rigs bzhi mnan
60b4(dkar chag): pa'i cho ga dang / zhi rgyas kyi sbyin sreg dang / drag po'i sbyin sreg dang / phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang / mdze nad kyi mtshan nyid dang / 'khor lo chen po'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha la bstod pa dang /
60b5(dkar chag): de ltar bco brgyad po nam gru'i rigs las byung ba dngos grub brnyes pa'i slob dpon dza pa ri pas mdzad pa/ bal po'i paN+Di ta daM ba pur+Na ma ti dang / lo tsA ba 'gar chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i
60b6(dkar chag): srung ba slob dpon dza ba ri pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de ba pur+Na ma ti dang / lo tsA ba she'u badz+ra de ba'i 'gyur/ phyag na rdo rje rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud du bkral ba la/ rdo rje me lce'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa de kho na nyid snang ba zhes bya ba
61a1(dkar chag): phyag na rdo rje'i sku dngos su sbrul nus pa phyag na rdo rje zhes bya bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta many+dzu shrI dang / lo tsA pa gzhon nu tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon des mdzad pa'i me lce'i phreng bya'i
61a2(dkar chag): sgrub thabs/ slob dpon b+ha ba pas mdzad pa'i skor la/ lag nA rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi sgrub thabs dang / gos sngon po can gyi sgrub thabs chen po dang / sgrub thabs chung bya dang / dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang / rdzogs
61a3(dkar chag): ma ston pa lung bstun po'i sbyor kha dang / rdo rje las kyi tshogs kyi rim pa phyi ba'i cho ga rnams bzhugs s+ho// / bI bi ma sbyor kha chen po'i man drug dang / gtor ma'i tshig dang
61a4(dkar chag): tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor kha dang / zhi ba dang / rgyas pa dang / dbang dang / drag po dang bsdus pa'i las kyi sbyor kha dang / gos sngon po can gyi sbyin sreg gi cho ga dang / maN+Dal gyi cho ga rnams slob dpon b+hA
61a5(dkar chag): babA pas mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba gzhon nu tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ las kyi rim pa mu tig phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dro bon b+ha ba pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta b+h+yor+ya gu ba sU tra dang / lo tsA ba gzhon nu tshul khrums kyi 'gyur/
61a6(dkar chag): rdo rje lce dbab kyi 'grel pa mu tig phreng ba zhes bya ba dang / lce dbab kyi gsang ba yang bkol gyi sgrub thabs gnyis rgyal bu sprin gyi shugs can gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza ya A kA ra ding / lo tsA ba mar pa'i
61b1(dkar chag): 'gyur/ rnal 'byor gyi spyod lam brgyad pa mdzad byang 'gyur byang gong dang 'dra/ nag po pas mdzad pa'i phyag rdor sgrub thabs/ gtum po lha lnga'i sbyor la/ gtum po lha lnga'i dkyil cho ga slob dpon klu sgrub kyis
61b2(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ phyag na rdo rje'i lam yan lag brgyud pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa dang gnyis so// gtum po khyod gsha ma ma'i sgor la/ lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi sgrub thebs nung sgrub ying bzhin nor tha~M zhes
61b3(dkar chag): bya ba dang / phyag na rdo rje'i sgrub thabs gsang ba thugs kyi phur gcig ma gnyis/ paN+Di ta las kyi rje rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta wa la tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba glan chung ngar ma tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ rig sngags
61b4(dkar chag): bcad pA dang minan pa'i tshig sbyin sreg mdor bsdus/ klu gtor rgyas pa rnams glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ gtum chung khra ci thogs ma'i sgrub thabs rgyal po zla ba'i snying pos mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba sgeg pa'i
61b5(dkar chag): dpal gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje khyung gi spro ba thabs slob dpon rdo rje pad+mas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sa'i snying po dang / rma ban gyi 'gyur/ gtum po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bzang po mdor bsdus pa zhes bya ba slob dpon las kyi
61b6(dkar chag): rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ti zla ba ba zang po dang / lo tsA ba glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ phyag na rdo rje be con mor grags pa'i skor la/ lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rnam par bshad pa sgron
62a1(dkar chag): ma gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa/ be con can gyi rgyud kyi 'grel pa rtog pa thams cad bsdus pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon shrI b+hA dras mdzad pa/ lag na rdo rje
62a2(dkar chag): gos sngon po can gyi rgyud rgya cher bshad pa slob dpon mchog rab snying pos mdzad pa/ lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi rgyud kyi rgya cher bshad pa rtog pa drug pa zhes bya ba 'di rgyud du yang 'dod do// de kho na nyid sgron ma zhes
62a3(dkar chag): bya ba/ phyag na rdo rje'i sgrub thabs thams cad rdzogs pa'i rgyan slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pad+ma 'byung gnas dang / lo tsA ba grangs dpal gyi seng ge'i 'gyur/ dpal gos sngon po can gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga
62a4(dkar chag): dong / sngogs kyi rgyan dang / rab gnas kyi rgyan dang gsum/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ gtor ma'i rgyun klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa/ dam tshig gi rgyan/ lag na rdo rje gros sngon po can gyi sgrub thabs/ slob dpon
62a5(dkar chag): klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa/ de'i 'grel po/ sngags kyi rgyan gyi 'grel pa slob dpon mchog rab kyis mdzod pa/ dam tshig gi rgyan gyi bshad pa slob dpon mchog rab kyis mdzad pa/ zangs dkar tshul khrims gzhon
62a6(dkar chag): nu'i 'gyur/ gos sngon po can gyi sgrub thabs kyi man ngag rgya cher bshad pa/ de kho na nyid sgron ma zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs rdzogs pa dang / de'i 'grel pa slob dpon dpa' bos byin gyis mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so//
62b1(dkar chag): phyag na rdo rje rnal 'byor chen por bkral ba'i sgor 'di dag la the tshom za ba'i gzhi mang du snang yang / bod na grags pa can du 'dug pas bris so// 'khor chen gtum po btson la sogs pa// phyag na rdo rje rnal 'byor bla med
62b2(dkar chag): dudagongs pa bkrol ba'i rgyud 'grel sgrub skor sogs// bcu phrag drug la lnga yis brgyan pa bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag srid zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/ phyag na rdo rje rnal 'byor bla med
62b3(dkar chag): du bkral ba'i sgor gyi le'u ste bcu bzhi pa'o// // de ltar thabs kyi rgyud dang / shes rab kyi rgyud dang / thabs shes rab gnyis su med pa'i rgyud kyi so so'i bstan bcos rnams bkod nas/ da ni rnal 'byor
62b4(dkar chag): bla na med pa'i rgyud spyi'i dgongs 'grel gyi skor la// / mi pa la don dam pa'i yi ge gsum dang ldan pa'i rgyud kyi don nges par bsdus pa/ dpal gsang ba grub pa zhes bya ba grub thob chen po pad+ma
62b5(dkar chag): badz+ra sa mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA kr-iSh+Na pa dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ slob dpon de'i slob ma slob dpon yan lag med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa thabs shes rab gtan la dbab pa grub pa/ paN+Di ta b+ha dra dang / lo
62b6(dkar chag): tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi'igyur/ gzhung de gnyis la brten nas/ slob dpon de'i slob ma rgyal po in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa'i ye shes grub pa/ rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba/ slad kyis nag chos bcos so// gzhung de
63a1(dkar chag): rnams la brten nas slob dpon de'i slob ma lham+b+ha lan+thi ka ras mdzad pa'i gnyis sku med par grub bya/ gzhung de rnams la brten nas l+h+wam gyi slob mya slob dpon sgeg pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i dngos pa/
63a2(dkar chag): gsal ba grub pa/ slob dpon de'i slob mu slob dpon dA ri ka pas mdzad pa'i ze gsang ba chen po de kho na nyid kyi man ngage slob dpon de'i slob ma lhan cig skyes pa'i rnal 'byor ma tsai tos mdzad pa'i dngos po gsal ba'i
63a3(dkar chag): rjes su 'gro ba'i de kho na nyid grub pa/ paN+Di ta zhi ba bzang po dang / lo tsA ba 'gros lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje'i slob ma slob dpon DoM bi pas mdzad pa'i lhan cig skyes grub de rnams la grub pa sde brgyad ces grags
63a4(dkar chag): so// rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal sa ra ha pa chen pos mdzad pa'i do ha mdzod ces bya ba/ de kho na nyid rnal du mtshon pa don dam pa'i yi ge slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i phyag rgya bzhi gtan la dbab pa/ paN+Di ta d+ha ri/
63a5(dkar chag): shrI dz+nyA ne dang / lo tsA ba rmya ba ni chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ 'di man ngag snye ma la sogs par slob dpon klu sgrub kyis byas pa ma yin te/ so so'i skye bo man ngag mo shes pa kha cig gis byas so zhes bshad mod kyi 'on kyang
63a6(dkar chag): rgya gar ma yin cing / bod la grags pa gtso bor byas nas bris so// slob dpon klu sgrub kyis Ar+ya ngo ba la bshad cing / nges sems kyi sgrib sbyong mdzad de gong du bris so// de ba tsan+das mdzad pa'i shes rab ye shes
63b1(dkar chag): gsal ba zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / lo tsA ba d+harma kIrti'i 'gyur/ slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i gnas pa bsdus pa zhes bya ba paN+Di ta d+hu ri shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA barma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur la/
63b2(dkar chag): paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / ba rog thos pa dgas bcos pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rim pa'i mno ngag ces bya ba slob dpon tog tse pas mi dzAd pa/ pAN+Di ta bde ba'i myu gu dang / lo tsA ba 'gos kyi 'gyur te de ltar lnga dang /
63b3(dkar chag): sems kyi sgrib sbyong dang bcas pa'i drug po de la snying po'i skor zhes grags so// tha snyad du chos spyod yod por ston pa lta ba ngan sel/ paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang lo tsA be mtshur ston ye shes 'byung gnas kyi 'gyur/ sngags
63b4(dkar chag): kyi lta ba ston pa dbu ma drug pa paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / lo tsA ba d+harma kIrti'i 'gyur/ lte ba ngan sel gyi dka' 'grel dran pa badz+ra pA Ni dang / mtshur gyi 'gyur/ sngags kyi spyod pa ston pa lhan skyes grub pa paN+Di ti badz+re pA
63b5(dkar chag): NI dang / mtshur gyi 'gyur/ lta ba dpas ston pa rmi lam nges bstan/ spyod pa dpes ston pa sgyu ma nges bstam lta ba'i don gtan la 'bebs pa rab tu mi gnas pa gsal bar ston pa gsum paN+Di te badz+ra pA Ni dang / nag tsho tshul rgyal
63b6(dkar chag): gyi 'gyur/ spyod pa gtan la 'bebs pa de kho na nyid bcu pa/ paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang kho mtshur gyi 'gyur la/ nag tsho tshul rgyal gyis bcos pa/ thabs shes rab dbyer meng du ston pa zung 'jug rab tu gsal bar ston/
64a1(dkar chag): pa/ badz+ra pA Ni dang / nag tsho tshul rgyal gyi 'gyur/ snang stong dbyer med du ston pa dga' bcu lnga pa/ badz+ra pA Ni dang / rma ban gyi 'gyur/ 'khor 'das gnyis med du ston pa mi phyed pa lnga pa dang /
64a2(dkar chag): bden gnyis tha mi dad du ston pa'i bde chen gsal ba dang gnyis paN+Di ti badz+ra bI Ni dang / rma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ theg pa thun mong gi lta ba ston pa de kho na nyid rin po che'i phreng ba badz+ra pA NaM dang / nag tsho tshul rgyal
64a3(dkar chag): gyi 'gyur/ gang zag gsum gyi rtog thabs ston pa/ de kho na nyid rab tu bstan pa dang / lha'i rnal 'byor gtan la 'bebs pa de bzhin gshegs pa lnga'i phyag rgya rnam par bshad pa gnyis/ paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang /
64a4(dkar chag): lo tsA ba rmA ban chos 'brur gyi 'gyur/ dbang gi dgos pa mdor bsdus/ paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / lo tsA bI mtshur ston gyi 'gyur/ dbang gi bya ba mdor bsdus pa gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ rdo rje sems dpa'i rang bzhin
64a5(dkar chag): lnga pe/ slob dpon gnyis meng rdo rjes mdzad pa/ thabs dang sha~MshaM sa rab brtse ba lnga pa slob dpon gnyis ming rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / lo tsI ba mtshur dz+nyA na A kA ra'i 'gyur/ 'di a ma nas kyi sbyor du mi
64a6(dkar chag): bgreng bar snang / d+ho ba ti zhes bya ba'i de kho na nyid kyi man ngag a ba d+hU tI pas mdzad pe/ d+hi ri shI dz+nyA na'i 'gyur/ gang zag gsum gyi sgom thabs ston pa theg chen nyi shu ba/ paN+Di tang ba A kA ra tsan+d+ra dang / mo tsA ba shA
64b1(dkar chag): brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/ yid la mi byed pa'i sgra la rtsod pa spong ba yid la mi byed pa ston pa/ badz+ra pA NI dang / lo tsA ba gnyen chung gi 'gyur/ mtha' bral rtogs pa'i shes rab ston pa de kho na nyid theg chen nyi shu pa/ paN+Di ta/
64b2(dkar chag): d+hi ri shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba 'bro seng dkar shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ shes pa spro bsdu myed par 'jog pa'i mun ngag gsang ba dam bA/ 'odi gzhan rnam grangs su mI bgrang bar smyung / dbang gi khyad par gtan la 'bebs pa
64b3(dkar chag): dbang bskur nges bstan kr-iSh+Na paN+Di ta dang / lo tsA bA tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur ni chos sgra nyi shu rtsa gnyis po de mnga' bdag maM tri pa/ mtshan gyi rnam grangs gnyis med rdo rje zhis kyang bya/ a waM d+hU tI pa zhes kyang bya bas
64b4(dkar chag): mdzad pa'i// de'i rjes su 'byung ba bkras bskur ba'i chos bzhi lo/ dbang bskur nges bstan gyi dka' 'grel dpal slob dpon dga' ba skyong gis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sa man+ta b+ha drA dang / lo tsA ba nag tshe'i 'gyur/ de kho na nyid
64b5(dkar chag): bAbacu pa'i 'grelnga pa slob dpon lhan cig skyes pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ka l+yA nA warma dang / mo tsA ba mtshur ye shes 'byung gnas kyi 'gyu ro/ pAN+Di tA badz+ra pA Nis mdzad pa'i rdo rje'i tshig/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang mtshur gyi 'gyur/
64b6(dkar chag): paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Nis mdzad pa'i lte ba ngan sel gyi dran pa ni ma rnyed de/ de ltar chos sna nyi shu rtsa drug la a ma na se ka ri'i skor zhes grags so// 'di ni gsang ba grub pa gsang 'dus kyi don 'grel yin pas de'i phyogasu
65a1(dkar chag): rigs kyang / bod na grub snying a mA na se'i sgor zhes bshad bka' dang / man ngag gi bka' phyogs gcig tu yod pas 'dir lhan cig tu bris so// da ni de dag gi 'grel pa'i skor la/ do ha
65a2(dkar chag): mdzod kyi dka' 'grel slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrI bai ro tsa na'i rang 'gyur/ mi zad pa'i gter mdzod yongs su gang ba'i glu'i rgya cher bshad pa dpal gnyis su med pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bsod
65a3(dkar chag): snyoms pa pradz+nyA brI dz+nyA nakr-iN+Do'i rlung 'gyur/ ngo hi mdzod kyi dka' 'grel slob dpon thar pa'i 'byung gnas pas mdzad pa/ prAd+d+hi tA rgyal ba'i lha dang / rgyu lo tsA'i 'gyur/ phyag rgya bzhi'i 'grel pa b+h+ra ma bi tA krArma sa mdzu pA/
65a4(dkar chag): bsod snyoms pa prad+d+ha shrI dz+nyA na k+Shirti'i rlung 'gyur/ dwA ri ka pas mdzad pa'i grub mtha' bdun pa/ rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta nags kyi rin tshon dang / rjes thang lo tsA ba'i 'gyuraro/ dbang bzhi pa'i rab tu byed pa paN+Di ta nags kyi rin
65a5(dkar chag): chen gyis mdzad pa byams pa gling ba'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / tsa~M pa laM lhan cig skyes grub rgyal po in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA zla ba mgon po dang / lo tsA ba shes rab glags kyi
65a6(dkar chag): 'gyur/ lhan cig skyes grub kyi gzhung 'grel lha lcam btsun ma dpal mos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma na b+hi ha la la dang / lo tsA ba pradz+nyA kIrti'i rang 'gyur/ slob dpon ke ri li pas mdzad pa'i de kho na nyid grub pa 'di gsum
65b1(dkar chag): kha cig grub pa'i skor du rtogs par 'dong ngo // da ni de dag dang phyogs mthun pa phyag rgya chen po ston pa'i gzhung ngo ha la sogs pa'i skor la/ ngo ha mdzod ces bya bya spyod pa'i glu dang / mi zad pa'i gter mdzod man ngag ge glu

66a1(dkar chag): snga nas gsungs pa/ dngos po sbyong ba zhes bya ba/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / lo tsA ba rma ba na chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzud pa'i tshogs su

66a5(dkar chag): pa la chu bo gang+gA'i 'gram du gsungs pa/ bdud rtsi grub pa'i rtsa ba zhes bya ba birba pas mdzad pa/ rgya gar e na de ba'i 'gyur/ mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyi brda gdung ba bcad pa'i man drug ces bya ba sprul pa'i rnal 'byor pas gzhung
66a6(dkar chag): du bkod pa/ phyag rgya chen po rdo rje'i glu brda rgyud gsang ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba dpal sha ba ri dbang phyug dang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma ye shes kyi spyan dang / pad+ma'i spyan gnyis kyi snying po'i don mgur du bzhos pa/ nA ro
66b1(dkar chag): pa'i rdo rje'i g+hu chu gnyis/ nag po pa'i rdo rje'i glu/ grub thob brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i rtog pa'i snying po zhes bya ba grub thob dpa' bo 'od gsal gyis phyogs gcig tu bsdus pa dang / grub thob rnams kyi gru phyogs gcig tu bsdus

67a1(dkar chag): dpag med kyis mdzad pa gnyis/ shrI ba ro tsa na badz+ra'i 'gyur/ 'khor ba las yid nges par 'byung ba'i glu jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA de nyid dang / lo tsA brgya brtson seng gi 'gyur/ skud nas paN+Di

67a3(dkar chag): pa gsung gi sgron ma/ yang dag lta ba'i sgron ma/ rin po che bsgom pa'i sgron ma/ mnyam pa nyid bzhi'i sgron ma/ mthar thug 'bras bu'i sgron ma/ byang chub spyod pa'i sgron ma/ rnal 'byor lam gyi sgron ma/ gsang ba thugs kyi
67a4(dkar chag): sgron ma/ maN+Dal dbul ba'i cho ga/ phyag rgya chen po yi ge med pa'i man ngag/ bskyed rim gyi skor la/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin mo'i sgrub thobs/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thubs/
67a5(dkar chag): 'jam dpal khro bor sgrub pa'i thabs/ de rnams thams cad rje btsun ka ma l+ya shrIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dz+nyA na gu h+ya dang / ong l-i tsA ba'i 'gyur rnams so// / chi ba la lhan cig skyes pa'i glu/ rnal

67b4(dkar chag): pa/ rdo rje bzhi'i g+hu a wa d+hU tI gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ bla ma mai tri ti'i glu/ sa rau ha'i glu/ yang sa ra tA'i glu/ bi ru byed pa'i glu/ kA na ba'i glu/ bla ma rje btsun d+hiSh+Thi dz+nyA nas mdzad pa'i rdo rje'i glu gnyis/ yang glu
67b5(dkar chag): gcig/ kar+Na ri'i glu/ ma'i two tsi tra'i glu/ yang glu gnyis/ dpa' bo rnam par snang mdzad kyi glu/ nA ro paN+Di ta'i glu/ lU i pa'i glu/ DoM bi pa'i glu/ bi rU pa'i glu/ lnga ba pa'i glu/ ma hA su kha ta'i glu/ rnal 'byor pA pra
67b6(dkar chag): sa ra'i glu/ klu sgrub kyi glu/ dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na'i chos kyi glu/ ngo ha spyod pa'i glu'i lta ba slob dpon ki ra pas gsungs pa/ stong pa nyid kyi lta pha slob da pon shaM ba ri pas gsungs pa/ bde sdug gnyis bral gyi lta
68a1(dkar chag): ba slob dpon shAn+ti pas mdzad pa/ 'brel med kyi lta ba slob dpon ka b+ha las mdzad pa rnams/ bla ma rat+na pha la'i rang 'gyur/ zhen med kyi lta ba slob dpon kaM b+ha las mdzad pa/ stong nyid
68a2(dkar chag): snying rje'i lta ba slob dpon tsa ta pas mdzad pa/ sems nyid rin chen gyi lta ba slob dpon d+he ta nas mdzad pa/ de nyid brgyad kyi lta ba slob dpon in+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa/ sems kyi rtog pa 'joms pa'i lta ba slob dpon lak+Sh+mI
68a3(dkar chag): gsungs pa/ mya ngan gyi lta ba d+ha'u ris mdzad pa/ sems tsam gyi lta ba slob dpon mai tri pas gsungs pa/ snying rje spyod pa thod pa'i lta ba slob dpo ni sa ra b+ha khas mdzad pa/ 'brel med kyi lta ba slob dpon nag po bas
68a4(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ de bzhin nyid kyi lta ba slob dpon dA ri ka pas mdzad pa'o// thig le bcu drug gi nyams len slob dpon DA kaM ka li pas mdzad pa/ byang chub kyi sems bcing ba'i man ngag slob dpon mi na pas mdzad pa/ rlung
68a5(dkar chag): gi de nyid sgom pa'i man ngag slob dpon g+ho ra Shas mdzad pa/ rlung gi de nyid bsgom pa'i man ngag slob dpon tso rang gis mdzad pa/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rdzogs pa'i rim pa/ slob dpon b+hi na pas mdzad rnal 'byor
68a6(dkar chag): bzhi'i nyams len slob dpon tan+ti pas mdzad pa/ thabs dang shes rab gtan la phab pa'i dngos grub bsdus pa slob dpon tsam ris gsungs pa/ rang bzhin grub pa med pa gzhi'i man ngag slob dpon kla sgrub kyis
68b1(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ rje btsun yi ge brgya pa'i sems dpa' gsum gyi sgom pa'i thabs slob dpon nA ro pas mdzad pa/ rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba silA a lis mdzad pa/ snying rje sgom pa'i byiHbas te lo pas mdzad pa/ theg pa

68b4(dkar chag): sgom pa'i man ngag slob dpon ku ku rI pas mdzad pa/ 'jog pa gocod pa'i man ngag slob dpon ku dzI pas mdzad pa/ mu stegs kyi gtum mo slob dpon a tsin+tas mdzad pa/ gser 'gyur gyi rtse slob dpon na lis mdzad
68b5(dkar chag): pa/ sems dang sems nyid 'dul ba'i thabs slob dpon me ko las mdzad pa/ lha kun gyi rdzogs pa'i rim pa'i lam g+hA d+ha r-is mdzad pa/ nyi zla bcing ba'i thabs ka ma ris mdzad pa/ sems nyid thig le hUM nyid bsgom

69a3(dkar chag): pa/ rlung gnas kyi nad kyi brtag pa slob dpon a dzo gis mdzad pa/ sems nyid kyi de nyid bcing ba slob dpon ko d+ha lis mdzad pa/ gra tum mo thig le bkram pa slob dpon tsA l-i kis mdzad pa/ lus kyi rtsa thig
69a4(dkar chag): mnyam pa nyid kyi man dag slob dpon ni ku nis mdzad pa/ 'byung bzhi'i sbrid pa'i cha lugs slob dpon tsa ra pA tis mdzad pa/ rang rig ye shes kyi lta ba'i nyams len slob dpon tsam+ba kas mdzad pa/ 'jigs pa

69b3(dkar chag): rnams paN+Di ta rat+na pa la'i rang 'gyur/ phyag rgya chen po brda'i brgyud pa dam pa rgya gar la bde bar gshegs pa bcu gnyis kyis gsungs pa/ zha ma lo tsA'i 'gyuraro// phyag rgya chen po'i man ngag rdo rje gsong ba'i glu rnal
69b4(dkar chag): 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal sa ra his mdzad po/ paN+Di ta ka ma lA shI la dang / lo tsA ba zha ma sed rgyal gyi 'gyur/ dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma'i mgur dang / mkha' 'gro mu'i bAdz+ra'i mgur rje dam pa rgyu gdu la gnang
69b5(dkar chag): bzha ma lho ts+tsha ba'i 'gyur/ thugs kyi gsang ba glur blangs pa thig le dag pa'i phreng ba zhes bya ba/ grub thob po mo brgyad cu'i rtogs brjod/ rje dam po rgya gar dang / zha mA lo tsA'i 'gyur/ grub thob lnga bcu'i rtogs pa
69b6(dkar chag): brjod pa thig mi 'od kyi phreng ba zhes bya ba/ mkha' 'gro ma'i gsang mdzod nas phyung ste rje dam po rgya gar la gnang ba/ zho ma lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ phyag rgya chen po rin po che brda'i man ngag ces bya ba rje dam pa la mkha' 'gro
70a1(dkar chag): mAs gtad pa/ zha ma'i 'gyur la dum bu drug dang / le phran lnga bcu rtsa lnga yod do// mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gsang ba'i glu zhes bya ba/ brul tsho bdun du bstan pa mkha' 'gro ma gsang ba'i mdzod
70a2(dkar chag): na gnas pa las/ dbyings kyi gtso mo rnams kyis bka' bgros nas/ ka ma la shU li la gtad pe/ zha ma seng rgyal gyi 'gyur/ rngon pa chen pas ko ma la shI la la gau nad kyi gdams pa bstan pa zab mo brda'i glu

70a4(dkar chag): thig le gser gyi phreng po zhes bya ba/ ye shos kyi mkha' 'gro ma sum cu rtsa lnga'i rtog pa brjod pa/ mkha' 'gro ma'i gsang mdzad na gnas pas dbyings kyi gtso mo rnams kyis bka' bgros nas rje dam pa rgya gar la

70a6(dkar chag): rgyu sbyar dpal gyi rol par gsungs pa/ rnal 'byor pa thams cad kyi de kho na nyid snang ba zhes bya ba grub pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i mgur/ rje dam pa rgya gor rin po che'i zhal snga nas rang 'gyur du mdzad po/ phyag rgya chen

70b2(dkar chag): rab kyi 'phrin yi ge slob dpon pad+ma badz+ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAn+ta badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lhas bcos kyi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor rtag pa'i gegs sel zhes bya ba slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ dug lnga spras pa'i

70b5(dkar chag): 'di dag mdo phyogs su bris pa ni nor pa yin no// bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa rin po che'i gru bo dang / 'ching ba rnam grol gyi bstan bcos rgyas pa gnyis dpal ni ska laM kas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrI dza ga tA A nan+da
70b6(dkar chag): dang / bud d+ha shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ lta spyod rnam dag gi man ngag/ paN+Di ta shAkya shrIs mdzad pa/ paN chen de nyid dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ sems rin po che sbyong ba'i
71a1(dkar chag): lam 'bras paN+Di ta bud d+hA shrI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa de nyid dang / oM tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'ching ba rnam grol gyi bstan bcos dang / grub pa dmya pA'i lam nges pa dang / rnam
71a2(dkar chag): 'byor pa rang gi sems mdud pa 'grol ba'i mon+ta ngag dang / rnal 'byor bdun gyi lam rnam par nges pa dang / ting nge 'dzin bdun gyi dbang bskur dang / pha rol dbang du bya ba rnams mi tra dzo kIs mdzad pa de nyid dang / khro phu

71a6(dkar chag): theg pa rtsa ba'i ltung ba bsdus pa dang / ltung ba sbom po bsdus pa gnyis slob dpon rta de 'byangs kyis mdzad pa/ ltung ba bco lnga pa dang / yan lag gi nyes pa bdun pa/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i sbom po'i

71b6(dkar chag): ga snying po'i rgyan zhes bya ba slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma na ka shrI dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta ha so badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba nyi ma rdo rjes bcos pa/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i
72a1(dkar chag): cho ga slob dpon a b+ha yA kA ra gup+tas mdzad pa/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa de nyid dang / 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ tshogs kyi 'khor mo'i

73a1(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ slob dpon d+harmA kir+t+tis mdzad pa'i thig gi cho ga/ khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi dum bu las 'phros pa 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i rtog pa'i 'grel pa slob dpon

73b3(dkar chag): rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / rgyud 'dzi rje snying po rgyan gyi rgyud las rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud du gsungs kyang / 'grel pa mkhan pos rnal 'byor gyi rgyud du bkram

74a1(dkar chag): sems dpa'i sgrub thabs gnyis slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud d+ha shrI shAn+ti dang / lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ khams gsum rnam par rgyal ba'i dkyil

74a4(dkar chag): che ba 'dri the tshom gyi gzhi zhig snang ste/ bla ma rnams yang dog tu bzhed kyi snang bas bris so// thugs rje 'byung ba'i bsgom bzlas zhes bya ba slob dpon ye shes rdo rje ming gzhan pad+ma dkar po zhes bya bas mdzad

74a6(dkar chag): bskyangs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrad d+hA ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ dpal ldan rgya che ba zhes bya ba'i dkyil tshig/ kun tu bzang po zhes bya ba'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga rab tu gnas pa'i
74b1(dkar chag): cho ga rab gnas kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba/ rdo rje 'byung ba'i 'grel pa rdo rje 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i don bsdus pa zhes bya ba slob dpon mu nin+d+ra b+ha dras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/
74b2(dkar chag): rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor gyi don bsgom pa'i don bsdus pa/ ku mA ra ka la sha'i 'gyur/ bya ba bsdus pa zhes bya ba slob dpon rigs kyi byin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kIrti tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan
74b3(dkar chag): gyi 'gyur/ 'di rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga yin pas 'dir bris so// de nyid bsdus pa dpal mchog dang po dang // sgyu 'phrul dra ba la sogs dgongs 'grel pa'i// mkhas grub gsum gyi gzhung lugs
74b4(dkar chag): rjes 'brang bcas// bcu phyag gnyis la bdun gyis brgyan pa bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chug srid zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/ rnal 'byor gyi rgyud de nyid bsdus pa dang / dpal mchog
74b5(dkar chag): dang / sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i skor gyi le'u bcu drug pa'o// / rtsa ba'i rgyud de nyid bsdus pa'i rdo rje dbyings kyi dum bu las 'phros pa mtshan yang dag par brjod pa rnal 'byor gyi rgyud du bkral ba'i skor la/
74b6(dkar chag): si pa la mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa 'grel chu nga zhes grags pa/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha kA ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang
75a1(dkar chag): po'i 'gyur/ 'grel pa bar ma mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rgya cher bshad pa mtshan gsang sngags kyi don du rnam par lta ba zhes bya ba slob dpon sgeg pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa sh+lo ka
75a2(dkar chag): nyis stong lnga brgya pa/ smr-i ti'i rang 'gyur la/ phyis paN+Di ta badz+ra pA Ni dang / klog skya shes rab brtsegs kyis bcos pa yang gnyen gyis bcos/ mtshan brjod 'grel tshon slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa/
75a3(dkar chag): praN+Di ta shrad+d+ha kA ra warma nga / ka ma la gup+ta dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / hi pa la mtshan brjod 'grel pa zla ba bzang po grags pa'i dpal gyis mdzad
75a4(dkar chag): papupaN+Di ta shrI ma hA dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa bsdus pa'i gsal ba zhes bya ba or+haN gyi slob dpon A wa d+hU tI pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+harma shrI mi tA dang /
75a5(dkar chag): lo tsA pa 'gar chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa mtshan don gsal bar byed pa zhes bya ba slob dpon gnyis med sbas pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta d+hi rma shrI mi tra dang / lo tsA ba 'gar chos kyi bzang
75a6(dkar chag): po'i 'gyur/ 'jam dpal mtshan brjod kyi bshad 'bum spro tis mdzad pa de nyid kyi rang 'gyur/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i man ngag gi 'grel pa slob dpon gzhon nu grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de ba nA dza
75b1(dkar chag): dang / lo tsA ba shes rab bla ma'i 'gyur/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa gsal ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ bla mya mngon shes can dang / 'gos lhas btsas dang / shwe rab
75b2(dkar chag): brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa tshul gsum gsal bar byed pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/ 'di gnyis rgyud sde spyir bkral bar bya zhing the tshom gyi gzhi'o// mtshan brjod kyi 'grel pa DoM bi he ru kas
75b3(dkar chag): mdzad pa dge tshul khyung grags kyi 'gyur/ 'di'ang the tshom gyi gzhi zhig snang / 'jam dpal gyi 'grel pa rat+na A kA ra gup+ta sa mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta kA la tsakra dang / lo tsA ba dz+nyA na gar+b+ha dang / 'brog jo sras dang / chos
75b4(dkar chag): kyi brtson 'grus la sogs pa'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// de ltar mtshan brjid kyi 'grel pa'i skor rnams bkod nas/ da ni de dag gi rjes su 'brang ba'i sgrub thabs dang / dkyil cho ga dang / man ngag gi skor la/

75b6(dkar chag): ces bya ba rigs bsdus pa'i dkyil cho ga dang / yang dkyil cho ga 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs dang / byang sems rdo rje dbugs 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang / rnam par snang mdzad dbugs

76a2(dkar chag): 'byung ldan dbugs 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang / don yod grub po dbugs 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dang / mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i khrus kyi cho ga/ mtshan brjod kyi chu sbyin dang / zas

76a4(dkar chag): pa bsgom pa'i man ngag/ 'khor ba las yid 'byung ba'i man ngag/ shes pa dus gsum las bzlog pa'i man ngag/ skyabs su 'gro ba'i cho ga/ sems bskyed pa'i cho ga/ byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa'i man ngag
76a5(dkar chag): tshad med pa bzhi bsgom pa'i man ngag/ dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas la lta ba'i man ngag/ dbang po tha mas rjes su dran pa drug bsgom pa'i man ngag/ dbang po 'bring gis rten 'brel yan lag bcu gnyis bsgom
76a6(dkar chag): pa'i man ngag/ dbang po rab kyis de kho na nyid bsgom pa'i man ngag/ sAts+tsha gdab pa'i cho ga/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga bsdus pa/ mnyam par bzhag pa'i rim pa'i man ngag/ dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ mtshan
76b1(dkar chag): brjod kyi cho ga mdo dang bsres pa/ rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga/ ngan sngags byad kyi 'khor los bsad pa'i cho ga/ tshe 'phos pa la phan gdags pa'i bdun tshogs kyi cho ga/ sdig pa sbyong ba'i sbyin sreg ro sreg gi cho ga
76b2(dkar chag): ngan song sbyong ba 'gro ba rigs drug gi cho ga rnams slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa paN+Di ta su badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba gu rub chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'di'i la la rgya gzhung yin min the tshom
76b3(dkar chag): za bar 'du ga na'ang / bla ma gong ma rnams rgya gzhung du bzhed cing / sngar gyi rnams la'ang bris 'dug pas bzhugs su bcug pa yin/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i byang chub sems kyi bsgom
76b4(dkar chag): don bcu gnyis pa tshigs su bcad pa bzhi bcu pa'i 'grel pa/ 'di mdo phyogs su bzhed pa mi 'thad de/ gzhung nas rnal 'byor gyi rgyud du gsal bar gsungs pa'i phyir ro// 'grel pa bar pa'i rjes su 'brangs pa'i skor
76b5(dkar chag): la/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i gsang ba dang ldan pa'i sgrub thabs/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa bklag pa'i sgom kho ga/ rim pa gnyis kyis phye ba'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga rgyas pa/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga yon tan
76b6(dkar chag): 'byung gnas zhes bya ba rnams slob dpon dpal ldan byang chu ba mchog gis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta smai to'i rang 'gyur/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rab gnos kyi cho ga/ slob dpon shAn+ti gar+b+has mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs
77a1(dkar chag): gsang ldan gyi 'grel pa ye shes gsal ba/ sgrub thabs gsang ba ldan pa'i thig gi cho ga rab tu gnas pa dang gsum smr-i tis mdzad cing de nyid kyis rang 'gyur du bsgyur ba/ 'phags pa

77a3(dkar chag): chen gyi skor/ nam kha' dri med che ba'i dkyil cho ga slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrang d+hA ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ de dag dang rjes su mthun pa/ 'jam
77a4(dkar chag): dpal rdo rje 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga sems can thams cad kyi bde ba bskyed pa zhes bya ba rnams bzhugs so// / ku pa la mtshan brjod 'grel pa chung ba'i sgor byang chub sems kyi
77a5(dkar chag): sgom don bcu gnyis pa slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i cho ga mdo dang bsres pa zhes bya ba slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ mtshan
77a6(dkar chag): brjod 'grel pa bar pa'i skar gsang ldan gyi dka' 'grel don bsdus sgron ma zhes bya ba paN+Di ta de ba a kA ra tsan+d+ra dang / klog skya'i 'gyur/ gsang ldan gyi tha yig don bsdus su mdzad pa smr-i tis mdzad pa de nyid
77b1(dkar chag): rang 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi dkyil cho ga skyob dpon shAn+ti gar+b+has mdzad pa smr-i ti'i rang 'gyur/ mtshan brjod kyi sgrub thabs gsang ba'i sgron pa zhes bya ba pradz+nyA gu rus mdzad ba/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'kho
77b2(dkar chag): lo'i rim pa/ mtshan brjod kyi sgrub thabs rdo rje las sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ 'jam dpal gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga yid bzhin nar bu zhes bya ba slob sde dpon zla bzung grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma hA dza na
77b3(dkar chag): dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims gzhi na nu'i 'gyu/ mtsha na brjod 'grel pa a wa d+hU tI pa'i rjes su 'brang ba'i skor la/ dpa sgrub thab so dang / dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga ye shes gsal ba zhes bya ba dang /
77b4(dkar chag): 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa' de kho na nyid kyi sgrub thabs dang gsum/ slob kyi dpon gnyis meng sbas pas mdzad cho ga slob dpon mya dran med pa'i dpal gyis mdzad pa/ 'jam dpal ye
77b5(dkar chag): shes sems dpa' dang po'i sangs rgyas kyi sgrub thubs dang / mchod rten grub pa'i cho ga gnyis slob dpon A wa d+hU tI pas mthor pa/ gas pa 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs paN+Di ta a sho shrI dang / lo ts+tsha ba la zha
77b6(dkar chag): rgya gar brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs/ gshin rje dgra nag gi sgrub thabs/ mi g.yo ba'i sgrub thabs/ gtar cha ga/ spyod lam la sogs pa'i rnal 'byor/ bum pa'i cho ga rnams
78a1(dkar chag): slob dpon mya ngan med pa'i dbul gyis mdzad pa/ ye shes sems dpa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon gnyis med spras pas mdzad pa/ de rnams paN+Di ta d+hArma shrI mi tra dang / lo tsA ba 'gar chos
78a2(dkar chag): bzang gi 'gyur/ 'di'i dgra nag 'dzags byed rnams kyang 'di nyid du bzhugs par bya'i gzhan du mi 'khyar bar bya'o// mtshan brjod kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon mi g.yo seng ges mdzad pa mar pa do ba'i 'gyur/ mtshan
78a3(dkar chag): yang dag par brjod pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon pra b+hA kA ras mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i rgyud kyi sgrub thabs gnyen dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ mtshan

78a5(dkar chag): cad la bstod pa dang bzhi/ paN+Di ta so ma shrIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma hA dze na dong / lo tsA ba gzhon nu 'od kyi 'gyur/ 'jam dpal gyi gtor cho ga gcig rnams so// mtshan yang dag par brjod pa rnal 'byor gyi// rgyud du

78b1(dkar chag): mtshan brjod rnal 'byor gyi rgyud kyi skor du bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu bdun pa'o// / thams cad gsang ba'i rgyud kyi bshad sbyar gsang ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas
78b2(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyo kA ra wa~Mrma dang / lo gr-I bai rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ rtsa rgyud de nyid bsdus pa'i dum bu gnyis pa khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi dum bu las ngan 'gro dgug cing sdig pa sbyang ba lus 'phros pa ngan song
78b3(dkar chag): thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i rgyud kyi skor la/ ngan song yongasu sbyong ba'i rgyud kyi don gyi 'i bru 'grel zhes bya ba slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad zer ba/ 'di paN+Di ta chos gsung ba la lo tsA bas zin bris byas
78b4(dkar chag): pa yin nam yang zer ro// 'phags pa ngan song thams cad yongasu sbyong ba zhes bya ba/ cho ga zhib mo'i rgyal po chen po'i rgya cher 'grel pa snying po rnam par bshad pa zhes bya ba dzA lan+d+ha ra'i slob dpon kA ma d+he nus

78b6(dkar chag): dpon rdo rje go chos mdzad zer bi sh+lo ka drug stong dang bcu bzhi pa dang / ngan song yongs su sbyong ba'i gzi brjid kyi rgyal po'i brtag pa snang ba'i rgyan zhes bya ba'i 'grol ba/ paN+Di ta bIr+ya ka ra warma dang / mo tsA ba dbang phyug
79a1(dkar chag): rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur gnyis bzhugs/ spyod rgyud kyi bshad pa byed lugs cung 'di drug pa 'dra'o// / gu ba la ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i gzi brjid kyi
79a2(dkar chag): rgyal po'i 'grel pa brtag pa bshad pa zhes kyang bya/ gsal ba'i na ma zhes bya ba slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad zer ba/ baN+Di ta ku mU ra kA la sha dang / lo ts+tsha ba khyung po chos brtson gyi 'gyur/ dkyil 'khor
79a3(dkar chag): spyi'i rim pa slob dpon s+yA ra b+hU dras mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA d+har+m+ma shrI b+hU dra dang / lo tsA ba rig po gzhin nu'i 'gyur/ dran song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon kun dga' snying pos
79a4(dkar chag): mdzad zer ba gtsug dgu'i gzhung dang cha 'dra ba/ paN+Di ta smr-i ti'o rang 'gyur zer/ dpe la la na paN+Di ta su b+hU ti shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur zer ba snang ngo // ngan song thams cad yongasu sbyong ba'i rtsa ba'i
79a5(dkar chag): dkyil 'khor chen po'i cho ga thugs rje'i phreng ba zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po kun dga' snying pos mdzad zer ba/ pAN+Di ta ki re NA ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba dge tshul khyed grugs kyi 'gyur/ 'di gnyis sdu ma thung drug par

79b3(dkar chag): sbyo po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga zhes bya ba slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bud d+hA shrI shAn+ti dang / lo tsA bu rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur 'di rtsod med yang dag pa yin no// ngan song thams cad yongs su
79b4(dkar chag): sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i rimo b+hA sgrib dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ many+dzu shrI wArma dang / bran+d+ha ka mU ti'i 'gyur/ ngan song sbyong bya'i ro'i sbyin+da skyeg gi dkyil cho ga slob dban d+harma kIrtis mdzad pa/
79b5(dkar chag): poN+Di ta d+harma pA la dang / lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon kun snying gis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog gi 'grel pa bsnyen pa yan chad rdzogs pa'i 'phro zhig 'dre bong ma 'dra ba zhig 'dug ste/ sngar gyi
79b6(dkar chag): rnams kyis kyang bris pas bris so// ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba zhes bya ba'i cho ga'i bya ba mdor bsdus pa/ rtsa ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i sgrub thabs pa N+Di ti 'gro kun dga' ba bzang
80a1(dkar chag): pos mdzad pa/ mnga' ris pa rdo rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i snying po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bai ro tsa nA rak+Shi ta dang / lo tsA ba glan chung gi
80a2(dkar chag): 'gyur la stag los bcos pa/ de la brten nas slob dpon dA ri bas mdzad pa'i shes rab snying po'i sgrub thabs/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag rdo rje lta bu zhes bya ba slob dpon kem+b+ha las mdzad pa/ dzaM b+ho rje
80a3(dkar chag): dang / dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ de kho na nyid gsal ba'i sgron ma zhes bya ba kam+bu la'i yum gyis mdzad pa/ mdo rgyas 'bring gi gleng gzhi'i sangs rgyas byang sems rnams rnal 'byor rgyud du dgongs pa bkral te/ dkyil
80a4(dkar chag): 'khor la bkod nas ston pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga zhes bya ba slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa dang / de la brten nas slob dpon rat+na kIrtis mdzad pa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin
80a5(dkar chag): pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi tshi ga/ bal po ma hA pA na'i rang 'gyur/ rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga slob dpon dad pa'i 'byung gnas go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA ka na ka wAr+m+ma dang / lo tsA bi pa tshab nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur/ shausau
80a6(dkar chag): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul brgya lnga bcu po rnal 'byor gyi rgyud du dgongs pa bkral ba slob dpon ye shes bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ yi ge brgya pa'i cho ga slob dpon pad+ma'i rdo rje lcags kyus mdzad pa/ yang
80b1(dkar chag): yi ge brgya pa'i cho ga bsdus pa gcig/ bzlas pa'i phreng ba'i mtshan nyid dang / sku khrus kyi cho ga gnyis/ pAN+Di tA pU ra he ta dang / nag tsho shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ gtsug tor dri med kyi gzungs las 'byung ba'i
80b2(dkar chag): mchod rten sgrub pa'i cho ga rnal 'byor gyi rgyud dang bsdebs nas slob dpon zhi ba snying pos mdzad pa/ las kyi sgrib pa thams cad rgyun gcod par byed pa'i gzungs rnal 'byor gyi rgyud du dgongs pa bkrol ba mi 'khrugs pa'i

80b4(dkar chag): chotshe gla jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA bA rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ mi 'khrugs pa'i cho ga'i tho yig slob dpon dpa' bo rdo rje mdzad pa dang / bcom ldan 'das mi 'khrugs pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon
80b5(dkar chag): dze ta ris mdzad pa/ gnyen dAr ma grags kyi 'gyur/ mi 'khrugs pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga ji bo rjes mdzad pa/ rdo rje chos kyi rnal 'byor gcig pa'i sgrub thabs lo chung legs pa'i shes rab kyis bsgyu ra bA 'di mdzad byang
80b6(dkar chag): med pas/ sngar gyi rnams kyis bris 'dug pas bzhugs su bcug pa yon/ rgyan dam pa sna tshogs pa rim par phye ba zhes bya ba'i yo ga'i dkyil cho ga slob dpon s+thi ra ma tis mdzad pa/ bam po gcig pa cog ro klu'i
81a1(dkar chag): rgyul mtshan gyi 'gyur yin zer ba/ 'di rnying ma 'am bong ma zhig yin pa 'dra ste/ sngar gyi rnams kyis kyang bris 'dug pas bzhugs su bcug pa yin no// thams cad gsang ba ngan song
81a2(dkar chag): sbyong rgyud dang // shwer phyin mi 'khrugs pa la sogs pa'i gzhung // 'grel pa dag dang sgrub thabs la sogs skor// bcu phyag gsum la brgyad kyis brgyan pa bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag
81a3(dkar chag): srong zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/ thams cad gsang ba dang ngan song sbyong ba la so gas pa'i skor gyi le'u ste btso brgyad pa'o// // spyod pa'i rgyud kyi skor la// / ngu pa la rtsa ba'i rgyud
81a4(dkar chag): rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyud kyi bsdus don slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shI len+d+ra bo d+hi dang / lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs rak+Shi ta'i 'gyur/ rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byeng
81a5(dkar chag): chub pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ skal bzang rab dgas mdzad pa'i mchod pa'i cho ga piN+Di ta pad+ma kA ra wArma dang rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ rnam par snang mdzad kyi sgrub thabs
81a6(dkar chag): rgyal ba'i 'od kyis mdzad pa rnams bzhugs so// // cu pa la rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa rtses thang lo tsA
81b1(dkar chag): bas bcos pa'i 'gyur/ 'jam dpal gsang rgyud kyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon lha sbas kyi mdzad pa sgrub thabs kun gyi gter zhes bya ba/ paN+Di tA pad+ma ka ra warma dang / lo tsA ba rig pa gzhon nu'i 'gyur/ 'jam
81b2(dkar chag): dpal gsang rgyud kyi dkyil cho ga slob dpon don yod zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs khro bo gshin rje gshed kyi sbyin sreg gi rim pa dang / dngos grub kyi tshul nges par bsten pa slob dpon
81b3(dkar chag): don yod zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ khro bo rnam par rgyal ba'i rtog pa gsang ba'i rgyud kyi rgya cher ba shad pa gsham ma tshang ba gcig rnams bzhugs so// rnam snang ma ngon byung rgyud kyi 'grel pa gnyis// 'jam
81b4(dkar chag): dpal gsang ba'i rgyud kyi chos skor bzhi// khro bo rnam rgyal rtog pa'i 'grel pa gci ga/ spyod pa'i rgyud kyi chos skor bdun bzhugs so// / bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag
81b5(dkar chag): sring zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/ spyod pa'i rgyud kyi skor gyi le'u ste bcu dgu pa'o// ba'i rgyud kyi skor la// // chu ba la bya ba spyi'i rgyud bsam gtan phyi ma rim par phye ba'i bshad pa slob dpon
81b6(dkar chag): sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bid+yA kaM ra pra b+hA dang / lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ dpung bzang gis zhus pa'i rgyud kyi bsdus doni slo ba dpon sangs rgyaso gsang bas mdzad pa/ dpung bzeng gis
82a1(dkar chag): zhus pa'i rgyud kyi tshig don bshad pa'i brjed byang / dpung bzang gis zhus pa'i rgyud kyi bsdus pa'i don dgrol ba'i brjed byung / 'di bod kyi byas pa yIn+d+ra nam sems/ so so'i dgongs
82a2(dkar chag): 'grel la/ dang po sku'i rigs 'jam da pal gyi sbyor la/ 'jam dpal dpa' bo gcig sgrub kyi 'grel pa/ paN+Di ti su b+hA kA ras mdzad pa/ dA ne shI la'i rang 'gyur/ gsung gi rigs thugs rje chen po'i skor gyi
82a3(dkar chag): 'grel pa ni mi snang ngo // thugs kyi rigs phyag na rdo rje'i skor la/ phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can gyi gzungs kyi 'grel pa zhes bya ba slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ jo bo rje dang / nag tshe tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/
82a4(dkar chag): phyag na rdo rje'i gzungs kyi 'grel ba paN+Di to karma badz+ras mdzad pa/ phyag na rdo rje dang phyogs mthun pa rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyiskor la/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi 'grol pa mkhan po po
82a5(dkar chag): d+his twas mdzad pa de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa rdo rje sgron ma zhes bya ba slob dpon pad+ma 'byung gnas kyis mdzad pa/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i
82a6(dkar chag): gzungs kyi 'grel pa rin chen gsal ba zhes bya ba slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dpal many+dzu shrI'i 'gyur la/ slad kyis paN+Di ta 'byon te ta du la dang / lo tsA ba dang 'og
82b1(dkar chag): bsod nams mos pa'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi don rnam par phye ste bshad pa zhes bya ba dang / de'i rgya cher 'grel pa gnyis/ slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i
82b2(dkar chag): gzungs kyi 'grel pa slob dpon rdo rje go chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shrad+d+ha ka ra wAr+m+ma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi don rnam par bshad pa slob dpon bde ba'i myu gus
82b3(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa rnam par 'joms pa'i man ngag ces bya ba smr-i tis mdzad pa de nyid kyi rang 'gyur/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa rin po che'i phreng ba
82b4(dkar chag): zhes bya ba slob dpon sa pa ri pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de ba pur+Na ma ti dang / lo tsA ba 'gar chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs rim par phye ba'i rgya cher 'grel pa gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya
82b5(dkar chag): ba slob dpon ye shes rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta sangs rgyas gsang ba dang / lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur la/ shrad+d+ha dang rin chen bzang pos bcos zer ba/ de dog dang 'brel pa'i gtsug tor la sogs pa'i gzung
82b6(dkar chag): kyi skor la/ kun nas sgor 'jug pa'i 'od zer gtsug tor dri ma med par snang ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po dang dam tshig la rnam par lta ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon lhan
83a1(dkar chag): cig skyes pa'i rol pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza ya de wa dang / lo tsA ba langs ban+de tshul khrims brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar can gyi 'grel pa/ slob dpon shu rang ga ma
83a2(dkar chag): badz+ras mdzad pa/ zangs dkar 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / dzu pa la stong chen mo rab tu 'joms pa'i 'bum 'grel/ rma bya chen mo'i 'bum 'grel/ gsang sngags rjes su
83a3(dkar chag): 'dzin pa'i mdo'i 'bum 'grel/ bsil ba'i tshal gyi mdo'i 'bum 'grel rnams slob dpon las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta don yod rdo rje'i rang 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// / nyu pa la sgo drug
83a4(dkar chag): pa'i gzungs kyi rnam par bshad pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ sgro mtha' yas pa bsgrub pa'i gzungs kyi rnam par bshad pa tshig le'ur byas pa dang / sgo mtha' yas pa bsgrub pa'i gzungs kyi rgya cher 'grel
83a5(dkar chag): pa/ slob dpon ye shes snying pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA wArma dang / lo tsA bA ban+de ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ chos spyod thams cad kyi mngon par rtogs pa'i man+da ngag gi rgyud kyi 'grelnga pa gzi bI rjid snang ba zhes bya ba klu'i dbang
83a6(dkar chag): phyug gis mdzad pa/ dge tshul khyung grags kyi 'gyur/ 'di rtsa 'grel gnyi ga rdzun ma yang dag pa gcig 'dug ste/ nag tsho lo tsA ba yang dag tu bzhed pa yin zer nas sngar gyi rnams kyi bris 'dug pas 'odi yang bzhugs
83b1(dkar chag): su bcug pa yin/ de ltar bya ba'i rgyud so so'i 'grel pa rnams bkod nas/ da ni de dag gi sgrub thabs dkyil cho ga la sogs pa'i sgor la/ bya ba'i rgyud kyi lha sum tshan lngar grags pa las/ drang po rigs kyi gtsu
83b2(dkar chag): gsum la/ sku'i rigs kyi gtso bo rnam par snang mdzad yin pas/ dri dang phyogs mthun pa/ dam tshig gsum bkod pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po'i yi ge brgya pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon ke d+hA ra Na d+his mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA dpal
83b3(dkar chag): go mi 'chi med dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'di spyod pa'i rgyud dang bskyed cho ga rnams mthun par bkod 'dug na'ing / rgyud 'grel dag las dam tshig gsum bkod bya rgyud du gsungs 'dug pas 'dir bris
83b4(dkar chag): so// gsung gi rigs kyi gtso bo che dpag med kyi skor la/ tshe dpog med kyi bstod pa/ tshe dpag med kyi sgrub thabs/ tshe dpag med kyi gzungs cho ga rnams slob dpon dze ta ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa/ baN+Di
83b5(dkar chag): ta shrI many+dzu dang / lo tsA ba lce dga' ba'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ rigs kyi bdag po gsum la/ sku'i rigs kyi bdag po 'jam dpal gyi skor la/ 'jam dpal rdo rje blo glos 'phel ba zhes bya ba 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzod
83b6(dkar chag): pa/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi dpyad 'phags pa lhas mdzad pa sh+lo ka brgya pa/ 'jam dpal dpa' bo gcig sgrub slob dpon mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ de nyid dang lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ 'jam
84a1(dkar chag): dpal shes rab 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta zla ba'i 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'dzum dpal g.yo ba'i 'khor
84a2(dkar chag): lho'i man ngag paN chen shAkya shrIs mdzad pa/ ngag gi dbang phyug la bu mo brgyad kyis bstod pa dang / 'phags pa 'dzum dpal la khye'u bcu drug gi bstod pa dang / ngag gi dbang phyug gtso 'khor lnga pa'i bstod pa
84a3(dkar chag): thig le bum pas mdzad pa/ gur gum gzhon nu lta bu'i bstod pa/ slob dpon seng ge mi g.yo bas mdzad pa rnams ni jo bo rje dang / nag tsho'i 'gyur/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi bstod pa byin rlabs dang bcas pa zhes bya ba
84a4(dkar chag): slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta su ma ti kIrti dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab dang / mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gi 'gyur/ dpal ye shes yon tan bzang po zhes bya ba'i bstod pa slob dpon rdo rje mtshon
84a5(dkar chag): chas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta 'bum phrag gsum pa dang / rdog lo tsA bA'i 'gyur/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi bstod pa yang dag pa'i 'khor lo zhes bya ba slob dpon phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa/ a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs
84a6(dkar chag): kyi cho ga slob dpon shrad+d+ha ka ra warmas mdzad pa/ a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs slob dpon mi pham bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta bi b+hU ti tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'jam dpal
84b1(dkar chag): dkar po'i sgrub thabs slob dpon ma tis mdzad pa/ d+ha na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ a ra pa tsa nA'i mchod cho ga nyi ma rgya lnga mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ gsung gi rigs kyi bdag po thugs rje chen po'i sgor la/ don
84b2(dkar chag): yod zhagasapa lha lnga'i bstod pa slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi bstod pa yid 'phrog sdig 'joms zhes bya ba slob dpon tsan+d+ra gau mis mdzad pa/ dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur/ don yod zhags
84b3(dkar chag): pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha bcu bdun la bstod pa dri ma med pa'i 'od/ 'jig rten mgon po'i bstod pa yid 'phrog sdig 'joms slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dA na shI la'i 'gyur/ thugs rje chen po la
84b4(dkar chag): bstod cing bskul ba nyer bzhi pa slob dpon tsan+d+ra gau mis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pA ra me shwa ra dang / 'gros lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ 'jig rten dbang phyug la bstod pa slob drab ni tsar+ya Di pas mdzad pa/ sgra mkhan chen po
84b5(dkar chag): rgyal ba snyan gyi zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ don zhugs lha lnga'i bstod pa paN+Di tA e re pa tis mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA e mo g+ha badz+ra dang / ba ri rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/ 'phags pa 'jig
84b6(dkar chag): rten dbang phyug la bstod pa grub thob tsan+di pa Tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nags kyi rin chen dang / 'gos lo tsA ba gzhon nu dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi bstod pa snyan ngag mkhan shrI badz+rA de bas mdzad pa/
85a1(dkar chag): paN+Di ta lad+d+hi ka ra dang / shong ston lo tsA'i 'gyur/ 'jig rten dbang phyug lnga bstod pa dge slong ma dpal myos mdzad pa/ nor bu gling gi thugs rje chen po lha lnga la bstod pa zhes bya
85a2(dkar chag): slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ spyan ras gzigs dbang la bstod pa slob dpon tsan+d+he go mis mdzad pa/ thugs rje chen po la smre sngags su gsol ba tsan+d+ra gr-i mIs mdzad pa/ yang smre sngags su gsol
85a3(dkar chag): bya slob dpon zlo ba grags pas mdzad pa/ snying rje la bstod pa dge bsnyen sbyin gyis mdzad pa/ phyag stong spyan stong gi sgrub thabs slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ piN+Di ta dwI paM ka ra dang / lo ts+tsha ba rin chen bzang
85a4(dkar chag): po'i 'gyur/ 'jig rten dbang phyug yi ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs slob dponi pad+mas mdzad pa/ rgyal ba mchog dbyangs kyi 'gyur/ spyan ras gro thigs bcu gcig zhal gyi sgrub thabs dge slong ma dpal mos
85a5(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / moM tsA ba ri na chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la bstod pa dge slong ma zla mdzes kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta tsan+d+ra shrI dang / byams pa gling pa'i 'gyur/
85a6(dkar chag): thugs rje chen po la klu rgyal nor rgyas kyi bus bstod pa/ paN+Di ta nags kyi rin cheno dang / bsod nams rnam par rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ thugs rje chen po'i bstod pa dge slong ma dpal mos mdzad pa/ 'jig rten dbang phyug
85b1(dkar chag): la bstod pa 'jigs pa brgyad skyobs dang / thugs rje chen po la bstod pa dge slong ma dpal mos mdzad pa rnams dang thugs rje chen po'i sgrub thabs brgya rtsa brgyad pa zhes pa la thog mar/ ba saR+Ya Ni'i sgrub
85b2(dkar chag): thabs tshigs bcang bzhi po/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi sgrub thabs thugs rje tshan 'a'i phyi mo slar rnyed mdzong po ye shes sems dpa'i sgrub thabs spyan gzigs 'khor lo gsum bsgom/ thugs rje chen po lha
85b3(dkar chag): lnga'i sgrub thabs 'jig rten mgon po tshe dpag med bzhi'i sgrub thabs/ yi ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs/ sems ngal bso ba'i thugs rje chen po'i sgrub thabs/ thugs rje chen po yi ge med pa'i sgrub thabs/ stong
85b4(dkar chag): pa nyid bsgom pa'i man ngag/ kha sAR+YA Ni me 'bar ba'i sgran thabs/ khA saR+YA NAM sku ga suma? gyi gdams pa/ thugs rje chen po mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs/ na mkha' dri med kyi sgrub thabs/ nu mkha'

85b6(dkar chag): sgrub thabs/ dpal 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i sgrub thabs/ lus kyi 'khor lo 'bar ba dka' thub can gyi sgrub thabs/ rtag tu bya ba'i rnal 'byor/ 'jig rten mgon po sgrub pa'i man ngag/ thugs rje
86a1(dkar chag): chen po'i gtor ma'i cho ga/ thugs rje chen po'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga/ thugs rje chen po'i bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mchod pa'i cho ga/ spyan ras gzigs kyi smon lam du bya ba/ spyan
86a2(dkar chag): ras gzigs bdud rtsi brnyes pa'i zas kyi cho ga/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug shrI mi tra'i gdums pa/ lus sbyin pa'i cho ga/ thugs rje chen po'i chu sbyin gyi cho ga/ thugs rje chen po'i tsha'i gtor gyi cho ga
86a3(dkar chag): mchod pa'i cho ga/ sku gzugs kyi cho ga/ sku gzugs dang / mchod rten gyi cho ga/ ye shes sbyar ba'i gdoms pa/ dri ma rnam dag gi cho ga/ chog nyams gso ba/ ting nge 'dzin myur du bskyed pa'i gdams ngag/
86a4(dkar chag): ting nge 'dzin brtan b+hai ra byed pa'i gdams ngag/ sems brtan par byed pa byin gyis brlab pa mi zad pa'i cho ga/ 'khor lo 'bar ba/ dgu gi mthu bskyed pa'i man ngag/ gsang sdigs myur du 'grub pa'i cho ga/
86a5(dkar chag): rmi lam dri ma med pa'i po sgom pa/ rmi lam gyi lta ba log pa rnam par bzlog po/ khro ba bsel ba/ thugs rje chen po'i gdug pa 'dul ba'i cho ga/ skye bo gdul dka' ba rnams kyi snying gi dregs pa zhi bar byed pa'i
86a6(dkar chag): man ngag/ dpal 'khor lo rnam dag gi sgrub thabs/ snying gi dug sbyong ba/ lus kyi 'khor lo bcing ba dang / 'grol ba'i man ngag/ dpal rdo rje thod pa'i dngos grub sgrub pa'i thabs/ dpal mi 'jigs pa sbyin
86b1(dkar chag): pa'i sgrub thabs/ kha saR+Wa rdzi pad+ma kha 'byed pa'i man ngag/ thugs rje chen po'i gzugs brnyan lnga brten pa'i sgrub thubs/ dpal me tog gdan gyi sgrub thabs/ me tog la brten pa'i sgrub thabs/ spyil bu can
86b2(dkar chag): gyi sgrub thabs/ thugs rje chen+ya po rnga sgra'i sgrub thabs/ nyi zla sgron ma'i cho ga/ grags pa bskyed pa'i cho ga/ gzi brjid bskyed pa'i chog/ sems can mo gu bar byed pa'i cho ga/ rmi lam ston par byed pa/ yid
86b3(dkar chag): rgya da pa bsal ba/ longs spyod mi zad pa sgrub pa'i thabs/ dpag bsam gyi shing can gyi sgrub thabs/ bum pa bzang bo can gyi sgrub thabs/ lam chen po'i sgrub thabs/ 'jig rten dbang phyug wa ti can gyi
86b4(dkar chag): sgrub thabs/ pad+ma'i sdong po can gyi sgrub thabs/ spyan ras gzigs dri ma 'jig pa'i bum pa'i cho ga/ rdo rje 'bar ba srung ba chen po'i man ngag/ srung ba'i 'khoralo/ rang bsrung ba'i cho ga/ ge zhen bskyang ba'i

87a1(dkar chag): pas ser ba bzlog pa'i cho ga/ rmi lam dri ma med pa bsgom pa/ slob ma byin gyis brlab pa'i man ngag/ ye shes gzhug pa'i cho gu ting nge 'dzin gyi byin rlabs/ ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang bskur
87a2(dkar chag): dpal ye shes 'bar ba'i 'khrul 'khor/ skye ba bsdum pa'i cho ga/ 'chi ba blu bya'i gdams pa/ dpal lha'i grong khyer du 'jug pa/ rdo rje skar mda'i man ngag/ tshe 'das pa la bya ba'i cho ga/ ro sreg pa'i cho ga/ sbyin
87a3(dkar chag): sreg gi cho ga/ bkra shis kyi cho ga/ swAts+tsha gdab pa'i tshig/ rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga rnams la brgya dang bzhi'o// 'di dag la rnal 'byor bla med dang / rnal 'byor gyi khongs su gtogs pa'ang snang mod kyi/ thugs
87a4(dkar chag): chen po phyogs gcig tu bya ba'i phyir bris so// thugs rje chen po phyag stong spyan stong gi sgrub thabs ta thA ga ta badz+ras mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nyi ma 'byung gnas zla ba dang / lo tsA ba dge tshul khyung grags kyi 'gyur/ 'jig
87a5(dkar chag): rten dbang phyug yid bzhin nor bu 'khor los sgyur ba'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dzA ta ris mi dzad pa/ paN+Di ta pur+N+Na kIr+t+ti dang / sna nAm rdo rje bla ma'i 'gyur/ 'jig rten dbang phyug zhal gcig phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs
87a6(dkar chag): slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa chag chos rje do pal gyi 'gyur/ yi ge drug pa'i rgyud kyi rim pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo bstan pa'i sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta ma hA dza na dang / lo tsA ba gzhon nu 'od kyi 'gyur/ 'phags
87b1(dkar chag): pa 'jig rten dbang phyug khA saR+YA Ni'i sgrub thabs/ baN+Di tA dI pa ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur/ thugs rje chen po yi ge drug pa'i sgrub thabs pU dza badz+ras mdzad pa jo bo rje dang / lo tsA ba shAkya blo gros

93b2(dkar chag): pas mi bzang pa'i nad yams drag po las thar par byed pa dang / klu sgrub rin po che dbyig sgrub ces bya ba/ klu'i gdon las grol bar byed pa sbrul 'dzin gsang ba zhes bya ba/ klu srog me dpal gyi 'khor lo zhes bya ba/

106a3(dkar chag): dpal 'od zer can pi tsu pa'i sgrub thabs/ 'od zer con gyi sgrub thabs/ 'od zer can gyi sgro ba thabs/ 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs mdor bsdus pa/ de'i gzungs gdon pa'i man ngag/ ri khrod lo ma can gyi sgrub thabs/
106a4(dkar chag): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ 'phags ma ri khrod ma lo ma can gyi gzungs/ dpal nag po chen ba'i sgrub thabs/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma sku mdog ser mo'i sgrub thabs/ nga'i sgrib thabs
106a5(dkar chag): mdor bsdusmra pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyi nA ma dkar mo'i sgrub thabs/ de'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dge 'dun sbyin gyis mdzad pa/ de'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta pad+ma 'phel gyis mdzad pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma gser
106a6(dkar chag): mdog can gyi sgrub thabs/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin mo'i sgrub thabs so/ ser mdog can gyi sher phyin gyi sgrub thabs/ sher byin gyi sgrub thabs 'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa/ 'phags pa rdo rje dbyangs
106b1(dkar chag): can ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon dpa lnga 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ yang rdo rje dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs gsum/ rdo rje pi wang dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs/ yang dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs/ klushin rje ga shed nag po'i rgyud
106b2(dkar chag): las phyung ba'i rdo rje dbyangs can mU'i sgrub thabs/ yang dbyangs can ma'i sgrub thabs/ khro gnyer can gyi sgrub thabs/ yang khro gnyer can gyi sgrub thabs/ sgrol ma'i rtog pa las phyung ba'i ku ru kul+le'i sgrub thabs/
106b3(dkar chag): sgrol mo'i rtog pa las 'byung ba'i tshig lhug pa'i rigs byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ ku ru kul+le'i sgrub thabs slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ ku ru kul+li'i dbang du byed pa'i man ngag/ rigs byed ma'i
106b4(dkar chag): sgrub thabs/ dpal 'phrugs ma rigs byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ oM D+ya Ne nas byung ba'i rigs byed ma'i sgrub thabs/ rigs byed ma'i sgrub thabs lhan cig skyes pa'i rol pas mdzad pa/ kye rdo rje'i rim pa'i ku ru kul+le'i
106b5(dkar chag): sgro ba thabs/ ku ru kul+le'i sgrub thabs/ dpal kye rdo rje'i rgyud las phyung ba/ snyan dngags mkhan tshe na po brtse ba can zhes bya bas tshogs bcad du bstobs pa/ rje btsun ma ku ru kul+le'i phyag drug ma'i sgrub thabs/
106b6(dkar chag): rigs byed ma phyag drug mo'i sgrub thabs/ rigs byed me phyag brgyad mi'i sgrub thabs/ in+d+ra b+hU tis zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ ku ru kul+le'i sgrub thabs/ rigs byed ma'i man ngag gi rim pa/ rigs byed ma daM kar mo'i sgrub
107a1(dkar chag): thabs dpal sgyu 'phrul dra ba rnal 'byor gyi rgyud chen po stong phrag bcu drug pa las 'byung ba ku ru kul+le'i sgrub thabs mchog tu 'gyur ba slob dpon dpal nag po spyod pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ ku ru
107a2(dkar chag): kul+le'i sgrub thabs/ bstod pa las gsungs pa'i ku ru kul+le'i sgrub thabs/ ku ru kul+la'i las rab tu bskyang ba sbyor ba/ gtsu ga tor rnam par rgyal ma'i sgrub thabs/ 'phags ma gzhan gyis mi thub ma gdugs
107a3(dkar chag): dkar mo can gyi sgrub thabs/ rdo rje tsartsi ka'i sgrub thabs/ so sor 'brang ma chen mo'i sgrub thabs gsum/ rma bya chen mo'i sgrub thabs gnyis/ 'phags ma stong chen mo rab tu 'joms pa'i sgrub thabs/ 'phags
107a4(dkar chag): ma gsang sngags tshon mo rjes su 'dzin ma'i sku'i thabs/ bsil ba'i tshal chen mo'i sgra thabs/ lha mo lnga'i sgrub thabs mdo bstan pa/ phyir bzlog ma chen mo'i sgrub thabs/ rgyal mtshan rtse mo 'i dpung rgyan gyi sgrub
107a5(dkar chag): thabs/ gzhan gyis mi thub ma'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje gan+d+ha ri'i sgrub thabs/ bsrung ba lnga 'i cho ga/ rdo rje lcags sgro ga gi sgrub thabs/ man ngag gi rim pa'i nang nas 'o byung ba'i rdo rje lcags sgrog gi sgrub thabs/ rdo rje

107b3(dkar chag): pathabs rgyas pa/ de la chu rgyu na dbul ba'i man ngag gnyis/ dpal rta ma grin gyi sgrub thabs/ slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ rtog pa bdun brgya pa las gsu ngas pa'i rta mgrin gyi sgrub thabs/ rgyud
107b4(dkar chag): thethams cad kyi snying po phyi ma'i rta migrin gyi sgrub thabs/ paN+Di ta pra b+ha kA ras mdzad pa/ 'jig rten gsum las rnam pari rgyal ba'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje me dang nyi ma 'bar ba'i sgrub thabs/ rta mchog gi sgrub thabs/ 'phags

108a1(dkar chag): ka'i sgrub thabs/ dgyes pa'i rdo rje phyag gnyis pa'i sgrub thabs/ bdag med ma'i sgrub thabs gnyis/ dpal 'byung po 'dul byed kyi sgrub thabs mdor bsdus pa/ 'byung po'i 'dul byed kyi
108a2(dkar chag): sgrub thabs kyi cho ga dam pa thams cad mkhyen pa 'jig rten gsum gyi rdo rjes ma dzad pa/ dpal nag po chen po'i sgrub thabs gsum rnams paN+Di ta kIr+No tsan+d+ra'o zhal snga nas zhus na sa/ lo tsA ba glags pa rgyal

108a4(dkar chag): dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon pad+mas mdzad pa/ byams pa'i sgrub thabs pAN chen shAkyai shrIs mdzad pa/ de nyid du lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'phrig
108a5(dkar chag): pa byams pa'i sgrub thabs slob dpon thogs med kyis mdzad pa/ daM ge bshes ston pa'i 'gyur la/ khro phu lo tsA bas bi cos pa/ mi pham mgon pa'i sgrub thabs nai ri ti pas mdzad pa/ lho tsA ba byams pa'i dpral g+hi
108a6(dkar chag): 'gyur/ seng ge sgra'i sgrub thabs/ seng ge sgra'i kha saR+Wa Ni 'jig rten mgon po'i sgrub thabs/ lha mo sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ yum shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma'i sgrub thabs/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rgyal po chen po

108b2(dkar chag): sgrub thabs te bcu gcig po rnams/ slob dpon dri ma me rjod pa'i lhas mdza pa babacu gcig/ lha mo 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs dang / yang 'od zer can gyi sgrub thabs/ slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad/

108b6(dkar chag): mu tshe 'phel ba'i cho ga slob dpon tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rat+na rak+Shi ta dang / zhang grub pa dpal gyi 'gyur/ dpal chen mo sgrol ma'i bstod pa slob dpon chen po tsan+d+ra go mis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba blo gros rgyal po'i

110a4(dkar chag): can ma'i mchod cho ga thub pa shAn+ti la'i bzhed pa d+hArma shrI b+hA dra'i 'gyur/ dpal nor rgyun ma'i sgrub thabs/ dpal nor rgyun ma'i mtsho nA brgya rtsa brgyad/ dpal nor rgyun ma'i smon lam/ dpal nor rgyun ma'i bstod pa rnams/

110a6(dkar chag): ze shaM kus mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal bram ze a ba d+hU tI pa chen po dpe med kyi zhal sngar lo tsA ba ban d+hi pradz+nyA kIrti'i 'gyur rnams bzhugs so// lha so so sna tshogs kyi sgrub thabs/ 'di rnams rgyud sde sna tshogs

112a1(dkar chag): rang 'gyur/ rdo rje theg pa'i rtsa ba'i ltung ba'i las kyi cho ga/ rdo rje gangan pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta a b+ha ya ka rA gup+tA dang / rtsa mi sangs rgyas grags kyi 'gyur/ zhen log sgron ma zhes bya ba
112a2(dkar chag): slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad zer ba 'di the tshom gyi gzhi zhig snang bas mjug tu bkod pa yin/ chos skyong dang nor lha la sogs pa'i sbyor la/ rnam sras kyi sgrub thabs/ rnam sras bde byed rtog pa dang / rnam sras
