112a4(dkar chag): rdo rjes mdzad pa/ rgyal po lus ngan po'i sgrub thabs/ dpa' bo rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta rgyal ba'i snyan dang / lo tsA ba nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ rnam sras kyi sgrub thabs slob dpon shu raM ga warmas
112a5(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta te dzA de ba dang / lo tsA ba zangs dkar 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur/ bai shra ba Na'i rtog pa dang / bde byed kyi cho ga sna tshogs pa'i mdzod gnyis/ paN+Di tra te dza de ba dang / lo tsA be zangs dkar
112a6(dkar chag): 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur/ tshogs bdag dmar tshan gyi sgrub thabs nag po spyod pas mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag gi gsang sgrub a mo g+ha badz+ra sa mdzad pa/ jo bo rje dang nag tsho'i 'gyur/ tshogs bdag chags pa
112b1(dkar chag): rdo rje'i bstod pa dz+nyA bo rjes mdzad pa paN+Di ta de nyid dang nag tsho'i 'gyur/ tshogs bdag sprin gyi sgron ma'i sgrub thabs bram ze rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ jo bo rje dang nag tsho'i 'gyur/ tshogs bdag 'jur bgegs sel ba'i sgrub
112b2(dkar chag): thithebs oMn+d+ra b+hU tis mdzad pa dzaM bo rje dang / rgya brtson seng gi 'gyur/ rmugs 'dzin 'a tshal po'i sgrub thabs/ sgeg pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ dA na shI la rang 'gyur/ dza~M b+hA la'i sgrub thabs slob dpon a b+hA ya k+Sha
112b3(dkar chag): gup+tas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta a laM ka de ba dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims 'byung gnas sbas pa'i 'gyur la/ paN+Di ta pI b+hu d+hi tsan+d+ra dang / chag chos rje dpal gyis bcos pa/ dzaM b+ha l-i la bstod pa btsun pa zla bas mdzad pa/
112b4(dkar chag): paN+Di ta mu ti t+yA shrI dz+nyA na'i zhal snga nas/ pa tshab nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur/ dzaM b+ha l+ya'i sgrub thabs/ rgyal po Ur+ya ma ti sa mdzid pa/ gnyen dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ dza b+ha la'i sgrub thubs/ sbas pa bum+b+ha 'khyil
112b5(dkar chag): zhes bya ba slob dpon nor sbyin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAkya shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ dzaM b+ha la'i sgrub thabs bsdus pa kha che shAkya shrIs mdzad pa de nyid dang / byams pa'i dpal gyi
112b6(dkar chag): 'gyur/ rmugs 'dzin chu'i dbang po la 'phrin las nyi shu'i sgo nas khyad par gyi bstod po/ slob dpon nor 'dzin dpal gyis mdza da pa/ paN+Di ti bud+d+ha shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'phags pa
113a1(dkar chag): rmugs 'dzin la bstod pa paN+Di ta dz+nyA na badz+ras mdzad pa/ 'phags pa dza~M b+ha la'i bstod pa/ mi'i dbang po nyi ma rnam par gnon pas mdzad pA paN+Di ta d+harma d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal
113a2(dkar chag): mtshan gyi 'gyur/ rmugs 'dzin 'chol ba'i man ngag gi bstod bai dA byang chub sems dpas mdzad pa/ nor rgyun ma'i bstod pa/ paN+Di ta dze mA ris mdzad cing / de nyid kyi rang 'gyur/ gnod sbyin gzhan gyis mi thub
113a3(dkar chag): pa'i sgrub thabs kyi rgyud paN+Di ta dza mA ri'i 'gyur/ rdo rje bkod pa'i rgyud las dkyil 'khor bdun pa'i rim pa rnam par phye ba'i sgrub thabs zhes bya ba/ legs ldan nag po'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon snang mdzad myu gus
113a4(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ 'di rnying ma yin pa 'dra'o// sde snod gsum dang rgyud s+t+waM bzhi sogs kyi// spyi yi rnam gzhag sngags kyi theg pa yi// dam tshig la sogs gsal bar ston pa'i glo zhung // bcu phrag gnyis la gcig gis
113a5(dkar chag): brgyan pa bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar cho ga srid zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/ sde snod dang / rgyud sde spyi'i rnam gzhag dang / sngags kyi theg pa'i dam tshig la sogs ston pa'i skor gyi le'u
113a6(dkar chag): ste nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa'o// / gnas chen du bgrod tshul dang / bla ma la gsol ba 'debs pa'i skor lo/ po Ta la kar 'gro ba'i lam yig/ rje btsun spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis
113b1(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta a b+hi yu ka ta de ba shrI dang / lo tsA ba d+harma yon tan gyi 'gyur/ grub thob brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i gsol 'debs bla ma rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa/ man lungs gu ru'i bstod pa/ chos 'byung rab
113b2(dkar chag): gzigs zhes bya ba/ paN+Di ta bi ma la shrIs mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA gau ta ma badz+ra dang / lo tsA ba grags pa byang chub kyi 'gyur/ maN+Dal dang / swats+tsha la sogs nyin zhag phrugs gcig gi chos spyod kyi skor la/ maN+Dal
113b3(dkar chag): gyi cho ga/ slob dpon kaM b+haM la'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa 'gyur rnying / slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga/ dze ta ri dgra las rgyal bas mdzad pa'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga/ paN+Di ta u tu lo pa
113b4(dkar chag): dang / lo tsA chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje gdan par grags pa rin chen 'byung gnas sbas pas mdzad pa'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga/ dar ma grags kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon srid gsum rnam par dag pa'i rdo rjes mdzad
113b5(dkar chag): pa'i las drang po pa'i tshogs sogs bya ba'i rim pa mdor bsdus pa slob dpon a b+ha yA ka ras mdzad pa'i byang chub gzhung lam sh+lo ka sum brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga/ kha che pa Na chen dang chag dgra bcom gyi 'gyur/ kha che
113b6(dkar chag): paN chen gyis mdzad pa'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga/ de nyid dang byams pa'i dpal gyi 'gyur/ gang zag gcig gi nyin gcig gi bya ba de kho na nyid bsdus pa'i man ngag ces bya ba/ slob dpon shI la swa b+ha bas mdzad pa/
114a1(dkar chag): gtor ma'i cho ga sna tshogs kyi skor lnga/ rgyud sna tshogs las btus pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta karma bad+d+ha dang / lo tsA ba gzhon nu tshul khrims
114a2(dkar chag): kyi 'gyur/ chos skyong thams cad kyi gtor ma'i cho ga/ slob dpon pa li A tsar+yas mdzad pa/ rmu ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ rgyal po chen po bzhi'i gtor ma'i cho ga/ jo bo rje dang / dge ba shes ston pa'i 'gyur
114a3(dkar chag): gtor mu chen po'i las kyi rim pa'i 'grol pa/ slob dpon mi bskyod pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta badz+ra kIr+t+ti dang lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyi 'gyur/ gtor ma cha gsum 'bring po shrad+d+ha ka ru war+m+ma sa mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid

114a5(dkar chag): pa'i man ngag ces bya ba slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba rin tshun bzang po'i 'gyur/ yang chab gtor 'jam dpal ma'i 'grel pra/ bI dwA dz+nyA nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta shAn+tiM gAr+b+ha dang / lo tsA bA
114a6(dkar chag): rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bdud rtsi 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i gtor cho ga jo bo rjes mdzad cing bsgyur te/ khu dngos grub kyis gtan la phab pa/ chab gtor dri med jo bo r+N+Ne sa mdzad pa/ de nyid dang tshul khrims rgyal ba'i
114b1(dkar chag): 'gyur/ klu gtor gyi cho ga jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bkra shis dang bde legs su byed pa'i skor la/ dkon mchog gsum gyi bkra shis kyi tshigs bcad slob dpon
114b2(dkar chag): zla 'od kyis mdzad pa/ rigs lnga'i bkra shis kyi tshogs su bcad pa rnal 'byor gyi rgyud kyi lha sum cu rtsa bdun gyi bkra shis kyi tshigasu bcad pa/ 'phags ma sgrol mas gsungs pa'i bkra shis brgyad pa/ paN+Di ta

114b4(dkar chag): skyong nor lho bkra shAs kyi// tshogs bcad la sogs pastan bcos dri ma med// bcu phyag bzhi la bdun gyis brgyan pa bzhugs// bstan bcos 'gyur ro cog gi dkar chag srid zhi'i rgyan gcig ces bya ba las/
114b5(dkar chag): lo sa dang po pa'i bya ba'i rim pa dang / chos skyong dang / nor lha dang / bkra shis la sogs pa'i skor te le'u nyi shu rtsa gsum pa'o// // da ni gsar bcug dbang dang grol byed rim gnyis kyi cha lag nyer mkho sna tshogs kyi
114b6(dkar chag): skor la// bu pa la rje btsun sangs rgyas la rgyun chags kyi tshigasu bcad pas bstod pa 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzod pa/ zha lu lo chen gyi 'gyur/ mi pham mgon po'i bstod pa 'chi bslu ma zhes pa dpal 'jigs med grags pas mdzad pa/
115a1(dkar chag): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad lnga bstod pa slob dpon klu'i blo'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta chen po nags kyis rin chen dang / byams pa gling pa bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sde'i 'gyur/ bAr+Na
115a2(dkar chag): chen nags rin gyi thugs dam rten bla ma'i bris thang rgyu ba yig de nyid kyis mdzad pa rnam gcig tu bsdebs pa byams pa gling pa bsod nams rgya mtsho'i sde'i 'gyur/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud kyi snying po'i
115a3(dkar chag): 'grel pa 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po shrI b+ha dra bo d+hi dang / lo tsA ba gyi rdo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ dbang gi rab tu byed pa zla ba mgon po dang / lo tsA ba shes
115a4(dkar chag): rab grags kyi 'gyur/ 'jam dpal gyi rat+na gi lta ba'i 'dod pa mdor bstan pa yongs su brtan pa mi'i dbang po grags pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta many+dzu shrI dang lo tsA ba shAkya'i dge slong chos grags dpal bzang pos dpalas
115a5(dkar chag): skya'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur ba/ rdo rje'i tshig gi rnam par dbye ba baN+Di ta dron yod rdo rjes mdzad pa/ ti byA gsung sngags sdong po'i drung du rus chung rdo rje grags kyi zhus shing bsgyur ba las slad kyi paN+Di ta d+hA na shi la'i drung
115a6(dkar chag): duHbal po mtsho kha ras bas zhus te spyan drangs pa/ gnyis su med pa'i rnal 'byor zhes bya ba'i dus kyi 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po shrI kA la tsa kra ra ti pas ma dzad pa/ dus 'khor zhabs pa chung ngu dang /

116a1(dkar chag): rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ bde mchog bcu gsum ma'i dbang cho ga slob dpon gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dz+nyA na badz+ra dang lo tsA ba zhang zhung gi 'gyur/ rtsa ltung gi bshags pa slob dpon in+d+ra bo d+his
116a2(dkar chag): mdzad pa/ bde mchog gi bstod pa shrI dza lan+d+ha ra bas mdzad pa/ 'khor lo bde mchog gi rnam 'phrul dang / yul nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i rgya mtshon bstan pa nA ro pas mdzad pa mar bya'i 'gyur/ pra khrid lung bstan tAM lo pas mdzad
116a3(dkar chag): pa/ chos drug gi man ngag nA ra pa dang mar pa 'i chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ gat+to rA mA tshogs mchod kyi rim pa dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi mdzad pa lo tshan rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ bde mchog mkha' 'gro snyan brgyad kyi
116a4(dkar chag): rtsa ba rdo rje'i tshig rkang nA ro pa dang mar ba chos kyi blo gros kyi 'gyur/ chos drug rdo rje'i tshig rkang ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ni gu ma dang / glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ phyag chen rdo rje'i tshig rkang ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma las sman

116a6(dkar chag): kyi mkha' 'gro ma ni gu mas mdzad pa/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i dbang cho ga de nyid kyis mdzad pa/ sman dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ 'chi med rdo rje'i tshig rkang ni gu mas mdzad pa/ lo ni b.rin chen bzang po'i gyur/ rang shar phyag rgya chen po rdo rje'i
116b1(dkar chag): tshig nang ni sums mdzan bldan dpa blo gros kyi 'byam gros byas rgya pon du ma ma sa pa khyer gyi chos gsum ye shes kyi DA ki mas mdzad pa glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur/ sgyu ma lam rim gyi rtsa ba dang de'i 'grel pa ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro mA ni gu mra

117a6(dkar chag): nag po'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+hA ra dang / lo tsA ba 'gos lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i gsang sgrub nA ro pas mdzad pa/ phag mo dbu bcad ma'i sgrub thabs paN+Di ta sha ri pu tras zhal nas gsung ba
117b1(dkar chag): bzhin blo brtan bzhi pas bsgyur ba/ phag dkar shes rab snang ba'i sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po kong kas byin gyi mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta nor bu dpal ye shes dang / lo tsA ba chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ mkha' spyod ma

117b6(dkar chag): kyi rin chen dang / chos 'khor lo tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes kyi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rdo rje rnam par sgeg ma zhes pa paN chen nags kyi rin chen gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / byams pa gling pa bsod/
118a1(dkar chag): nams rgya mtsho ba sdes bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa/ phag mo'i bstod pa rim pa gnyis pa pa Na chen nags rin gyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta de nyid dang / chos 'khor lo tsA ba 'jam dpal ye shes kyi
118a2(dkar chag): 'gyur/ rdo rje phug mo mchod pa'i sgrub thabs ye shes rdo rje'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa jo nang kun snying gi 'gyur/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs rim pa lnga pa zhes pa rngon pa'i gdams ngag/ paN+Di ta bud+d+ha gup+ta dang / lo tsA ba dze

131a1(dkar chag): pak+Shu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag sgrub thabs 'khor lo chen po slob dpon A wa d+hU ti bas mdzad pa paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA na dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ bgegs

131a3(dkar chag): d+ha ra dang lo tsA ba gyi rdo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sgrub thabs nag po spyod pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha ra dang / lo tsA ba 'brog mi shAkya ye shes kyi 'o gyur/ bgags kyi rgyal po'i sgrub thabs nag
131a4(dkar chag): byi pas mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA ga ya d+hA ra dang / mo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i bstod pa slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ bgegs bdag chen po'i sku bri ba'i man ngagayid bzhin
131a5(dkar chag): nor bu slob dpon nag po pas mdzad bA/ baN+Di ta ga ya d+hA rA dang / lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i gtor cho ga nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ paN+Di tA ga ya d+hA ra dang / lo rA d+ya kyi rdo zla ba'i

131b3(dkar chag): nor bu'i sgrub thabs nag po pas mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag sbyin sreg/ tshogs bdag gi bstod pa nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ tshogs bdag gsang sgro ba dzo bos mdzad pa/ tshogs kyi bstod pa a mo g+ha badz+ra gyis

132a1(dkar chag): lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'phags pa dzaM b+ha la'i bstod pa bram ze rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta ma hA dz+nyA nA dang / lo tsA ba mal gyo blo gros grags kyi 'gyur/ nor bdag gtso

161a1(dkar chag): bo d+hi dang / d+hA na shI la dang / ban+de ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ las grub pa'i rab tu byed pa'i 'grel pa blo bzang ngang tshul gyis mdzad pa/ baN+Di ta bi shud+d+ha sing ha dang / lo tsA brtsangs de l+r-in+d+ha rak+Shi tas bsgyur
161a2(dkar chag): ts+tshing ban+de dpal brtsegs kyis gtan laM phab pa/ slob dpon shAn+ti pes mdzad pa'i// dbu ma'i rgyan gyi 'grel bshang dbu ma'i lam grub pa zhes bya ba 'di la byed na sems tsam rgyan zhes grags pa/ lo tsA bi shAkya 'od
161a3(dkar chag): kyi 'gyur/ de ltar rnal 'byor spyod pa sems tsam pa'i lta ba gtan la 'bebs pa'i bstan bcos rnams bstan nas/ sgom pa gtan la 'bebs po'i bstan bcos ni/ slob dpon 'phags pa thogs med kyis mdzad pa'i bas

161a5(dkar chag): dpon chos kyi dbang pos mdzad po/ paN+Di tA dzA rad dA na dang / lo ts+tsha bya rIn chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa'i man ngag/ slob dpon rin chen 'byung gnaso zhi bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta zhi ba
161a6(dkar chag): bzang po dang / le tsA ba 'gos lhas bcas kyi 'gyur/ rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sgom pa'i don mngar bsdus nas bstan pa/ slob ngopon ye shes zla bas mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta pradz+nyA warma dang / lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ shes rab

161b2(dkar chag): paN+Di ta zhi ba bzang po dang / lo tsA ba 'gros lhas btsas kyi 'gyur/ dge ba'i sdong po zhes bya ba'i rab tu byed pa/ slob dpon rat+na kIrtis mdzad pa/ spyod pa dang bslab bya ston pa'i skor la/ byang chub sems dpa'i sdom pa nyi shu pa/

161b4(dkar chag): bzang pos mdzad pa/ paN+Di tak+She la ka ga nA dang / l-i tsA pA mang 'or byang chub shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'di dag rtsom pa po rnams sems tsam gyi lta ba 'dzin pa ma yin yang / bong na 'di dag sems tsam lugs su grags 'dug

162a1(dkar chag): lta ba ston pa'i bstan bcos yin kyang / dus phyis rnyed pas po ti'i gsham du bzhugs pa yin no// chos rnams gzung dang 'dzin pa las grol ba'i// rnam rig tsam du ston pa'i lha sgom spyod//

166b6(dkar chag): kIrtis mdzad pa/ paN+Di ta dza nar dA na dang / lo tsA ba shAn+ya blo gros kyi 'gyur gnyis bzhugs so// / khe ba la slob pa pon rgyal po'i sras seng ge zhabs 'bring pos mdzad pa'i skyes rabs sum cu rtsa lnga pa/

167a2(dkar chag): paN+Di ta kIr+t+ti tsan+d+ra dang / lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur/ rig pa 'dzin pa sprin gyi bzhon pa'i skyes rabs klu kun tu dga' ba'i zlos g+har/ dpal dga' ba'i lhas mdzad pa/ praN+Di ta lAk+ShAM ka ra dwang / lo tsA ba shong ston

167a6(dkar chag): chub sems dpa'i 'dul ba yin pas sngar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i phyogs su bris kyang rung mod kyis/ bka' 'khor lo dang po dang / tha ma'i gseb nas btus pa shas che bar snang zhing / bka' 'khor lo'i rim pa
